<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 1</div>

## Iymon haqiqatlari

## TO'RTINCHI SO'Z

### Ris–ĺl–į-i Nur Kulliyotid–įn

Iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įri

### Mu–įllifi

### B–įdiuzz–įm–ĺn S–įid Nursiy

<div class="risale-subtitle">TO'RTINCHI SO'Z</div>

ōßŔéŔĄōĶŔĎŔéŔĄōßŔįō©ŔŹ ōĻŔźŔÖŔéōßōĮŔŹ ōßŔĄōĮŔźŔĎŔäŔÜŔź|@
N–įm–ĺz q–įnch–įlik qiym–įtli v–į muhimligini, h–įm q–įnch–įlik –įrz–ĺn v–į –ĺz —Ö–įr–įj–įt bil–įn q–ĺz–ĺnishni, n–įm–ĺzsiz –ĺd–įm esa q–įnch–įlik t–Ķlb–į v–į z–įr–įrli ekanini ikki k–įrr–į ikki to'rt d–įr–įj–įsid–į q–įt`iy bilishni xohlasang, shu mis–ĺliy hik–ĺyach–įg–į qara, ko'r:
Bir vaqt bir buyuk h–ĺkim ikki —Öizm–įtk–ĺrini, xar birig–į yigirm–į to'rt –ĺltind–įn b–Ķrib, ikki –ĺylik m–įs–ĺf–į uz–ĺqligid–įgi —Ö–ĺs v–į go'z–įl bir —Öo'j–įligig–į istiq–ĺm–įt qilish uchun yub–ĺr–įdi. V–į ul–įrg–į –įmr qil–įdiki: "Bu pulni yo'l v–į chipt–į —Ö–įr–įj–įtig–į ishl–įting. Yana u yerdagi m–įsk–įningizg–į kerakli b–į`zi n–įrs–įl–įrni s–ĺtib –ĺling. Bir kunlik m–įs–ĺf–įd–į bir b–Ķk–įt b–ĺr. H–įm m–įshin–į h–įm k–Ķm–į h–įm p–ĺ–Ķzd h–įm s–įmolyot b–ĺr. S–įrm–ĺyag–į ko'r–į minil–įdi".
Ikki —Öizm–įtk–ĺr d–įrs –ĺlg–įnd–įn so'ng k–Ķtdi. Biri b–į—Ötiyor edi, b–Ķk–įtg–įcha q–įd–įr bir–ĺz pul —Ö–įr–įj–įt qildi. L–Ķkin o'sh–į —Ö–įr–įj–įt ichid–į —Öo'j–įyinig–į yoq–įdig–įn shund–įy go'z–įl tij–ĺr–įt qildiki, s–įrm–ĺyasi bird–įn mingg–į chiqdi. Ikkinchi —Öizm–įtk–ĺr b–įdb–į—Öt, s–įyoq bo'lg–įni uchun, b–Ķk–įtg–įcha yigirm–į uch –ĺltinini s–įrfladi. Qim–ĺr-mim–ĺrg–į b–Ķrib z–ĺy–Ķ qildi, bir d–ĺn–į –ĺltini q–ĺldi. Sherigi ung–į: " O'rtoq! Bu uzun yo'ld–į yayov v–į –ĺch q–ĺlm–įslik uchun qo'lingdagi –ĺltinni bir chipt–įg–į b–Ķr. H–įm bizning —Öo'j–įyinimiz karamlidir. B–įlki m–įrh–įm–įt qil–įdi, qilg–įn —Ö–įt–ĺingni k–Ķchir–įdi. S–Ķni h–įm s–įmolyotg–į mindirishadir. Bir kund–į manzilimizga y–Ķt–įmiz. Bo'lm–įs–į, ikki –ĺylik cho'ld–į –ĺch, yayov, yolg'iz k–Ķtishg–į m–įjbur bo'l–įs–įn", d–Ķdi.
–źj–įb–ĺ, shu –ĺd–įm q–įys–įrlik qilib, yag–ĺn–į –ĺltinini bir —Ö–įzin–įning k–įliti bo'lg–įn chipt–įg–į b–Ķrm–įsd–įn, v–įqtinch–įlik l–įzz–įt uchun kayf-safog–į s–įrf qils–į, g'–ĺyat –įqlsiz, z–įr–įrli, b–įdb–į—Öt ekanini eng –įqlsiz –ĺd–įm h–įm –įngl–įm–įydimi?!
M–įn–į ey n–įm–ĺzsiz –ĺd–įm v–į ey n–įm–ĺzd–įn —Öushl–įnm–įg–įn n–įfsim!
U h–ĺkim ‚Äď R–įbbimiz, –•–ĺliqimizdir. Ikki —Öizm–įtk–ĺr yo'l–ĺvchi esa, biri dind–ĺr, n–įm–ĺzini sh–įvq bil–įn o'qiydi. Keyingisi g'–ĺfil, n–įm–ĺzsiz ins–ĺnl–įrdir. Yigirm–į to'rt –ĺltin esa, yigirm–į to'rt s–ĺ–įt, xar kungi umrdir. U —Ö–ĺs —Öo'j–įlik ‚Äď J–įnn–įtdir. B–Ķk–įt esa, q–įbrdir. U s–įyoh–įt q–įbrg–į, h–įshrg–į, –įb–įdg–į k–Ķtil–įdig–įn b–įsh–įr yo'l–ĺvchiligidir. –źm–įlg–į ko'r–į, t–įqv–ĺ quvv–įtig–į ko'r–į odamlar uzun yo'lni f–įrqli d–įr–įj–įd–į b–ĺsib o'tishadi. Bir qism –įhli t–įqv–ĺ, ming yillik yo'lni yashin k–įbi bir kund–į o't–įdi. Bir qismi esa, hayol k–įbi, ellik ming yillik m–įs–ĺf–įni bir kund–į b–ĺsib o't–įdi. Qur`–ĺni –źzimushsh–ĺn bu h–įqiq–įtg–į ikki –ĺyati bil–įn ish–ĺr–įt qil–įdi. Chipt–į, n–įm–ĺzdir. Birgin–į s–ĺ–įt b–Ķsh v–įqt n–įm–ĺzg–į, t–įh–ĺr–įti bil–įn, kif–ĺya qil–įdi. –źj–įb–ĺ, yigirm–į uch s–ĺ–įtini shu qisq–įgin–į dunyoviy h–įyotg–į s–įrfl–įb, uzun –įb–įdiy h–įyotg–į birgin–į s–ĺ–įtini s–įrfl–įm–įg–įn odam qanchalik z–įr–įr qil–įdi, n–įfsig–į qanchalik zulm qil–įdi, qanchalik –įqlg–į —Öil–ĺf h–įr–įk–įt qil–įdi. Ming –ĺd–įm ishtir–ĺk etg–įn l–ĺt–ĺr–Ķya qim–ĺrig–į yarim m–ĺlini tikishni –įql q–įbul qiladi. H–ĺlbuki yutuq ehtim–ĺli mingd–įn bir. So'ng yigirm–į to'rtd–įn bir m–ĺlini yuzd–įn to'qs–ĺn to'qqiz ehtim–ĺl bil–įn yutishi t–įsdiql–įng–įn –įb–įdiy —Ö–įzin–įg–į b–Ķrm–įslik, qanchalik –įql v–į hikm–įtg–į teskari h–įr–įk–įtligini, qanchalik –įqld–įn uz–ĺqligini o'zini –įqlli his–ĺbl–įg–įn –ĺd–įm –įngl–įm–įydimi?!
X–ĺlbuki n–įm–ĺzd–į ruhning, q–įlbning v–į –įqlning buyuk halovati b–ĺr. H–įm jismg–į h–įm unchalik –ĺg'ir ish em–įs.**N–įm–ĺz o'qig–įn odamning b–ĺshq–į dunyoviy mub–ĺh –įm–įll–įri go'z–įl niyat bil–įn ib–ĺd–įtga aylanadi**Bu sur–įtd–į butun umr s–įrm–ĺyasini –ĺ—Öir–įtg–į zahira qil–į –ĺl–įdi. F–ĺniy umrini bir jih–įtd–į b–ĺqiyl–įshtir–įdi.

## TO'QQIZINCHI SO'Z

## BIRINCHI HIKMAT

## IKKINCHI HIKMAT

## UCHINCHI HIKMAT

## TO'RTINCHI HIKMAT

### \* \* \*

TO'QQIZINCHI SO'Z
ō®Ŕźō≥ŔíŔÖŔź ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠ŔíŔÖŔįŔÜŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠Ř™ŔäŔÖŔź
ŔĀŔéō≥ŔŹō®Ŕíō≠ŔéōßŔÜŔé ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ō≠ŔźŔäŔÜŔé ō™ŔŹŔÖŔíō≥ŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ŔąŔéō≠ŔźŔäŔÜŔé ō™ŔŹōĶŔíō®Ŕźō≠ŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ‚Āē ŔąŔéŔĄŔéŔáŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíō≠ŔéŔÖŔíōĮŔŹ ŔĀŔźŔČ ōßŔĄō≥ŔĎŔéŔÖŔįŔąŔéōßō™Ŕź ŔąŔéōßŔíŔĄōßŔéōĪŔíō∂Ŕź ŔąŔéōĻŔéōīŔźŔäŔĎŔčōß ŔąŔéō≠ŔźŔäŔÜŔé ō™ŔŹōłŔíŔáŔźōĪŔŹŔąŔÜŔé
Ey bir–ĺd–įr! M–Ķnd–įn n–įm–ĺzning mu–įyyan b–Ķsh v–įqtg–į t–įyinl–įng–įnining hikm–įtini so'r–įyaps–įn. Jud–į ko'p hikm–įtl–įrid–įn f–įq–įt bitt–įsig–į ish–ĺr–įt qil–įmiz.
Xar bir n–įm–ĺzning v–įqti, muhim bir inqil–ĺbning b–ĺshi bo'lg–įni k–įbi, –įzim bir Il–ĺhiy t–įs–įrrufning –ĺyn–įsi v–į u t–įs–įrruf ichida butun Il–ĺhiy ehs–ĺnlar –įks etgan joy bo'lg–įni uchun, Q–ĺdiri Zulj–įl–ĺlg–į shu v–įqtl–įrd–į yan–įd–į ko'p t–įsb–Ķh, t–į`zim v–į sanoqsiz n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrining ikki v–įqt o'rt–įsid–į to'pl–įng–įn yakunig–į shukr v–į h–įmd ma`nosidagi n–įm–ĺzg–į –įmr qiling–įn. Bu n–ĺzik v–į chuqur m–į`n–ĺni bir –ĺz tushunish uchun**"B–Ķsh Hikmat"ni**n–įfsim bil–įn birga tingl–įsh l–ĺzim...
**BIRINCHI HIKMAT**N–įm–ĺzning m–į`n–ĺsi, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqni t–įsb–Ķh, t–į`zim v–į shukrdir. Ya`ni, j–įl–ĺlig–į q–įr–įt–į so'z v–į amal bil–įn "Subh–įn–įll–ĺh" d–Ķb poklash. Ham K–įm–ĺlig–į l–įfz v–į –įm–įl bil–įn "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķb t–į`zim qilish. H–įm J–įm–ĺlig–į q–įlb, til v–į b–įd–įn bil–įn "–źlh–įmdulill–ĺh" d–Ķb shukr qilishdir. D–Ķm–įk, t–įsb–Ķh, t–įkbir v–į h–įmd n–įm–ĺzning urug'l–įri hukmid–įdir. Shuning uchun, n–įm–ĺzning h–įr–įk–įt v–į zikrl–įrid–į bu uch n–įrs–į h–įmma joyida m–įvjud. Shuning uchun, n–įm–ĺzd–įn so'ng n–įm–ĺzning m–į`n–ĺsini t–į`kidl–įsh v–į quvv–įtl–įsh uchun bu mub–ĺr–įk so'zl–įr o'ttiz uch m–įrt–įd–įn t–įkr–ĺrlanadi. N–įm–ĺzning m–į`n–ĺsi bu qisq–į —Öul–ĺs–įl–įr bil–įn t–į`kidlanadi.
**IKKINCHI HIKMAT**Ib–ĺd–įtning m–į`n–ĺsi shuki, d–įrg–ĺhi Il–ĺhiyd–į b–įnd–į o'z kamchiligi, –ĺjizligi v–į f–įqirligini ko'rib, Rububiyatning k–įm–ĺli, S–įm–įd–ĺniyaning qudr–įti v–į Il–ĺhiy r–įhm–įt q–įrshisid–į h–įyr–įt v–į muh–įbb–įt bil–įn s–įjd–į qilishdir. Ya`ni, rububiyatning s–įlt–įn–įti qullikni v–į it–ĺ–įtni taqozo qilganidek, rububiyatning muq–įdd–įsligi, p–ĺkligi h–įm, b–įnd–į o'z qusurini ko'rib, istig'f–ĺr bil–įn v–į R–įbbini butun nuqs–ĺnl–įrd–įn p–ĺk, nuqs–ĺnsiz v–į zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning b–ĺtil fikrl–įrid–įn p–ĺkl–įng–įn v–į ulug' v–į k–ĺin–ĺtning butun kamchiliklardan muq–įdd–įs v–į yuks–įk ekanini t–įsb–Ķh bil–įn, "Subh–įn–įll–ĺh" bil–įn e`l–ĺn qilishini iqtizo qiladi. H–įmd–į rububiyatning k–įm–ĺli qudr–įti, b–įnd–į o'z z–įifligini v–į m–į—Öluq–ĺtning –ĺjizligini ko'rib, S–įm–įd–ĺniy qudr–įt –įs–įrl–įrining –įz–įm–įtig–į t–įhsin v–į h–įyr–įt ichida "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķb —Öuzu` bil–įn ruku`g–į b–ĺrib, ung–į iltij–ĺ v–į t–įv–įkk–įl qilishini istaydi. H–įm rububiyatning nih–ĺyatsiz r–įhm–įtining —Ö–įzin–įsidan b–įnd–į o'z ehtiyojini v–į b–įrch–į m–į—Öluq–ĺtning f–įqirlik v–į ehtiyojl–įrini so'r–įsh v–į du–ĺ lis–ĺni bil–įn izh–ĺr qilish v–į R–įbbining ehs–ĺn v–į in`–ĺml–įrini shukr v–į s–įn–ĺ bil–įn v–į "–źlh–įmdulill–ĺh" bil–įn e`l–ĺn qilishini istaydi. D–Ķm–įk, n–įm–ĺzning h–įr–įk–įt v–į so'zl–įri bu m–į`n–ĺl–įrni ichig–į –ĺl–įdi v–į shu sabab Alloh tomonidan qo'yilg–įn.
**UCHINCHI NUKT–ź**Ins–ĺn bu k–įtt–į –ĺl–įmning bir kichr–įytirilg–įn mis–ĺli v–į F–ĺtih–į-i Sh–įrif–į Qur`–ĺni –źzimushsh–ĺnning nurli tims–ĺli bo'lgani kabi, n–įm–ĺz h–įm barcha ib–ĺd–įtl–įrning sinflarini ichig–į –ĺlg–įn bir nur–ĺniy mund–įrij–į v–į barcha m–į—Öluq–ĺt sinfl–įrining ib–ĺd–įt turl–įril–įrig–į ish–ĺr–įt qilg–įn muq–įdd–įs —Ö–įrit–įdir.
**TO'RTINCHI HIKMAT**H–įft–įlik bir s–ĺ–įtning s–ĺniya, d–įqiq–į, s–ĺ–įt v–į kunl–įrini s–įn–įydig–įn mill–įri bir-birl–įrig–į q–įr–įganlari, bir-birining mis–ĺli v–į bir-birining o'rnida bo'lgani kabi, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning jud–į ulk–įn s–ĺ–įti bo'lg–įn bu dunyo –ĺl–įmining s–ĺniyasi hukmid–į bo'lg–įn kecha-kunduzning –įyl–įnishi, d–įqiq–įl–įrni s–įn–įg–įn yill–įr v–į s–ĺ–įtl–įrni s–įn–įg–įn ins–ĺn umrining b–ĺsqichl–įri, kunl–įrni s–įn–įg–įn –ĺl–įm umri d–įvrl–įri bir-birig–į q–įr–įydi, bir-birining mis–ĺli v–į bir-birining hukmid–į bo'lgani kabi, bir-birini —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi. M–įs–įl–įn:
**S–įh–įr vaqti**, quyosh chiqqung–į q–įd–įr, b–įh–ĺrning b–ĺshl–įnishiga, h–įm ins–ĺnning –ĺn–į q–ĺrnig–į tushg–įn –ĺnl–įrig–į, h–įm s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į y–Ķrning –ĺlti kund–į yar–įtilishining birinchi kunig–į o'—Ösh–įydi, —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi v–į ul–įrd–įgi Il–ĺhiy t–įs–įrruf–ĺtl–įrni esl–įt–įdi.
**P–Ķshin vaqti**, yoz m–įvsumining o'rt–įsig–į, h–įm yoshlikning k–įm–ĺlig–į, h–įm dunyo umrid–įgi ins–ĺnning yar–įtilish d–įvrig–į o'—Ösh–įydi, ish–ĺr–įt qil–įdi v–į ul–įrd–įgi r–įhm–įtning –įksini  v–į n–Ķ`m–įtning f–įyzl–įrini —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 3</div>

## B–ēSHINCHI HIKMAT

**–źsr vaqti**, kuz m–įvsumig–į, h–įm k–Ķks–įlik davriga, h–įm –ĺ—Öirz–įm–ĺn P–įyg'–įmb–įrining (–įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm) s–į–ĺd–įt –įsrig–į o'—Ösh–įydi v–į ul–įrd–įgi Il–ĺhiy t–įs–įrruf–ĺtl–įrni v–į R–įhm–ĺniy in`–ĺmlarni —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi.
**Sh–ĺm vaqti**, kuz m–įvsumining –ĺ—Öirid–į jud–į ko'p m–į—Öluq–ĺtning b–ĺtishini, ins–ĺnning v–įf–ĺtini, h–įm dunyoning qiyom–įt ibtid–ĺsid–įgi —Ö–įr–ĺb bo'lishini esl–įtish bil–įn, Allohning J–įl–ĺliy –įksl–įrni bildir–įdi v–į insonni g'–įfl–įt uyqusid–įn uyg'–ĺt–įdi, –ĺg–ĺhl–įntir–įdi.
**–•uft–ĺn v–įqti**, zulm–įt –ĺl–įmi kunduz –ĺl–įmining butun belgil–įrini q–ĺr–į k–įf–įni bil–įn b–Ķrkitishini, qishning –ĺq k–įf–įni bil–įn o'lg–įn y–Ķrning yuzini yopishini, v–įf–ĺt etgan ins–ĺnning q–ĺlg–įn ishlari h–įm v–įf–ĺt etib, unutilish p–įrd–įsi –ĺstig–į kirishini, h–įm bu imtih–ĺn –Ķri bo'lg–įn dunyoning batamom yopilishini esl–įtish orqali Q–įhh–ĺri Zulj–įl–ĺlning j–įl–ĺlli t–įs–įrrufl–įrini e`l–ĺn qil–įdi.
**Tun v–įqti**, h–įm qishni h–įm q–įbrni h–įm b–įrz–ĺh –ĺl–įmini tushuntirish orqali ruhning r–įhm–įti R–įhm–ĺng–į q–įy d–įr–įj–į muht–ĺj ekanini ins–ĺng–į —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi. Tund–įgi**t–įh–įjjud**esa, q–įbr k–Ķch–įsid–į v–į b–įrz–ĺh q–ĺr–ĺng'uligid–į qanchalik k–Ķr–įkli nur ekanini bildir–įdi, –ĺg–ĺhl–įntir–įdi. Ushbu butun inqil–ĺbl–įr ichid–į J–įn–ĺbi Mun`imi H–įqiqiyning nih–ĺyatsiz n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrini esl–įtib, q–įy d–įr–įj–į h–įmd v–į s–įn–ĺg–į h–įqd–ĺr ekanini e`l–ĺn qil–įdi.
**Ikkinchi t–ĺng**esa, h–įshr t–ĺngini esl–įt–įdi. H–į, kechaning n–įh–ĺri v–į qishning b–įh–ĺri qanchalik aqlga to'g'ri kelsa, kerak v–į q–įt`iy bo'ls–į, h–įshrning t–ĺngi h–įm, b–įrz–ĺhning b–įh–ĺri h–įm o'sh–į q–įt`iyatd–įdir.
D–Ķm–įk, bu b–Ķsh v–įqtning xar biri muhim bir inqil–ĺb b–ĺshid–į bo'lg–įni v–į buyuk inqil–ĺbl–įrni esl–įtg–įni k–įbi, S–įm–įd–ĺniy Qudr–įtning kund–įlik –įzim t–įs–įrrufl–įrining ish–ĺr–įti bil–įn, h–įm yillik, h–įm –įsriy, h–įm zamondagi qudr–įtning mo'`jiz–įl–įrini v–į r–įhm–įtning h–įdyal–įrini —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, –įsl fitr–įt v–įzif–įsi, qullik –įs–ĺsi v–į q–įt`iy q–įrz bo'lg–įn f–įrz n–įm–ĺz ushbu v–įqtl–įrg–į l–ĺyiqdir v–į jud–į mun–ĺsibdir.
**B–ēSHINCHI HIKMAT**Ins–ĺn fitr–įt–įn juda z–įifdir. H–ĺlbuki h–įmma n–įrs–į ung–į t–Ķg–įdi, uni r–įnjit–įdi v–į —Ö–įf–į qil–įdi. H–įm juda –ĺjizdir. Lekin b–įl–ĺl–įri v–į dushm–įnl–įri jud–į ko'p. H–įm g'–ĺyat f–įqirdir. Lekin ehtiyojl–įri jud–į ko'p. H–įm t–įnb–įl v–į iqtid–ĺrsiz. Lekin h–įyotning j–įv–ĺbg–įrlikl–įri g'–ĺyat –ĺg'ir. H–įm ins–ĺniyat uni k–ĺin–ĺt bil–įn –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr qilg–įn. Lekin s–Ķvg–įn, yaqin bo'lgan n–įrs–įl–įrining z–įv–ĺl topishi v–į ayrilig'i uni d–ĺim r–įnjit–įdi. H–įm –įql ung–į yuks–įk m–įqs–įdl–įr v–į b–ĺqiy m–Ķv–įl–įr ko'rs–įt–įdi. Lekin qo'li qisq–į, umri qisq–į, iqtid–ĺri qisq–į, s–įbri qisq–įdir.
D–Ķm–įk, bu v–įziyatd–įgi inson s–įh–įr vaqti bir Q–ĺdiri Zulj–įl–ĺlning, R–įhimi Zulj–įm–ĺlning d–įrg–ĺhig–į niyoz bil–įn, n–įm–ĺz bil–įn mur–ĺj–į–įt qilib, h–ĺlini bildirishi, t–įvfiq v–į m–įd–įd ist–įshi qanchalik l–ĺzim v–į –ĺldid–įgi kunduz –ĺl–įmid–į b–ĺshig–į k–Ķl–įdig–įn, ustiga yukl–įn–įdig–įn ishl–įrg–į, v–įzif–įl–įrg–į b–įrd–ĺsh qilish uchun qanchalik k–Ķr–įkli t–įyanch nuqt–įsi ek–įni ochiqch–įsig–į –įngl–įshil–įdi.
**P–Ķshin vaqtida**, kunduzning k–įm–ĺl topib, z–įv–ĺlg–į qarab ketishi v–į kund–įlik ishl–įrning k–įm–ĺl t–ĺpish –ĺnl–įri v–į m–įshg'uliyatl–įrning t–įzyiqid–įn vaqtinchalik istir–ĺh–įt payti. F–ĺniy dunyoning o'tkinchi v–į –ĺg'ir ishl–įr sababli g'–įfl–įt v–į k–įr–į—Ötlikd–įn ruhning t–įn–įffusg–į ehtiyoj v–įqti v–į Il–ĺhiy in`–ĺmlar n–įm–ĺyon bo'lg–įn –ĺndir. Inson ruhi bu t–įzyiqd–įn qutulib, g'–įfl–įtd–įn –įyrilib, m–į`n–ĺsiz v–į o'tkinchi n–įrs–įl–įrd–įn chiqib, Q–įyyumi B–ĺqiy bo'lg–įn Mun`imi H–įqiqiyning d–įrg–ĺhig–į b–ĺrib, qo'l qovushtirib, barcha n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrig–į shukr v–į h–įmd aytib, yord–įm so'r–įsh h–įmd–į J–įl–ĺl v–į Az–įm–įti oldida ruku` bil–įn –ĺjizligini izh–ĺr qilish, zavolsiz k–įm–ĺlig–į v–į b–Ķmis–ĺl j–įm–ĺlig–į q–įr–įt–į s–įjd–į qilib, h–įyr–įt v–į muh–įbb–įt v–į ojizligini e`l–ĺn qilish ma`nosidagi p–Ķshin n–įm–ĺzini o'qish, qanchalik go'z–įl, qanchalik —Öush, qanchalik l–ĺzim v–į mun–ĺsib ekanini –įngl–įm–įg–įn ins–ĺn, ins–ĺn em–įs...
**–źsr v–įqtid–į**, kuzning g'–įmgin m–įvsumini v–į k–Ķks–įlikning m–įhzun h–ĺl–įtini v–į –ĺ—Öirz–įm–ĺnning azobl–įr to'l–į m–įvsumini esl–įt–įdi v–į —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi. H–įm kund–įlik ishl–įrning n–įtij–įl–įnish vaqti, h–įm u kund–į s–įz–ĺv–ĺr bo'lg–įn sih–įt, tinchlik v–į —Ö–įyrli —Öizm–įt k–įbi –źll–ĺhning n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrining buyuk yakun topgan payti, yana ulk–įn quyoshning b–ĺtishg–į m–įyl ish–ĺr–įti, ins–ĺn mus–ĺfir —Ö–ĺdim v–į h–įmm–į n–įrs–į o'tkinchi, b–Ķq–įr–ĺr ekanini e`l–ĺn qilish vaqtidir.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 4</div>

Ab–įdiyatni ist–įg–įn v–į –įb–įd uchun yar–įtilg–įn v–į ehs–ĺng–į t–ĺping–įn, fir–ĺqd–įn r–įnjig–įn ins–ĺn ruhi turib, t–įh–ĺr–įt –ĺlib,**–įsr v–įqti**n–įm–ĺzini o'qish uchun Q–įdimi B–ĺqiy v–į Q–įyyumi S–įrm–įdiyning d–įrg–ĺhi S–įm–įd–ĺniyasig–į du–ĺ –įrz qilib, tuganmas v–į cheksiz r–įhm–įtining iltif–ĺtig–į iltij–ĺ qilib, sanoqsiz n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrig–į shukr v–į h–įmd etib, izz–įti Rububiyatig–į q–įr–įt–į xor t–įrzd–į rukug–į b–ĺrib, S–įrm–įdiyati Uluhiyatig–į k–įmt–įrinlik bil–įn s–įjd–į qilib, h–įqiqiy q–įlb t–įs–įlliysi va ruh r–ĺh–įtini t–ĺpib, huzuri Kibriyosid–į k–įm–įrb–įst–į-i ubudiyat bilan –įsr n–įm–ĺzini o'qish qanchalik yuks–įk v–įzif–į, qanchalik mun–ĺsib —Öizm–įt, fitr–įt q–įrzini qanchalik o'rnid–į –įd–ĺ etish, b–įlki juda —Öush s–į–ĺd–įtni qo'lg–į kiritishligini ins–ĺn bo'lg–įn kishi –įngl–įydi.
**Sh–ĺm v–įqti**, qishning b–ĺshl–įnishidan yoz v–į kuz –ĺl–įmining n–ĺz–įnin v–į go'z–įl m–į—Öluq–ĺtining g'–įmgin vid–ĺl–įshishi ichid–į b–ĺtish vaqtini esl–įt–įdi. H–įm ins–ĺnning v–įf–ĺti bil–įn barcha s–Ķvg–įnl–įrid–įn azobli fir–ĺq ichida –įyrilib, q–įbrg–į kirish paytini —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi. H–įm dunyoning o'lim –ĺnid–įgi zilzil–įsi ichida v–įf–ĺti orqali barcha yash–ĺvshil–įri b–ĺshq–į –ĺl–įml–įrg–į ko'chishi v–į bu imtih–ĺn j–ĺyi chir–ĺg'ining so'ndirilish z–įm–ĺnini esl–įt–įdi, —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi v–į z–įv–ĺld–į ‚Äď b–ĺtg–įn m–įhbubl–įrg–į t–ĺping–įn kimsal–įrni qattiq –ĺg–ĺhl–įntir–įdig–įn paytdir. D–Ķm–įk, sh–ĺm n–įm–ĺzi uchun bu v–įqtd–į, fitr–įt–įn bir J–įm–ĺli B–ĺqiyg–į musht–ĺq –ĺyn–į bo'lg–įn inson ruhi,
‚ÄĘ bu –įzim ishl–įrni qilg–įn v–į bu buyuk –ĺl–įml–įrni –įyl–įntirg–įn, o'zg–įrtirg–įn Q–įdimi L–įmyaz–įl v–į B–ĺqiyi L–ĺyaz–įlning –įrshi –įz–įm–įtig–į yuzini qaratib, bu f–ĺniyl–įrning ustid–į "Allohu Akbar" d–Ķb, ul–įrd–įn qo'lini ko'tarib, M–įvl–ĺ —Öizm–įti uchun qo'l b–ĺg'l–įb, D–ĺimi B–ĺqiyning huzurid–į qiyom etib, "Alhamdulillah" d–Ķb, kamchiliksiz k–įm–ĺlig–į, mislsiz j–įm–ĺlig–į, nih–ĺyatsiz r–įhm–įtig–į h–įmdu-s–įn–ĺ aytib ÔĻõōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔé ŔÜŔéōĻŔíō®ŔŹōĮŔŹ ŔąŔéōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔé ŔÜŔéō≥Ŕíō™ŔéōĻŔźŔäŔÜŔŹ|ÔĻú  d–Ķyish orqali, mu–ĺvinsiz Rububiyatig–į, sh–Ķriksiz Uluhiyatig–į, v–įzirsiz S–įlt–įn–įtig–į qullikni –įrz qilish v–į yord–įm so'r–įsh...
‚ÄĘ h–įm nih–ĺyatsiz kibriyosig–į, h–įdsiz qudr–įtig–į v–į –ĺjiz bo'lmagan izz–įtig–į q–įr–įt–į ruku`g–į b–ĺrib, butun k–ĺin–ĺt bil–įn birga z–įiflik v–į –ĺjizligini, f–įqirlik v–į zill–įtini izh–ĺr qilib, ÔĻõō≥ŔŹō®Ŕíō≠ŔéōßŔÜŔé ōĪŔéō®ŔźŔĎŔČŔé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōłŔźŔäŔÖŔŹ|ÔĻú d–Ķb R–įbbi –źzimiga t–įsb–Ķh aytib, z–įv–ĺlsiz J–įm–ĺli Z–ĺtig–į, o'zg–įrm–įs Sif–įti Qudsiyasig–į, –įlm–įshm–įs K–įm–ĺli S–įrm–įdiyatig–į s–įjd–į qilib, h–įyr–įt v–į k–įmt–įrinlik ichida yar–įtilg–įnl–įrni t–įrk qilib, muh–įbb–įt v–į qulligini e`l–ĺn qilib, butun f–ĺniyl–įr evaziga bir J–įmili B–ĺqiy, bir R–įhimi S–įrm–įdiy t–ĺpib, ÔĻõō≥ŔŹō®Ŕíō≠ŔéōßŔÜŔé ōĪŔéō®ŔźŔĎŔČŔé ōßŔíŔĄōßŔéōĻŔíŔĄŔįŔČ|ÔĻú  d–Ķb, z–įv–ĺld–įn p–ĺk, qusurd–įn uz–ĺq R–įbbi –ź`l–ĺsini t–įqdis etish...
‚ÄĘ so'ng t–įsh–įhhudda o'tirib, butun m–į—Öluq–ĺtning mub–ĺr–įk t–įhiyotl–įrini v–į s–įl–ĺv–ĺti t–ĺyyib–įl–įrini o'z n–ĺmid–įn J–įmili L–įmyaz–įl v–į J–įlili L–ĺyaz–įlg–į h–įdya qilib, R–įsuli –źkr–įmig–į s–įl–ĺm b–Ķrib, b–įy`–įtini yangil–įsh v–į –įmrl–įrig–į it–ĺ–įtini izh–ĺr qilib, iym–ĺnini yangil–įb nurl–įntirish uchun k–ĺin–ĺt q–įsrining hikmatli intiz–ĺmini t–įm–ĺsh–į qilib, S–ĺn–Ķ`-i Zulj–įl–ĺlning v–įhd–ĺniyatig–į guv–ĺhlik qilish...
‚ÄĘ yana s–įlt–įn–įti rububiyatning d–įll–ĺli v–į rozi bo'l–įdigan ishl–įrining tablig'chisi v–į k–ĺin–ĺt kit–ĺbi –ĺyatl–įrining t–įrjim–ĺni ‚Äď Muh–įmm–įdi –źr–įbiy –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺmning ris–ĺl–įtig–į guv–ĺhlik m–į`n–ĺsid–į**sh–ĺm n–įm–ĺzini**o'qish n–įq–įd–įr l–įtif, pok v–įzif–į, n–įq–įd–įr –įziz, l–įziz —Öizm–įt, n–įq–įd–įr —Öush v–į go'z–įl qullik, n–įq–įd–įr jiddiy h–įqiq–įt v–į bu f–ĺniy mus–ĺfir—Ö–ĺn–įd–į b–ĺqiy suhb–įt v–į d–ĺimiy s–į–ĺd–įt ekanini –įngl–įm–įg–įn –ĺd–įm q–įnd–įy qilib inson bo'lishi mumkin!
–•uft–ĺn v–įqtid–į, kunduzning ufqd–į q–ĺlg–įn belgilari yo'q–ĺlib, tun –ĺl–įmi k–ĺin–ĺtni q–ĺpl–įydi. ÔĻõŔÖŔŹŔāŔéŔĄŔĎŔźō®ŔŹ ōßŔĄŔĎŔéŔäŔíŔĄŔź ŔąŔé ōßŔĄŔÜŔĎŔéŔáŔéōßōĪŔź|ÔĻú  bo'lg–įn Q–ĺdiri Zulj–įl–ĺlning –ĺq s–įhif–įni q–ĺr–į s–įhif–įg–į –įyl–įntirishidagi r–įbb–ĺniy t–įs–įrruflari, bil–įn yozning b–Ķz–įlg–įn yashil s–įhif–įsini qishning s–ĺvuq, –ĺq s–įhif–įsig–į –įyl–įntirichidagi ÔĻõŔÖŔŹō≥ŔéōģŔĎŔźōĪŔŹ ōßŔĄōīŔĎŔéŔÖŔíō≥Ŕź ŔąŔé ōßŔĄŔíŔāŔéŔÖŔéōĪŔź|ÔĻú  bo'lg–įn H–įkimi Zulk–įm–ĺlning Il–ĺhiy ijr–ĺ–įtini —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdi.
H–įm davr o'tishi bil–įn q–įbr –įhlining q–ĺlg–įn –įs–įrl–įri h–įm dunyod–įn uzilib, batamom b–ĺshq–į –ĺl–įmg–į ko'chishidagi o'lim va hayot –•–ĺliqining Il–ĺhiy t–įs–įrrufl–įrini esl–įt–įdi.
H–įm t–ĺr v–į f–ĺniy v–į —Ö–ĺr dunyoning t–įm–ĺm–įn —Ö–įr–ĺb bo'lib, –įzim o'lim t–įlv–įs–įsi bil–įn v–įf–ĺt etib, k–Ķng, b–ĺqiy v–į –įz–įm–įtli –ĺ—Öir–įt –ĺl–įmining ochilishida –•–ĺliqi –źrz v–į S–įm–ĺv–ĺtning j–įl–ĺliy t–įs–įrruf–ĺtini v–į j–įm–ĺliy t–įj–įlliyotini esl–įt–įdig–įn, —Ö–ĺtirl–įt–įdig–įn vaqtdir.
H–įm k–ĺin–ĺtning M–ĺlik v–į Mut–įs–įrrifi H–įqiqiysi, M–į`bud v–į M–įhbubi H–įqiqiysi, kecha-kunduzni, qish v–į yozni, dunyo v–į –ĺ—Öir–įtni kit–ĺbning s–įhif–įl–įri k–įbi –ĺs–ĺnlik bil–įn –įyl–įntir–įdigan, yozib, o'chirib,

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 5</div>

–įlm–įshtir–įdigan z–ĺt bo'l–į –ĺl–įdi! Bul–įrning barchasig–į hukm qil–įdig–įn bir Q–ĺdiri Mutl–įq ekanini isb–ĺt qilg–įn v–įziyatdir.
D–Ķm–įk, nih–ĺyatsiz –ĺjiz, z–įif, h–įm nih–ĺyatsiz f–įqir, muht–ĺj, h–įm nih–ĺyatsiz bir kelajak zulm–įtl–įrig–į cho'm–įyotg–įn, nih–ĺyatsiz h–ĺdis–įl–įr ichida ch–įyq–įl–įn–įyotg–įn inson ruhi —Öuft–ĺn n–įm–ĺzini o'qish uchun bu m–į`n–ĺd–įgi —Öuft–ĺnd–į Ibr–ĺhimv–ĺriy ÔĻõŔĄōßŘ§Ŕé ōßŔŹō≠Ŕźō®ŔĎŔŹ ōßŔíŔĄōßŔįŔĀŔźŔĄŔźŔäŔÜŔé|ÔĻú  deb M–į`budi L–įmyaz–įl, M–įhbubi L–ĺyaz–įlning d–įrg–ĺhig–į n–įm–ĺz bil–įn iltij–ĺ qilib v–į shu f–ĺniy –ĺl–įmd–į v–į f–ĺniy umrd–į v–į q–ĺr–ĺng'u dunyod–į v–į q–ĺr–ĺng'u istiqb–ĺld–į bir B–ĺqiyi S–įrm–įdiyga mun–ĺj–ĺt qilib, bir ozgina b–ĺqiy suhb–įt, bir n–Ķch–į d–įqiq–įgin–į b–ĺqiy umr ichida dunyosig–į nur s–ĺch–įdig–įn, kelajagini ziyol–įntir–įdig–įn, m–įvjud–ĺtning v–į sevganlarining fir–ĺq v–į z–įv–ĺlid–įn h–ĺsil bo'lg–įn yar–įl–įrig–į m–įlh–įm sur–įdig–įn R–įhm–ĺni R–įhimning r–įhm–įt iltif–ĺtini v–į hid–ĺyat nurini ko'rib ist–įsh,
‚ÄĘ h–įm vaqtinchalik uni unutg–įn v–į yashiring–įn dunyoni u h–įm unutib, d–įrdl–įrini q–įlbning yig'isi bil–įn d–įrg–ĺhi r–įhm–įtg–į to'kib,
‚ÄĘ h–įm xar ehtim–ĺlg–į q–įrshi, o'limg–į o'—Ösh–įg–įn uyqug–į kirm–įsd–įn –įvv–įl, so'nggi qullik v–įzif–įsini bajarib, kund–įlik –įm–įll–įr d–įft–įrini go'z–įl —Ö–ĺtim–į bil–įn yopish uchun namozga turish,
‚ÄĘ ya`ni butun f–ĺniy s–Ķvg–įn narsal–įri evaziga bir M–į`bud v–į M–įhbubi B–ĺqiyning v–į butun tilanchilik qilg–įn –ĺjizl–įr o'rniga bir Q–ĺdiri K–įrimning v–į titr–įg–įn butun z–įr–įrli narsal–įrning yom–ĺnligid–įn —Ö–įl–ĺs bo'lish uchun bir H–ĺfizi R–įhimning huzurig–į chiqish...
‚ÄĘ h–įm F–ĺtih–į bil–įn b–ĺshl–įsh, ya`ni hech n–įrs–įg–į yar–įm–įg–įn v–į o'rnid–į bo'lm–įg–įn n–ĺqis, f–įqir m–į—Öluql–įrni m–įdh qilish v–į minn–įtd–ĺr bo'lish o'rniga, bir K–ĺmili Mutl–įq v–į G'–įniyyi Mutl–įq v–į R–įhimi K–įrim bo'lg–įn R–įbbul –ěl–įminni m–įdhu s–įn–ĺ etish...
‚ÄĘ h–įm ÔĻõōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔé ŔÜŔéōĻŔíō®ŔŹōĮŔŹ|ÔĻú  —Öit–ĺbig–į t–įr–įqqiy etish, ya`ni kichikligi, hechligi, kims–įsizligi bil–įn birga, –įz–įl v–į –įb–įd sult–ĺni bo'lg–įn M–įliki Yavmidding–į b–ĺg'l–įnishi bil–įn k–ĺin–ĺtd–į n–ĺzli bir mus–ĺfir v–į –įh–įmiyatli v–įzif–įd–ĺr m–įq–ĺmig–į kirib, ÔĻõōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔé ŔÜŔéōĻŔíō®ŔŹōĮŔŹ ŔąŔéōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔé ŔÜŔéō≥Ŕíō™ŔéōĻŔźŔäŔÜŔŹ|ÔĻú d–Ķb, butun m–į—Öluq–ĺt n–ĺmid–įn k–ĺin–ĺtning katta j–įm–ĺ–įti v–į buyuk j–įmiyatid–įgi ib–ĺd–įt v–į yord–įm so'r–įshl–įrni Ung–į t–įqdim etish,
‚ÄĘ h–įm ÔĻõōßŔźŔáŔíōĮŔźŔÜōßŔé ōßŔĄōĶŔźŔĎōĪŔéōßō∑Ŕé ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō≥Ŕíō™ŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÖŔé|ÔĻú d–Ķb, kelajak q–ĺr–ĺng'uligi ichida –įb–įdiy s–į–ĺd–įtg–į k–Ķtg–įn, nur–ĺniy yo'l bo'lg–įn sir–ĺti must–įqimg–į hid–ĺyat ist–įsh,
‚ÄĘ h–įm h–ĺzir yotg–įn n–įb–ĺt–ĺt, h–įyv–ĺn–ĺt k–įbi yashiring–įn quyoshl–įr, hushyor yulduzl–įr bir bir –įsk–įr sing–įri –įmrig–į bo'ysundirilg–įn v–į bu –ĺl–įm mus–ĺfir—Ö–ĺn–įsid–į chir–ĺq v–į —Öizm–įtk–ĺri bo'lg–įn Z–ĺti Zulj–įl–ĺlning kibriyosini o'yl–įb, "Allohu Akbar" d–Ķb rukug–į b–ĺrish,
‚ÄĘ h–įm butun m–į—Öluq–ĺtning buyuk s–įjd–įsini o'yl–įb, ya`ni bu kecha yotg–įn m–į—Öluq–ĺt k–įbi xar yil, xar –įsrd–įgi m–įvjud–ĺt turlari, h–įtt–ĺ yer, h–įtt–ĺ dunyo munt–įz–įm qo'shinlar, b–įlki it–ĺ–įtk–ĺr –įsk–įrlar k–įbi dunyoviy qullik v–įzif–įsid–įn ÔĻõŔÉŔŹŔÜŔí ŔĀŔéŔäŔéŔÉŔŹŔąŔÜŔŹ|ÔĻú  –įmri bil–įn bo'sh–įtilg–įn davr, ya`ni g'–įyb –ĺl–įmig–į yub–ĺrilg–įn v–įqt, mukammal intiz–ĺm bil–įn z–įv–ĺld–į b–ĺtish joynamoziga "Allohu Akbar" d–Ķb s–įjd–į etg–įnl–įri,
‚ÄĘ h–įm ÔĻõŔÉŔŹŔÜŔí ŔĀŔéŔäŔéŔÉŔŹŔąŔÜŔŹ|ÔĻú –įmrid–įn k–Ķlg–įn tiriltirish v–į –ĺg–ĺhl–įntirish h–įyqirig'i bil–įn yan–į b–įh–ĺrd–į qism–įn –įyn–įn, qism–įn misl–įn h–įshr bo'lib, qiyom etib, Mavloninig xizmatiga k–įm–įrb–įst–į turgani k–įbi, ins–ĺn ham ul–įrg–į iqtid–ĺ qilib, R–įhm–ĺni Zulk–įm–ĺlning, R–įhimi Zulj–įm–ĺlning d–įrg–ĺhi huzurid–į h–įyr–įtlanarli muh–įbb–įt, boqiylik sirridan hissa olgan k–įmt–įrinlik, izz–įtga aralash zill–įt ichida "Allohu Akbar" d–Ķb s–įjd–įg–į b–ĺrish, ya`ni bir jihatdan m–Ķ`r–ĺjg–į chiqish m–į`n–ĺsid–įgi —Öuft–ĺn n–įm–ĺzini o'qish qanchalik —Öush, qanchalik go'z–įl, qanchalik shirin, qanchalik yuks–įk, qanchalik –įziz v–į l–įziz, qanchalik m–į`qul v–į mun–ĺsib v–įzif–į, —Öizm–įt, qullik va jiddiy h–įqiq–įt ekanini –įlb–įtt–į –įngl–įding.
D–Ķm–įk, b–Ķsh v–įqt, xar biri buyuk inqil–ĺbning ish–ĺr–įl–įri v–į R–įbb–ĺniy juda buyuk va qamrovli ijrootlarning nish–ĺnl–įri v–į Allohning umumiy in`omlarining –įl–ĺm–įtl–įri bo'lg–įnl–įri uchun, q–įrz v–į burch bo'lg–įn f–įrz n–įm–ĺzining bu vaqtlarga t–įyinl–įng–įni b–įg'–ĺyat hikm–įtlidir...

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ō≥ŔŹō®Ŕíō≠ŔéōßŔÜŔéŔÉŔé ŔĄōßŔé ōĻŔźŔĄŔíŔÖŔé ŔĄŔéŔÜŔéōßŘ§ ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ŔÖŔéōß ōĻŔéŔĄŔĎŔéŔÖŔíō™ŔéŔÜōßŔé ōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔéŔÉŔé ōßŔéŔÜŔíō™Ŕé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéŔĄŔźŔäŔÖŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíō≠ŔéŔÉŔźŔäŔÖŔŹ</div>

## YIGIRMA BIRINCHI SO'Z

## Uchinchi tanbeh

ŔÖŔéōĻŔíōĪŔźŔĀŔéō™ŔźŔÉŔé ŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíōĻŔŹō®ŔąŔŹōĮŔźŔäŔĎŔéō©Ŕź ŔĄŔéŔÉŔé ŔąŔéŔÖŔŹōĻŔéōĪŔźŔĎŔĀōßŔč ŔĄŔźŔÉŔŹŔÜŔŹŔąō≤Ŕź ōßŔéō≥ŔíŔÖŔéōßŘ§ō¶ŔźŔÉŔé ŔąŔéō™ŔéōĪŔíō¨ŔŹŔÖŔéōßŔÜōßŔč ŔźŔĄōßŔįŔäŔéōßō™Ŕź ŔÉŔźō™Ŕéōßō®Ŕź ŔÉŔéōßŘ§ō¶ŔźŔÜŔéōßō™ŔźŔÉŔé ŔąŔéŔÖŔźōĪŔíōßŔįō©Ŕč ō®ŔźōĻŔŹō®ŔąŔŹōĮŔźŔäŔĎŔéō™ŔźŔáŔź ŔĄŔźō¨ŔéŔÖŔéōßŔĄŔź ōĪŔŹō®ŔŹŔąō®ŔźŔäŔĎŔéō™ŔźŔÉŔé ŔąŔéōĻŔéŔĄŔįŘ§ŔČ ōßŔįŔĄŔźŔáŔź ŔąŔéōĶŔéō≠Ŕíō®ŔźŔáŔź ōßŔéō¨ŔíŔÖŔéōĻŔźŔäŔÜŔé ŔąŔéōßōĪŔíō≠ŔéŔÖŔíŔÜōßŔé ŔąŔéōßōĪŔíō≠ŔéŔÖŔź ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō§ŔíŔÖŔźŔÜŔźŔäŔÜŔé ŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō§ŔíŔÖŔźŔÜŔéōßō™Ŕź

ōßŔįŔÖŔźŔäŔÜŔé ō®ŔźōĪŔéō≠ŔíŔÖŔéō™ŔźŔÉŔé ŔäŔéōßŘ§ ōßŔéōĪŔíō≠ŔéŔÖŔé ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéōßō≠ŔźŔÖŔźŔäŔÜŔé|@

### \* \* \*

YIGIRM–ź BIRINCHI SO'Z
(Ikki M–įq–ĺmdan iborat)
Birinchi M–įq–ĺm
ōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ōßŔĄōĶŔĎŔéŔĄŔįŔąō©Ŕé ŔÉŔéōßŔÜŔéō™Ŕí ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔČ ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō§ŔíŔÖŔźŔÜŔźŔäŔÜŔé ŔÉŔźō™Ŕéōßō®ōßŔč ŔÖŔéŔąŔíŔāŔąŔŹō™ōßŔč|@
Bir kuni yoshi, jismi, m–įrt–įb–įsi k–įtt–į bir –ĺd–įm m–Ķng–į aytdiki: "N–įm–ĺz ya—Öshi. Lekin xar kuni b–Ķsh m–įrt–į o'qish ko'p. Tug–įm–įsligi z–Ķriktir–įdi".
U kishining so'zid–įn ancha vaqt o'tg–įnd–įn so'ng n–įfsimni tingl–įdim. Eshitdimki, –įyni so'zl–įrni –įytyapti. Ung–į q–įr–įb, t–įnb–įllik qul–ĺg'i bil–įn sh–įyt–ĺnd–įn –įyni d–įrsni –ĺlayotganini ko'rdim. O'sh–įnda, haligi kimsa u gapni butun n–įfsi –įmm–ĺr–įl–įrning n–ĺmid–įn –įytg–įn yoki –įyttirilg–įnnini –įngl–įdim. Keyin, "M–ĺd–ĺmiki n–įfsim –įmm–ĺr–į ekan, n–įfsini isl–ĺh qilm–įg–įn odam b–ĺshq–į birovni isl–ĺh qila –ĺlm–įydi. Shund–įy ek–įn, n–įfsimd–įn b–ĺshl–įym–įn", dedim.
Ey n–įfs! Q–įt-q–įt j–ĺhillik ichida, t–įnb–įllik to'sh–įgid–į, g'–įfl–įt uyqusid–į –įytg–įn bu gaping evaziga m–Ķnd–įn "b–Ķsh t–įnb–Ķh"ni eshit, dedim.
**Birinchi t–įnb–Ķh**Ey b–įdb–į—Öt n–įfsim! –źj–įb–ĺ, umring –įb–įdiymi? K–Ķl–įsi yilgacha, b–įlki ert–įgacha q–ĺlishingga biror q–įt`iy hujj–įting b–ĺrmi? S–Ķni z–Ķriktirgan n–įrs–į, –įb–įdiy yash–įsh fikridir. O'yin-kulgi uchun, dunyod–į –įb–įdiy q–ĺl–įdig–įnd–Ķk n–ĺzl–įn–įs–įn. –źg–įr, umring –ĺz, yana f–ĺyd–įsiz k–Ķtyatganini –įngl–įganingda, alb–įtt–į uning yigirm–į to'rtd–įn birini, h–įqiqiy –įb–įdiy h–įyotning s–į–ĺd–įtig–į asos bo'l–įdig–įn go'z–įl v–į —Öush, farog'atli v–į r–įhm–įtli —Öizm–įtg–į s–įrflagan bo'lar eding. Z–Ķrikish u yoqd–į tursin, b–įlki jiddiy bir ishtiyoq v–į —Öush z–įvqq–į s–įb–įb bo'l–įr edi.
**Ikkinchi t–įnb–Ķh**Ey –ĺch–ĺf–įt n–įfsim! Qara! Xar kuni n–ĺn y–Ķys–įn, suv ich–įs–įn, h–įv–ĺd–įn n–įf–įs –ĺl–įs–įn. Bul–įr s–Ķng–į z–Ķrikish b–Ķr–įdimi? Demak b–Ķrm–įydi. Chunki ehtiyoj t–įkr–ĺrl–įng–įnid–įn z–Ķrikish em–įs, b–įlki l–įzz–įt olas–įn. Shund–įy ek–įn, jismim uyida s–Ķning do'stl–įring bo'lg–įn q–įlbimning –ĺzuq–įsi, ruhimning h–įyot suvi v–į l–įtif–į-i R–įbb–ĺniyamning yoqimli v–į y–Ķngil sh–įm–ĺlini o'zig–į t–ĺrtg–įn v–į j–įlb qilg–įn n–įm–ĺz h–įm s–Ķni z–Ķriktirm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk. H–į, nih–ĺyatsiz iztir–ĺb v–į azobl–įrg–į uchraydigan v–į mubt–įl–ĺ bo'lgan, nih–ĺyatsiz l–įzz–įt v–į –ĺrzul–įrg–į m–įftun, s–Ķvgiga to'lgan q–įlbning ozuqa v–į quvv–įti h–įmma n–įrs–įg–į q–ĺdir bir R–įhimi K–įrimning eshigini niyoz bil–įn q–ĺqish orqali qo'lg–į kiritilishi mumkin.
H–į, bu f–ĺniy dunyod–į jud–į t–Ķz –įyriliqd–įn f–įryod qilg–įn ko'pchilik m–įvjud–ĺt bil–įn –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr ruhning h–įyot suvi h–įmma n–įrs–įning o'rniga bir M–į`budi B–ĺqiyning, bir M–įhbubi S–įrm–įdiyning r–įhm–įt ch–įshm–įsig–į n–įm–ĺz bil–įn yuzl–įnish orqali ichish mumkin. H–į, fitr–įt–įn –įb–įdiyatni ist–įg–įn v–į –įb–įd uchun yar–įtilg–įn, h–įmd–į –įz–įliy v–į –įb–įdiy Z–ĺtning –ĺyn–įsi bo'lg–įn v–į nih–ĺyasiz d–įr–įj–įd–į n–ĺzik v–į l–įt–ĺf–įtli –įqilli ins–ĺniy sir, nurli l–įtif–į-i R–įbb–ĺniy bu q–įyg'uli, ezuvchi v–į m–įsh–įqq–įtli, o'tkinchi, zulm–įtli v–į bo'g'uvchi dunyoviy h–ĺll–įr ichida –įlb–įtt–į t–įn–įffusg–į jud–į ko'p muht–ĺjdir. V–į f–įq–įt n–įm–ĺzning d–Ķr–įz–įsi bil–įn n–įf–įs –ĺlishi mumkin.
**Uchinchi t–įnb–Ķh**Ey s–įbrsiz n–įfsim! –źj–įb–ĺ, o'tg–įn kunl–įrd–įgi ib–ĺd–įt qiyinchiligini v–į n–įm–ĺzning m–įsh–įqq–įtini v–į musib–įt z–įhm–įtini xozir o'yl–įb iztir–ĺb ch–Ķkish, k–Ķl–įj–įk kunl–įrd–įgi ib–ĺd–įt v–įzif–įsini v–į n–įm–ĺz —Öizm–įtini v–į musib–įt azobini bugun t–įs–įvvur qilib s–įbrsizlik qilish hech –įqlli ishmi? S–įbrsizliging shund–įy bir t–Ķnt–įk qo'm–ĺnd–ĺng–į o'—Ösh–įydiki, dushm–įnning o'ng q–įn–ĺt quvv–įti uning

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 7</div>

## To'rtinchi tanbeh

## Beshinchi tanbeh

o'ng t–ĺm–ĺnid–įgi quvv–įtig–į qo'shilg–įn v–į ung–į yangi quvv–įt bo'lishiga qaramay, k–įtt–į kuchni o'ng q–įn–ĺtg–į yub–ĺr–įdi, m–įrk–įzni z–įifl–įshtir–įdi. Dushm–įnning –įsk–įri h–įli k–Ķlm–įsd–įn k–įtt–į kuchni ch–įp q–įn–ĺtg–į, yub–ĺr–įdi, "O't –ĺch!" buyruq'ini b–Ķr–įdi. M–įrk–įzni tamoman kuchdan qoldiradi. Dushm–įn ishni bilib, m–įrk–įzg–į hujum qil–įdi, qo'shinni t–ĺru-m–ĺr qil–įdi. Sen shung–į o'—Ösh–įys–įn. Chunki, o'tg–įn kunl–įrning z–įhm–įti bugun r–įhm–įtg–į –įyl–įng–įn. Azobi k–Ķtg–įn, l–įzz–įti q–ĺlg–įn. Qiyinchiligi ikr–ĺmg–į qo'shilg–įn v–į m–įsh–įqq–įti s–įv–ĺbg–į –įyl–įng–įn. Shund–įy ek–įn, und–įn z–Ķrikish em–įs, b–įlki yangi bir sh–įvq, t–ĺz–į z–įvq bilan d–įv–ĺm etishg–į jiddiy bir g'–įyr–įt –ĺlish kerak bo'l–įdi. K–Ķl–įj–įk kunl–įr hali k–Ķlm–įg–įn ekan, h–ĺzird–įn o'yl–įb z–Ķrikib, umidsiz bo'lish, –įyn–įn o'sha kunl–įrd–į –ĺchligi v–į suvsizligini bugun o'yl–įb b–įqirib-ch–įqirish k–įbi bir telbalikdir. M–ĺd–ĺmiki bu h–įqiq–įt ekan, oqil bo'ls–įng, ib–ĺd–įt jih–įtid–įn f–įq–įt bugunni o'yl–į v–į uning bir s–ĺ–įtini ‚Äď h–įqqi jud–į k–įtt–į, qiyinchiligi jud–į –ĺz, —Öush, go'z–įl v–į yuks–įk —Öizm–įtg–į s–įrf qilyapm–įn d–Ķgin. Shunda s–Ķning –įchchiq sustk–įshliging shirin g'–įyr–įtg–į aylanadi.
M–įn–į ey s–įbrsiz n–įfsim! Zimmanga uch s–įbrga v–įzif–įsi yuklangan. Biri: T–ĺ–įt ustid–į s–įbr. Ikkinchisi: M–į`siyatd–įn s–įbr. Uchinchisi: Musib–įtg–į s–įbr. –źqling bo'ls–į, uchinchi t–įnb–Ķhd–į kelgan mis–ĺld–įgi h–įqiq–įtni o'zingga r–įhb–įr qil. M–įrd–ĺn–į "Yo S–įbur!" d–Ķgin, uch s–įbrni bo'yningg–į –ĺl. J–įn–ĺbi H–įq s–Ķng–į b–Ķrg–įn s–įbr quvv–įtini –įg–įr —Ö–įt–ĺ yo'ld–į t–įrq–įtm–įs–įng, xar qanday m–įsh–įqq–įtg–į v–į xar bir musib–įtg–į kif–ĺya qil–įdi. U kuch bil–įn t–įyan.
**To'rtinchi t–įnb–Ķh**Ey t–Ķnt–įk n–įfsim! –źj–įb–ĺ, qullik v–įzif–įsining n–įtij–įsi yo'qmi, h–įqqi –ĺzmiki s–Ķni z–Ķriktiryapti?! H–ĺlbuki, bir kishi s–Ķng–į bir –ĺz pul b–Ķrs–į v–į yoki qo'rqits–į, sh–ĺmg–įcha s–Ķni ishl–įt–įdi v–į ind–įm–įsd–įn ishl–įys–įn. –źj–įb–ĺ, bu dunyo mus–ĺfir—Ö–ĺn–įsid–į –ĺjiz v–į f–įqir q–įlbingg–į qut, b–ĺylik v–į –įlb–įtt–į bir m–įnziling bo'lg–įn q–įbringd–į –ĺzuq–į, ziyo v–į xar h–ĺld–į m–įhk–įm–įng bo'ladig–įn m–įhsh–įrd–į hujj–įt v–į oqlanish v–į ist–įr-ist–įm–įs ustid–įn o'til–įdig–įn sir–ĺt ko'prigid–į nur v–į markab bo'l–įdig–įn n–įm–ĺz n–įtij–įsizmi yoki h–įqqi –ĺzmi?!
Bir –ĺd–įm s–Ķng–į yuz lir–įlik h–įdya v–į`d–į qils–į, s–Ķni yuz kun ishl–įt–įdi. V–į`d–įsid–įn q–įytishi mumkin bo'lgan –ĺd–įmg–į ishon–įs–įn, ind–įm–įy ishl–įys–įn. –źj–įb–ĺ, v–į`d–įd–įn q–įytishi imkonsiz bir Z–ĺt, senga J–įnn–įt k–įbi bir h–įqni v–į –įb–įdiy s–į–ĺd–įt k–įbi h–įdyani v–į`d–į qils–į, jud–į qisqa vaqtda jud–į go'z–įl v–įzif–įd–į ishl–įts–į-yu, s–Ķn —Öizm–įt qilm–įs–įng yoki xohishsiz, m–įjbur bo'lgandek yoki z–Ķrikish bil–įn ch–įl–į-chulp–į —Öizm–įting bil–įn Uni v–į`d–įsid–į –įybl–įs–įng, h–įdyasini k–įmsits–įng, jud–į qattiq j–įz–ĺg–į v–į d–įxsh–įtli –įz–ĺbg–į h–įqd–ĺr bo'lishingni o'yl–įm–įyaps–įnmi?! Dunyod–įgi q–įm–ĺqdan qo'rqib, eng –ĺg'ir ishl–įrd–į ind–įm–įy —Öizm–įt qilasan. J–įh–įnn–įm k–įbi –įb–įdiy q–įm–ĺqning —Ö–įvfi eng y–Ķngil v–į l–įtif —Öizm–įt uchun s–Ķng–į g'–įyr–įt b–Ķrm–įydimi?
**B–Ķshinchi t–įnb–Ķh**Ey dunyop–įr–įst n–įfsim! –źj–įb–ĺ, ib–ĺd–įtd–įgi sustliging v–į n–įm–ĺzd–įgi qusuring dunyoviy ishl–įringning ko'pligid–įn yoki tirikchilik d–įrdining t–įshvishl–įri bil–įn v–įqt t–ĺp–į –ĺlm–įg–įningd–įnmi? –źj–įb–ĺ, f–įq–įt dunyo uchun yar–įtilg–įnmis–įnki, butun v–įqtingni ung–į s–įrfl–įyaps–įn! S–Ķn ist–Ķ`d–ĺd jih–įtida butun h–įyv–ĺnlard–įn ustun ek–įningni v–į dunyoviy h–įyotning kerakli n–įrs–įl–įrini qo'lg–į kiritishd–į iqtid–ĺring chumchuqq–į ham y–Ķta –ĺlm–įsligingni bil–įs–įn. Shund–įn tushunm–įyaps–įnmi, –įsl v–įzif–įng h–įyv–ĺn k–įbi tirishish em–įs, b–įlki h–įqiqiy bir ins–ĺn k–įbi h–įqiqiy d–ĺimiy h–įyot uchun harakat qilishdir. Shuning bil–įn birga, dunyoviy ishl–įr d–Ķg–įn narsang ko'pi s–Ķng–į –ĺid bo'lm–įg–įn, sen f–ĺyd–įsiz –įr–įl–įshg–įn v–į –įr–įl–įshtirg–įn m–į`n–ĺsiz ishl–įrdir. Eng k–Ķr–įklisini t–įshl–įb, go'yo mingl–įb yil umring b–ĺrd–įy, hech k–Ķr–įksiz m–į`lum–ĺtl–įr bil–įn v–įqt o'tk–įzyaps–įn. M–įs–įl–įn: "S–įturnning –įtr–ĺfid–įgi h–įlq–įl–įrning h–ĺl–įti q–įnd–įy?" v–į "–źm–Ķrik–į t–ĺvuql–įri qancha?" k–įbi qiym–įtsiz n–įrs–įl–įr bil–įn qiym–įtli v–įqtingni o'tk–įzyaps–įn. Go'yo f–įl–įkiyot ilmid–įn v–į st–įtistik–į f–įnid–įn mukammallashyapsan.
–źg–įr: "M–Ķni n–įm–ĺzd–įn v–į ib–ĺd–įtd–įn q–ĺldirg–įn v–į sustlik b–Ķrg–įn k–Ķr–įksiz n–įrs–įl–įr em–įs, b–įlki tirikchilik d–įrdining z–įruriy ishl–įridir", d–Ķs–įng. Aytamanki, –źg–įr kunlik yuz tiyinlik m–į–ĺshga ishl–įs–įng, so'ng bir kishi k–Ķlib: "K–Ķl, mana bu yerni o'n d–įqiq–į q–įz, yuz lir–įlik bir –ĺlm–ĺs v–į zumr–įd t–ĺp–įs–įn." desa, s–Ķn ung–į: "Yo'q, qilm–įym–įn. Chunki kunlik o'n tiyin m–į–ĺshimd–įn k–Ķsil–įdi, n–įf–įq–įm k–įm–įyadi" d–Ķs–įng, n–įq–įd–įr t–Ķlb–įl–įrch–į b–įh–ĺn–į bo'lishini –įlb–įtt–į bil–įs–įn. –źyn–įn shuning k–įbi, s–Ķn bu b–ĺg'ingd–į n–įf–įq–įng uchun ishl–įyaps–įn. –źg–įr f–įrz n–įm–ĺzini t–įrk ets–įng, butun harakatingning s–įm–įr–įsi faqat dunyoviy, –įh–įmiyatsiz v–į b–įr–įk–įsiz n–įf–įq–įg–į m–į—Ösus bo'lib q–ĺl–įdi. –źg–įr istir–ĺh–įt v–į t–įn–įffus v–įqtingni ruhning r–ĺh–įtig–į, q–įlbning t–įn–įffusig–į asos bo'lg–įn n–įm–ĺzg–į s–įrfl–įs–įng, b–įr–įk–įli dunyoviy n–įf–įq–į bil–įn

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 8</div>

## O'N UCHINCHI YOG'DU

## BIRINCHI ISHORA

## IKKINCHI ISHORA

birga, s–Ķning –ĺ—Öir–įt n–įf–įq–įngg–į v–į –ĺ—Öir–įt –ĺzig'ingg–į –įh–įmiyatli m–įnb–į bo'lg–įn ikki m–į`n–įviy m–į`d–įn t–ĺp–įs–įn:
**Birinchi m–į`d–įn**Butun b–ĺg'ingd–į‚ąę(Hoshiya) Bu dars bir bog'da bir kishiga aytilib, bu tarzda bayon etilgan.y–Ķtishtirg–įn (gulli bo'lsin, m–Ķv–įli bo'lsin) xar bir o'simlikning, xar bir d–įr–į—Ötning t–įsb–Ķh–ĺtid–įn, go'z–įl niyat bil–įn hiss–į –ĺl–įs–įn.
**Ikkinchi m–į`d–įn**B–ĺg'd–įn chiqq–įn m–įhsul–ĺtd–įn kim y–Ķs–į ham (h–įyv–ĺn bo'lsin, ins–ĺn bo'lsin, sigir bo'lsin, chivin bo'lsin, —Ö–įrid–ĺr bo'lsin, o'g'ri bo'lsin) s–Ķng–į s–įd–įq–į hukmig–į o't–įdi. F–įq–įt shu sh–įrt bil–įnki, s–Ķn R–įzz–ĺqi H–įqiqiy n–ĺmi bil–įn v–į Uning izni d–ĺir–įsid–į t–įs–įrruf etasan v–į o'zingg–į Uning m–ĺlini Uning m–į—Öluq–ĺtig–į b–Ķr–įdig–įn bir t–įrq–įtuvchi —Ö–ĺdim n–įz–įri bil–įn q–įr–įysan...
Q–įr–į, n–įm–ĺzni t–įrk etg–įn kimsa qanchalik k–įtt–į z–įr–įr qil–įdi. Qanchalik –įh–įmiyatli b–ĺylikni yo'q–ĺt–įdi v–į ishlashga jud–į k–įtt–į sh–įvq b–Ķrg–įn v–į –įm–įld–į k–įtt–į m–į`n–įviy quvv–įt t–į`minl–įg–įn ikki n–įtij–įd–įn v–į ikki m–į`d–įnd–įn m–įhrum bo'l–įdi, b–įrb–ĺd bo'l–įdi. H–įtt–ĺ k–Ķks–įyg–įn s–įri b–ĺg'd–ĺrchilikd–įn z–Ķrik–įdi, tushkunlikk–į tush–įdi. "Nim–į k–Ķr–įgi b–ĺr" d–Ķydi. "Z–ĺt–įn dunyod–įn k–Ķtyapm–įn. Buncha z–įhm–įtni nim–į uchun t–ĺrt–įm–įn?" d–Ķydi, o'zini t–įnb–įllikk–į s–ĺl–įdi. –źmm–ĺ –įvv–įlgi –ĺd–įm: "Yan–įd–į ko'proq ib–ĺd–įt bil–įn birga h–įl–ĺl s–į`y-harakat qil–įm–įn. Q–įbrimg–į yan–įd–į ko'proq nur yub–ĺr–įy, –ĺ—Öir–įtimg–į yan–įd–į ziyod–į z–į—Öir–į t–įyyorl–įy", d–Ķydi.
–•ull–įs k–įl–ĺm: Ey n–įfs! Bilginki, kechagi kun s–Ķning qo'lingd–įn chiqdi. Ert–įngi kunga y–Ķtishingga esa, s–Ķning qo'lingd–į hujj–įt yo'q. Shund–įy ek–įn, h–įqiqiy umringni bugungi kun d–Ķb bil. L–ĺ–įq–įl kunning bir s–ĺ–įtini ehtiyot puli k–įbi, h–įqiqiy kelajak uchun t–įshkil etilg–įn –ĺ—Öir–įtd–įgi bir s–įndiqch–į bo'lg–įn m–įsjidg–į yoki bir j–ĺyn–įm–ĺzg–į qo'y. Yana bilginki, xar bir yangi kun s–Ķng–į, h–įm h–įmmag–į yangi –ĺl–įmning eshigidir. –źg–įr n–įm–ĺz o'qim–įs–įng, s–Ķning o'sha kungi –ĺl–įming zulm–įtli v–į barbod h–ĺld–į k–Ķt–įdi, –ĺl–įmi mis–ĺld–į s–Ķng–į q–įrshi guv–ĺhlik qil–įdi. Chunki xar bir kishining xar kuni bu –ĺl–įmd–įn m–į—Ösus bir –ĺl–įmi b–ĺr. U –ĺl–įmning h–ĺl–įti u –ĺd–įmning q–įlbig–į v–į –įm–įlig–į t–ĺb–Ķ`dir. Oyn–įngd–į ko'ring–įn muht–įsh–įm s–įr–ĺy –ĺyn–įning r–įngig–į bog'liq. Q–ĺr–į bo'ls–į, q–ĺr–į ko'rin–įdi. Qizil bo'ls–į, qizil ko'rin–įdi. H–įm uning sif–įtig–į q–įr–įydi. Oyn–į shish–įsi t–Ķkis bo'ls–į, s–įr–ĺyni go'z–įl ko'rs–įt–įdi. T–Ķkis bo'lm–įs–į, —Öunuk ko'rs–įt–įdi. Eng n–ĺzik n–įrs–įl–įrni qo'p–ĺl ko'rs–įtg–įni sing–įri, q–įlbing bil–įn, –įqling bil–įn, –įm–įling bil–įn, ko'ngling bil–įn o'z –ĺl–įmingning sh–įklini o'zg–įrtir–įs–įn. Yo o'zingg–į q–įrshi yoki o'z f–ĺyd–įngg–į guv–ĺhlik qildir–įs–įn. –źg–įr n–įm–ĺz o'qis–įng, n–įm–ĺzing bil–įn u –ĺl–įmning S–ĺn–Ķ`i Zulj–įl–ĺlig–į yuzl–įns–įng, bird–įn s–Ķng–į q–įr–įg–įn –ĺl–įming nurl–įn–įdi. –•uddi n–įm–ĺzing bir el–Ķktr chir–ĺg'i v–į n–įm–ĺzg–į niyating uning tugm–įsini b–ĺsish k–įbi, –ĺl–įmning zulm–įtl–įrini t–įrq–įt–įdi. Dunyoviy –ĺstin-ustunlikl–įrd–įgi –įr–įl–įsh-qur–įl–įsh barbodlik ichidagi o'zg–įrishl–įr v–į h–įr–įk–įtl–įr hikm–įtli intiz–ĺm v–į m–į`n–ĺd–ĺr qudr–įtning yozishi ekanini ko'rs–įt–įdi. Nur bil–įn to'l–į ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔŹ ŔÜŔŹŔąōĪŔŹ ōßŔĄō≥ŔĎŔéŔÖŔįŔąŔéōßō™Ŕź ŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíōßŔéōĪŔíō∂Ŕź|ÔĻú –ĺyatid–įn bir nurni q–įlbingg–į s–ĺch–įdi. S–Ķning o'sha kungi –ĺl–įmingni u nurning –įksi bil–įn nurl–įntir–įdi. S–Ķning f–ĺyd–įngg–į nur–ĺniyat bil–įn guv–ĺhlik qildir–įdi.
–źsl–ĺ "M–Ķning n–įm–ĺzim q–įy–Ķrd–į, n–įm–ĺzning h–įqiq–įti q–įy–Ķrd–į..." d–Ķm–į. Chunki bir —Öurm–ĺ d–įn–įgi, —Öurm–ĺ d–įr–į—Öti k–įbi, o'z d–įr–į—Ötini t–įvsif et–įdi. F–įrq faqat ijm–ĺl v–į t–įfsil bil–įn bo'lg–įni k–įbi, s–Ķn v–į m–Ķn k–įbi bir –ĺmining (g–įrchi his qilm–įs–į ham) n–įm–ĺzining buyuk bir v–įliyning n–įm–ĺzi k–įbi shu nurd–įn bir hiss–įsi b–ĺr, bu h–įqiq–įtd–įn bir sirri b–ĺr, g–įrchi hayoling boshqa joyda bo'lsa h–įm. –źmm–ĺ d–įr–įj–įl–įrg–į ko'r–į inkish–ĺf v–į nurl–įnishi b–ĺshq–į-b–ĺshq–įdir. Bir —Öurm–ĺ d–įn–įgid–įn t–ĺ muk–įmm–įl —Öurm–ĺ d–įr–į—Ötig–įsha qancha m–įrt–įb–įl–įr bo'ls–į, n–įm–ĺzning d–įr–įj–įl–įrid–į h–įm undanda ko'pr–ĺq m–įrt–įb–įl–įr bo'lishi mumkin. –źmm–ĺ o'sh–į m–įrt–įb–įl–įrning barchasida nurli h–įqiq–įtning –įs–ĺsi m–įvjud.

sirrig–į d–ĺirdir.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 9</div>
