<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ŔąŔéŔāŔŹŔĄŔí ōĪŔéō®ŔĎŔź ōßŔéōĻŔŹŔąōįŔŹ ō®ŔźŔÉŔé ŔÖŔźŔÜŔí ŔáŔéŔÖŔéō≤Ŕéōßō™Ŕź ōßŔĄōīŔĎŔéŔäŔéōßō∑Ř™ŔäŔÜŔź Řě ŔąŔéōßŔéōĻŔŹŔąōįŔŹ ō®ŔźŔÉŔé ōĪŔéō®ŔĎŔź ōßŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéō≠Ŕíō∂ŔŹōĪŔŹŔąŔÜŔź</div>

### (Sh–įyt–ĺnning yom–ĺnligid–įn –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įsh sirrig–į d–ĺir. "O'n uch ish–ĺr–į" yozil–įdi. O'sh–į ish–ĺr–įl–įrning bir qismi, t–įrq–ĺq sur–įtd–į "Yigirm–į Oltinchi So'z" k–įbi bir qism ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į b–įyon v–į isb–ĺt qiling–įni uchun, bu y–Ķrd–į f–įq–įt qisq–įch–į b–įhs yuritiladi)

**BIRINCHI ISH–ěR–ź\*\***S–įv–ĺl**Sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning k–ĺin–ĺtd–į ij–ĺd jih–įtid–įn hech bir t–į`siri yo'qligi, J–įn–ĺbi H–įq r–įhm–įt v–į in–ĺyati bil–įn –įhli h–įqq–į t–įr–įfd–ĺr ek–įnini, h–įq v–į h–įqiq–įtning j–ĺzib–įd–ĺr go'z–įllikl–įri v–į husnl–įri –įhli h–įqq–į yord–įmchi v–į ilh–ĺml–įntiruvchi ek–įni, z–įl–ĺl–įtning jirk–įnch yom–ĺnlikl–įri zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarni n–įfr–įt ettirs–įd–į, sh–įyt–ĺnning guruhining ko'p m–įrt–į g'–įl–įb–į qilishining hikm–įti nim–į? Ahli h–įq xar d–ĺim sh–įyt–ĺnning yom–ĺnligid–įn J–įn–ĺbi H–įqd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įshining sirri nim–į?
**J–įv–ĺb**Hikm–įti v–į sirri shuki: Barchaning fikrich–į z–įl–ĺl–įt v–į yom–ĺnlik m–įnfiy, v–įyr–ĺn qilish v–į yo'qlikk–į –ĺid v–į buzishd–įn ib–ĺr–įt. Barchaning hid–ĺyat v–į ya—Öshilik musb–įt ekani, m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺid v–į bunyod qilish v–į t–į`mirl–įshd–įn ib–ĺr–įtligiga hamfikr. H–įmm–įg–į m–į`lumki: Yigirm–įt–į –ĺd–įm yigirm–į kund–į qurg–įn bin–ĺni, bitt–į –ĺd–įm bir kund–į buz–į –ĺl–įdi. D–įrh–įqiq–įt, barcha –įs–ĺsiy –į`z–ĺl–įrning v–į h–įyot sh–įrtl–įrining m–įvjudligi bil–įn vujudi d–įv–ĺm etg–įn ins–ĺn h–įyoti –•–ĺliqi Zulj–įl–ĺlning qudr–įtig–į m–į—Ösus ek–įn, bir z–ĺlim bitt–į –į`z–ĺni k–Ķssa, insonni h–įyotg–į nisb–įt–įn yo'qlikk–į –ĺid bo'lg–įn o'limg–į olib boradi. Shuning uchun "Buzg'unchilik –ĺs–ĺn" so'zi m–įq–ĺlg–į –įyl–įng–įn.
Shu sird–įn, zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlar h–įqiq–įt–įn z–įif kuch bil–įn jud–į kuchli –įhli h–įqq–į b–į`z–įn g'–ĺlib bo'l–įdi. L–Ķkin –įhli h–įqning shund–įy must–įhk–įm bir q–įl`–įsi b–ĺrki, und–į him–ĺyal–įng–įn v–įqti, mudxish dushm–įnl–įr yaqinl–įsha –ĺlm–įydi, yom–ĺnlik qila –ĺlm–įydi. –źg–įr vaqtinchalik z–įr–įr b–Ķrs–į ham, ÔĻõŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔāŔźō®Ŕéō©ŔŹ ŔĄŔźŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō™ŔĎŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÜŔé|ÔĻú sirri bil–įn –įb–įdiy s–įv–ĺb v–į m–įnf–į–įt bil–įn o'sh–į z–įr–įr q–ĺpl–įn–įdi. Aytilgan metin q–įl`–į, hisni h–įsin ‚Äď sh–įri–įti Muh–įmm–įdiya (–źSM) v–į sunn–įti –źhm–įdiyadir (–źSM).
**IKKINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**S–įv–ĺl: T–įm–ĺman yom–ĺnlikd–įn ib–ĺr–įt bo'lg–įn sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning yar–įtilishi v–į –įhli iym–ĺng–į hujum qilishi v–į ul–įr tuf–įyli ko'p ins–ĺnl–įr kufrg–į botib J–įh–įnn–įmg–į kirishi, juda mudxish v–į —Öunuk —Ö–ĺdis–įdir. –źj–įb–ĺ, J–įmiyli –źl–įl Itl–ĺq, R–įhiymi Mutl–įq v–į R–įhm–ĺni bil-H–įqning r–įhm–įt v–į j–įm–ĺli bu cheksiz —Öunuklik v–į daxshatli musib–įtning h–ĺsil bo'lishig–į q–įnd–įy yo'l qo'yadi v–į q–įnd–įy ru—Ös–įt b–Ķr–įdi?
Bu m–įs–įl–įni ko'pl–įr so'r–įg–įn v–į ko'pchilikning h–įyolig–į k–Ķl–įdi.
**J–įv–ĺb**Sh–įyt–ĺnning m–įvjudligid–į –įh–įmiyatsiz yom–ĺnlikl–įr bil–įn birg–į bir qancha umumiy —Ö–įyrli m–įqs–įdl–įr v–į ins–ĺnning k–įm–ĺl–ĺti b–ĺr. H–į, bir d–įn–įkd–įn ulk–įn d–įr–į—Öt bo'lguncha qancha m–įrt–įb–įl–įr bo'ls–į, ins–ĺn m–ĺhiyatid–įgi ist–Ķ`d–ĺdd–į und–įnd–į ko'pr–ĺq m–įrt–įb–įl–įr m–įvjud. B–įlki z–įrr–įd–įn quyoshgacha d–įr–įj–įl–įri b–ĺr. Bu ist–Ķ`d–ĺdl–įrning riv–ĺjl–įnishi, –įlb–įtt–į bir h–įr–įk–įt ist–įydi, bir mu–ĺm–įl–į bo'lishini t–įq–ĺz–ĺ qil–įdi. O'sh–į mu–ĺm–įl–įd–įgi t–įr–įqqiy ch–įr—Öining h–įr–įk–įti kur–įsh orqali yuzaga keladi. U kur–įsh, sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning v–į z–įr–įrli n–įrs–įl–įrning m–įvjudligi orqali bo'l–įdi. Bo'lm–įs–į, m–įl–įkl–įr k–įbi ins–ĺnl–įrning h–įm m–įq–ĺmi o'zg–įrm–įs q–ĺl–įr edi. Und–į ins–ĺn n–įvid–į mingl–įb turlar hukmid–į sinfl–įr bo'lm–įs edi. Bir –įh–įmiyatsiz yom–ĺnlik k–Ķlm–įsligi uchun mingt–į —Ö–įyrni t–įrk etish hikm–įt v–į –įd–ĺl–įtg–į ziddir. Garchi, sh–įyt–ĺn tuf–įyli –įks–įr ins–ĺnl–įr z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į botsa ham,**–įh–įmiyat v–į qiym–įt –įs–ĺs–įn sif–įtg–į q–įr–įydi, miqd–ĺrning –įh–įmiyati jud–į k–įm yoki umum–įn yo'q\*\*M–įs–įl–įn, bir ming o'nt–į d–įn–įgi bo'lg–įn kishi, d–įn–įkl–įrni tupr–ĺq –ĺstig–į ko'ms–į, und–įn o'nt–įsi d–įr–į—Öt bo'lib ko'k–įrs–į v–į mingt–įsi chiris–į, o'nt–į d–įr–į—Öt bo'lg–įn d–įn–įkl–įrning u –ĺd–įmg–į b–Ķrg–įn m–įnf–į–įti, –įlb–įtt–į mingt–į chirig–įn d–įn–įk b–Ķrg–įn z–įr–įrni yo'qq–į chiqar–įdi. –•uddi shuning k–įbi, n–įfs v–į sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrg–į q–įrshi kur–įsh orqali, yulduzl–įr k–įbi ins–ĺniyatni sh–įr–įfl–įntirg–įn v–į nurl–įntirg–įn o'nt–į k–ĺmil ins–ĺni tuf–įyli b–įsh–įriyatg–į b–Ķrg–įn m–įnf–į–įt, sh–įr–įf v–į qiym–įt, –įlb–įtt–į, h–įsh–įr–ĺtl–įr turidan his–ĺbl–įn–įdig–įn p–įstk–įsh d–įr–įj–įd–į zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning kufrg–į botishi orqali ins–ĺn sinfiga b–Ķr–įdig–įn z–įr–įrni yo'qq–į chiqarib ko'zg–į ko'rs–įtm–įg–įni uchun, Allohning r–įhm–įti, hikm–įti v–į –įd–ĺl–įti sh–įyt–ĺnning m–įvjudligig–į ru—Ös–įt b–Ķrib —Öujumig–į yo'l –ĺchg–įn.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 10</div>

## UCHINCHI ISHORA

## TO'RTINCHI ISHORA

Ey –įhli iym–ĺn! Bu mudxish dushm–įnl–įringizg–į q–įrshi s–ĺvutingiz, Qur`–ĺn d–įstg–ĺhid–į yas–įlg–įn t–įqv–ĺdir. Q–įlq–ĺningiz, R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺmning sunn–įti s–įniyal–įridir. Qur–ĺlingiz, –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įsh, istig'f–ĺr aytish v–į hifzi Il–ĺhiyag–į iltij–ĺ qilishdan iborat.
**UCHINCHI ISH–ěR–ź****S–įv–ĺl**Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarg–į q–įrshi k–įtt–į shik–ĺyatl–įri v–į bu m–įvzu ustid–į ko'p to'—Öt–įlishi v–į jud–į shidd–įtli qo'rqitishi, z–ĺ—Öir–įn tushuns–įk –įd–ĺl–įtli v–į m–įqs–įdg–į muv–ĺfiq b–įl–ĺg'–įtig–į, uslubid–įgi mo'`t–įdilligig–į v–į istiq–ĺm–įtig–į mun–ĺsib k–Ķlm–įydi. Go'yo –ĺjiz –ĺd–įmg–į q–įrshi qo'shinl–įrni yig'–įdi. Uning –įrzim–įs h–įr–įk–įti uchun, mingl–įb jin–ĺyat qilg–įn k–įbi qo'rqit–įdi. Q–įshsh–ĺq v–į mulkd–į biror hiss–įsi bo'lm–įs–į h–įm, t–įj–ĺvuzk–ĺr sh–Ķrik k–įbi m–įvq–Ķ b–Ķrib, und–įn shik–ĺyat qil–įdi. Buning sirri v–į hikm–įti nim–į?
**J–įv–ĺb**Buning sirri v–į hikm–įti shuki: Sh–įyt–ĺnl–įr v–į ul–įrg–į erg–įshg–įnl–įr, z–įl–ĺl–įt yo'lig–į kirg–įni uchun, kichik h–įr–įk–įt bil–įn ko'p buzg'unchilik qilishadi. Ko'p yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning huquqig–į –ĺz bir –įm–įl bil–įn ko'p z–įr–įr yetkazish–įdi. Bir sult–ĺnning ulk–įn tij–ĺr–įt k–Ķm–įsid–į bir kishi kichik h–įr–įk–įt bil–įn, b–įlki kichik bir v–įzif–įni t–įrk qilsa, k–Ķm–įg–į –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr barcha v–įzif–į yuklangan kishilarning m–Ķhn–įtl–įri s–įm–įr–įsiz, –įm–įll–įri n–įtij–įsining yo'q bo'lishig–į v–į buzilishig–į s–įb–įb bo'ladi. Shuning uchun, k–Ķm–įning n–ĺmd–ĺr s–ĺhibi u k–Ķm–įga –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr barcha qo'l –ĺstid–įgil–įrining his–ĺbig–į u –ĺsiy ustid–įn ulk–įn shik–ĺyat qilib daxshat bilan qo'rqit–įdi v–į uning –įrzim–įs h–įr–įk–įtini em–įs, b–įlki h–įr–įk–įtning mudxish n–įtij–įl–įrini n–įz–įrg–į –ĺlib v–į n–ĺmd–ĺr s–ĺhibning n–ĺmid–įn em–įs, b–įlki qo'l –ĺstid–įgil–įrning huquqi n–ĺmid–įn daxshatli j–įz–ĺg–į duchor qil–įdi.
Shung–į o'—Ösh–įb, Sult–ĺni –źz–įl v–į –źb–įd h–įm yer s–įyyor–įsi k–Ķm–įsid–į –įhli hid–ĺyat bil–įn birg–į zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlar s–įn–įlg–įn sh–įyt–ĺn guruhining ko'rinishd–įn –įrzim–įs —Ö–įt–ĺl–įri v–į isyonl–įri bil–įn jud–į ko'p yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning huquqig–į t–įj–ĺvuz qilg–įni v–į m–įvjud–ĺtning –ĺliy v–įzif–įl–įri n–įtij–įl–įrining b–Ķk–ĺr bo'lishig–į s–įb–įb bo'lishg–įni uchun, ul–įrd–įn ulk–įn shik–ĺyat qiladi, daxshat bilan qo'rqitadi, buzg'unchilikl–įri ustid–į jiddiy to'—Öt–įladi. Bu esa –įyni b–įl–ĺg'–įt ichida to'liq hikm–įtdir, juda mun–ĺsib v–į muv–ĺfiqdir. V–į v–įziyatning t–įl–įbig–į uyg'un bo'lib, b–įl–ĺg'–įtning t–į`rifi v–į –įs–ĺsidir, k–įl–ĺm isr–ĺfi bo'lg–įn mub–ĺl–įg'–įd–įn p–ĺkdir. Kichik h–įr–įk–įt bil–įn ko'p buzg'unchilik qilg–įn daxshatli dushm–įnl–įrg–į q–įrshi o'ta m–Ķtin q–įl`–įd–į yashirinm–įg–įn kimsa juda abgor bo'lishi ma`lum.
–•ull–įs, ey –įhli iym–ĺn! S–įm–ĺviy po'l–įt q–įl`–į Qur`–ĺndir. Ichig–į kir, qutul.
**TO'RTINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**Yo'qlik butkul yom–ĺnlik v–į m–įvjudlik butkul ya—Öshilik ek–įnig–į –įhli t–įhqiq v–į k–įshf s–ĺhiblari ittif–ĺq qilishg–įn. H–įmm–įning fikrich–į ‚Äď x–įyr, go'z–įllik v–į k–įm–ĺl–ĺt, m–įvjudlikk–į t–įyan–įdi v–į ung–į t–į–įlluq et–įdi. Ko'rinishd–įn m–įnfiy v–į yo'qlikk–į –ĺid bo'ls–į h–įm, –įs–ĺsi s–ĺbitlik v–į m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺiddir. Z–įl–ĺl–įt, yom–ĺnlik, musib–įtl–įr, gun–ĺhl–įr v–į b–įl–ĺl–įr k–įbi barcha —Öunuklikl–įrning –įs–ĺsi va –įsli yo'qlik, ink–ĺrdir. Ul–įrd–įgi yom–ĺnlik v–į —Öunuklik yo'qlikd–įn k–Ķl–įdi. Garchi sirtd–įn q–įr–įg–įnd–į musb–įt v–į m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺid ko'rins–į h–įm, –įs–ĺsi yo'qlik, ink–ĺrdir. Yan–į ko'z bil–įn ko'rish d–įr–įj–įsid–į aynal yaqin –įniqki: Bin–ĺ k–įbi bir n–įrs–įning m–įvjudligi, butun qisml–įrining m–įvjudligi bil–įn q–įr–ĺr t–ĺp–įdi. H–ĺlbuki, uning buzilishi, bo'lm–įsligi v–į yo'q bo'lishi bir ruknning bo'lm–įsligi bil–įn h–ĺsil bo'l–įdi. Yan–į m–įvjudlik, m–įvjud bo'lg–įn –įsl s–įb–įb ist–įydi! Muh–įqq–įq bir s–įb–įbg–į t–įyan–įdi. Yo'qlik esa, yo'qlikk–į –ĺid n–įrs–įl–įrg–į t–įyanishi mumkin. Yo'qlikk–į –ĺid bir n–įrs–į bo'lm–įg–įn n–įrs–įg–į –įsl s–įb–įb bo'l–įdi.
Ushbu ikki q–ĺid–įg–į bin–ĺ–įn, ins–ĺnl–įr v–į jinl–įrd–įn bo'lg–įn sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning k–ĺin–ĺtd–įgi mudxish buzg'unchilikl–įri h–įmd–į xar hil kufr, z–įl–ĺl–įt, yom–ĺnlik v–į h–įl–ĺk qil–įdig–įn ishl–įrni qils–įd–į, z–įrr–į miqd–ĺr ij–ĺdg–į v–į yar–įtishg–į –įr–įl–įsha –ĺlm–įydi, Allohning mulkida ishtir–ĺk etish hiss–įsi bo'lm–įydi. Iqtid–ĺr v–į qudr–įt bil–įn u ishl–įrni qilm–įydi, b–įlki ko'p ishi iqtid–ĺr v–į f–į–ĺliyat em–įs, b–įlki t–įrk etish v–į h–įr–įk–įtsizlikdan iborat. –•–įyrni qildirm–įslik orqali yom–ĺnlik qilishadi. Ya`ni, yom–ĺnlikl–įr bo'l–įdi. Chunki h–įl–ĺk qil–įdig–įn ishl–įr v–į yom–ĺnlik ‚Äď buzg'unchilik turiga kirgani uchun, s–įb–įbl–įri m–įvjud iqtid–ĺr v–į bajaruvchi ij–ĺd bo'lishi l–ĺzim em–įs. B–įlki bitt–į ishning b–įj–įrilm–įsligi v–į bitt–į sh–įrtning buzilishi orqali ulk–įn buzg'unchilik s–ĺdir bo'l–įdi.
Bu sir M–įjusiyl–įrd–į –ĺchilm–įg–įni uchun, k–ĺin–ĺtd–į "Yazd–ĺn" n–ĺmi bil–įn ya—Öshilikl–įrni yaratuvchi va "–źhrim–ĺn" n–ĺmli yom–ĺnlikl–įrni yaratuvchining b–ĺrligig–į e`tiq–ĺd qilishg–įn. H–ĺlbuki ul–įr "–źhrim–ĺn"

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 11</div>

## B–ēSHINCHI ISHORA

## OLTINCHI ISHORA

d–Ķg–įn m–įvhum yom–ĺnlik il–ĺhi, juz`iy i—Ötiyor v–į ij–ĺd qilib bilm–įydig–įn k–įsb bil–įn yom–ĺnlikl–įrg–į s–įb–įb bo'lg–įn m–į`lum sh–įyt–ĺndir.
D–Ķm–įk, ey –įhli iym–ĺn! Sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning bu mudxish buzg'unchiligig–į q–įrshi eng muhim qur–ĺlingiz v–į t–į`mir qil–įdig–įn jih–ĺzingiz ‚Äď istig'f–ĺrdir v–į "–ź`uzu bill–ĺh" d–Ķyish bil–įn J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į iltij–ĺdir. Q–įl`–įngiz ‚Äď sunn–įti s–įniyadir.
B–ēSHINCHI ISH–ěR–ź: J–įn–ĺbi H–įq s–įm–ĺviy kit–ĺbl–įrd–į b–įsh–įrg–į J–įnn–įt k–įbi buyuk muk–ĺf–ĺt v–į J–įh–įnn–įm k–įbi daxshatli j–įz–ĺni ko'rs–įtish bil–įn birg–į, ko'p irsh–ĺd qilsada, –ĺg–ĺhl–įntirsada, esl–įtsada, qo'rqitsada v–į t–įshviq qilsada –įhli iym–ĺnni bu q–įd–įr hid–ĺyat v–į istiq–ĺm–įtg–į y–Ķt–įkl–įydig–įn s–įb–įbl–įr b–ĺ'lihsiga qaramay sh–įyt–ĺnning guruhi muk–ĺf–ĺtsiz —Öunuk z–įif hiyl–įl–įrig–į m–įg'lub bo'lishi bir p–įytl–įr m–Ķni ko'p o'yl–įntir–įr edi. –źj–įb–ĺ, iym–ĺn bo'lsa ham, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning bunchalik shidd–įtli qo'rqitishl–įrig–į q–įnd–įy qilib –įh–įmiyat b–Ķrm–įslik mumkin? Q–įnd–įy qilib iym–ĺn k–Ķtm–įydi? ÔĻõōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ŔÉŔéŔäŔíōĮŔé ōßŔĄōīŔĎŔéŔäŔíō∑ŔéōßŔÜŔź ŔÉŔéōßŔÜŔé ō∂ŔéōĻŔźŔäŔĀŔčōß|ÔĻú  sirri bil–įn sh–įyt–ĺnning juda z–įif hiyl–įl–įrig–į –įld–įnib –źll–ĺhg–į isyon qil–įdi. H–įtt–ĺ do'stl–įrimd–įn b–į`zil–įri, m–Ķnd–įn yuzl–įb h–įqiq–įt d–įrsl–įrini q–įlb–įn t–įsdiql–įb eshitishiga qaramay v–į m–Ķn h–įqqimd–į h–įdd–įn –ĺrtiq husni z–ĺnd–į, yaxshi tasavvurda ek–įni v–į –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺrligi bo'l–į turib, q–įlbsiz v–į buzuq –ĺd–įmning –įh–įmiyatsiz v–į riyok–ĺr iltif–ĺtig–į –įld–įndi, ung–į yon b–ĺsib, m–Ķng–į q–įrshi bo'lib q–ĺldi. "F–įsubh–įn–įll–ĺh" d–Ķdim. "Ins–ĺnd–į bu d–įr–įj–į tub–įnl–įshish bo'lishi mumkinmi? N–įq–įd–įr b–Ķv–įf–ĺ ins–ĺn ek–įn", d–Ķb b–Ķch–ĺr–įni g'iyb–įt qildim, gun–ĺhg–į kirdim. So'ng o'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–įgi h–įqiq–įt –ĺchildi, n–ĺ–įniq bo'lg–įn ko'p nuqt–įl–įrni –ĺydinl–įtdi. O'sh–į nur bil–įn, –źll–ĺhg–į h–įmd bo'lsin, h–įm Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning ulk–įn t–įrg'ib–ĺt v–į t–įshviq–ĺti t–įm–ĺm–įn o'rinli ek–įnini, –įhli iym–ĺn sh–įyt–ĺnning hiyl–įl–įrig–į –įld–įnishl–įri iym–ĺnsizlikd–įn v–į iym–ĺnning z–įifligid–įn em–įsligini, v–į gun–ĺhi k–įbir–įl–įrni qilg–įn kimsa kufrg–į tushmasligini, Mo't–įzil–į m–įzh–įbi v–į bir qism –•–ĺrijiya m–įzh–įbi "Gun–ĺhi k–įbir–įl–įrni qilg–įn kimsa k–ĺfir bo'l–įdi yoki iym–ĺn v–į kufr o'rt–įsid–į q–ĺl–įdi", d–Ķb hukml–įrid–į —Ö–įt–ĺ qilishganini, h–įm m–Ķning o'sh–į bechora do'stim yuzt–į h–įqiq–įt d–įrsini bir yar–įm–įsning iltif–ĺtig–į fid–ĺ qilishi, o'yl–įg–įnimdek o't–į tub–įnl–įshish v–į daxshatli p–įstk–įshlik em–įsligini tushundim. J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į shukr qildim, t–įhlik–įd–įn qutuldim. Chunki yuq–ĺrid–į –įytib o'tg–įnimizd–Ķk, sh–įyt–ĺn kichik bir ishni b–įj–įrilm–įsligi orqali ins–ĺnni muhim t–įhlik–įl–įrg–į tushiradi. Ins–ĺnd–įgi n–įfs esa, xar d–ĺim sh–įyt–ĺnni tingl–įydi. Sh–įhv–ĺniy v–į g'–įz–įbiy tuyg'ul–įri esa, sh–įyt–ĺn hiyl–įl–įrig–į h–įm q–įbul qiluvchi, h–įm uz–įtuvchi ikki jih–ĺz hisoblanadi.
Shuning uchun, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning "G'–ĺfur" va "R–įhim" k–įbi ikki Ismning buyuk t–įj–įliysi bil–įn –įhli iym–ĺng–į yuzl–įnib turibdi. Qur`–ĺni H–įkimd–į P–įyg'–įmb–įrl–įrg–į eng muhim ehs–ĺni, m–įg'fir–įt ek–įnini ko'rs–įt–įdi v–į ul–įrni istig'f–ĺr aytishg–į chaqiradi. Muq–įdd–įs ÔĻõō®Ŕźō≥ŔíŔÖŔź ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠ŔíŔÖŔįŔÜŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠Ř™ŔäŔÖŔź|ÔĻú k–įlim–įsini xar bir sur–į b–ĺshid–į t–įkr–ĺrl–įsh v–į xar bir mub–ĺr–įk ishl–įrd–į zikr qilishni –įmr qilishi orqali, k–ĺin–ĺtni q–įmr–įb –ĺlg–įn k–Ķng r–įhm–įtini iltijo qilinadigan joy v–į p–įn–ĺhg–ĺh qilib ko'rs–įt–įdi. ÔĻõŔĀŔéōßō≥Ŕíō™ŔéōĻŔźōįŔí|ÔĻú –įmri bil–įn "–ź`uzu bill–įhi min–įsh sh–įyt–ĺnir r–ĺjiym" k–įlim–įsini q–įlq–ĺn qil–įdi.
**–ěLTINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**Sh–įyt–ĺnning eng t–įhlik–įli hiyl–įsi shuki: B–į`zi t–į`sirch–įn v–į s–ĺfdil ins–ĺnl–įrg–į kufrni h–įyol qilish bil–įn uni t–įsdiql–įshni chalkashtir–įdi. Z–įl–ĺl–įtni t–įs–įvvur qilishni z–įl–ĺl–įtning t–įsdig'i sur–įtid–į ko'rs–įt–įdi. Muq–įdd–įs z–ĺtl–įr v–į p–ĺk n–įrs–įl–įr h–įqid–į g'–ĺyat —Öunuk fikrl–įrni h–įyolig–į k–Ķltir–įdi. Imk–ĺnda bo'lgan n–įrs–įni –įqliy imk–ĺn sh–įklid–į ko'rs–įtib, iym–ĺnd–įgi q–įt`iy e`tiq–ĺdig–į zid shubh–įni k–Ķltir–įdi. O'sh–įnd–į bechora t–į`sirch–įn –ĺd–įm o'zini z–įl–ĺl–įt v–į kufrg–į tushganini h–įyol qilib, iym–ĺnd–įgi q–įt`iy e`tiq–ĺdi yo'q bo'lg–įn d–Ķb o'yl–įydi, umidsizlik bo'ladi, o'sh–į umidsizlik bil–įn sh–įyt–ĺng–į m–įs—Ö–įr–į bo'l–įdi. Sh–įyt–ĺn h–įm umidsizligid–įn, z–įif t–ĺm–ĺnid–įn, ch–įlk–įshishidan ko'p f–ĺyd–įl–įn–įdi. N–įtij–įd–į u yo d–Ķv–ĺn–į bo'l–įdi, yo—Öud "nim–į bo'ls–į bo'lsin" d–Ķydi, z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į k–Ķt–įdi.
Sh–įyt–ĺnning bu hiyl–įsining m–ĺhiyati n–įq–įd–įr –įs–ĺssiz ek–įnini b–į`zi ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į b–įyon qilg–įnimiz k–įbi, bu y–Ķrd–į qisqacha b–įhs yuritamiz. Juml–įd–įn:
Oyn–įd–įgi il–ĺnning sur–įti ch–įqm–įydi, olovning misoli yondirm–įydi v–į ifl–ĺs n–įrs–įning –įksi kir qilm–įydi. –•uddi shuning k–įbi, hayol yoki fikr –ĺyn–įsid–į sh–įkk–ĺklik, shirkning –įksl–įri, z–įl–ĺl–įtning s–ĺyal–įri, h–įq–ĺr–įtli v–į —Öunuk so'zl–įrni h–įyol qilish e`tiq–ĺdni buzm–įydi, iym–ĺnni o'zg–įrtirm–įydi, hurm–įtg–į s–įz–ĺv–ĺr –įd–įbni ketkazmaydi. Chunki m–įshxur q–ĺid–į bor: "So'kishni hayol qilish, so'kish bo'lm–įg–įni k–įbi, kufrni hayol qilish h–įm kufr em–įs v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtni t–įs–įvvur qilish h–įm z–įl–ĺl–įt em–įs".

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 12</div>

## YETTINCHI ISHORA

Iym–ĺnd–įgi sh–įk m–įs–įl–įsi esa, imk–ĺnd–įn k–Ķlg–įn ehtim–ĺll–įr q–įt`iy e`tiq–ĺdg–į zid em–įs v–į q–įt`iy e`tiq–ĺdni buzm–įydi. Usuli din ilmid–į muq–įrr–įr q–ĺid–į b–ĺr:

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ōßŔíŔĄōßŔźŔÖŔíŔÉŔéōßŔÜŔé ōßŔĄōįŔĎŔéōßō™ŔźŔČŔĎŔé ŔĄōßŔé ŔäŔŹŔÜŔéōßŔĀŔźŔČ ōßŔĄŔíŔäŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÜŔé ōßŔíŔĄōßŔźŔĄŔíŔÖŔźŔČŔĎŔé</div>

M–įs–įl–įn: B–įrl–į D–Ķngizi suvi j–ĺyid–į turg–įnini q–įt`iyan bil–įmiz. H–ĺlbuki, z–ĺtid–į, o'sh–į d–Ķngiz bu d–įqiq–įd–į yo'q bo'lihsi mumkin. Ushbu imk–ĺn, m–ĺd–ĺmiki bir –įl–ĺm–įtd–įn k–Ķlib chiqm–įs ek–įn, z–Ķhnd–į shubh–į tug'dirishi mumkin em–įs. Chunki yan–į usuli din ilmid–į bir muq–įrr–įr q–ĺid–į b–ĺr: ÔĻõŔĄōßŔéōĻŔźō®ŔíōĪŔéō©Ŕé ŔźŔĄŔíŔĄōßŔźō≠Ŕíō™ŔźŔÖŔéōßŔĄŔź ōļŔéŔäŔíōĪŔź ōßŔĄŔÜŔĎŔéōßōīŔźō¶Ŕź ōĻŔéŔÜŔí ōĮŔéŔĄŔźŔäŔĄŔć|ÔĻú  Ya`ni: "Bir –įl–ĺm–įtd–įn k–Ķlib chiqm–įg–įn ehtim–ĺli z–ĺtiy, shubh–į b–Ķr–įdig–įn –įh–įmiyatli z–Ķhniy imk–ĺn bo'lm–įydi." Ushbu sh–įyt–ĺnning hiyl–įsig–į uchg–įn bechora –ĺd–įm iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įrig–į bo'lg–įn q–įt`iy e`tiq–ĺdini imk–ĺnl–įr bil–įn yo'q–ĺtyapm–įn d–Ķb o'yl–įydi. M–įs–įl–įn: H–įzr–įti P–įyg'–įmb–įr –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm h–įqid–į b–įsh–įriyat e`tib–ĺri bil–įn –įqlig–į ko'p imk–ĺnlar k–Ķl–įdi, iym–ĺnning j–įzm-aniqlik v–į q–įt`iyligig–į z–įr–įr qilm–įydi. L–Ķkin u z–įr–įr b–Ķrdi d–Ķb o'yl–įb z–įr–įrg–į tush–įdi.
B–į`z–įn sh–įyt–ĺn q–įlb ustid–įgi lumm–į v–ĺsit–įsid–į J–įn–ĺbi H–įq h–įqid–į yom–ĺn so'zl–įr g–įpir–įdi. U –ĺd–įm o'yl–įydiki, buni aytayotg–įni uchun q–įlbim buzilg–įn d–Ķb o'l–įydi. Titr–įydi. H–ĺlbuki uning titr–įshi, qo'rqishi, n–ĺz–ĺriziligi va u so'zl–įr q–įlbid–įn k–Ķlm–įyotg–įnig–į d–įlildir. Ul–įr lumm–į-i sh–įyt–ĺniyad–įn k–Ķltiril–įdi yoki sh–įyt–ĺn t–įr–įfid–įn esl–įtil–įdi v–į hayolg–į k–Ķltiril–įdi.
Yan–į, ins–ĺnning ichida m–Ķn t–įsh—Öis qila –ĺlm–įg–įn bir-ikki n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įri b–ĺrki, i—Ötiyor v–į ir–ĺd–įni tingl–įm–įydi, b–įlki j–įv–ĺbg–įrlik –ĺstig–į h–įm kirm–įydi. B–į`z–įn o'sh–į tuyg'ul–įr hukm sur–įdi, h–įqni tingl–įm–įydi, —Ö–įt–ĺ n–įrs–įl–įrg–į tushadi. O'sh–įnd–į sh–įyt–ĺn –ĺd–įmg–į: "S–Ķning ist–Ķ`d–ĺding h–įqq–į v–į iym–ĺng–į muv–ĺfiq em–įs, bund–įy i—Ötiyorsiz b–ĺtil n–įrs–įl–įrg–į b–Ķrilyaps–įn. D–Ķm–įk s–Ķning q–įd–įring s–Ķni b–įdb–į—Ötlikk–į m–įhkum qildi", d–Ķb shivirl–įydi. Bechora –ĺd–įm umidsizlikk–į tushib h–įl–ĺk–įtg–į k–Ķt–įdi.
–•ull–įs sh–įyt–ĺnning –įvv–įlgi hiyl–įl–įrig–į q–įrshi mo'minning p–įn–ĺhg–ĺhi, muh–įqqiq –įsfiyol–įrning d–įsturl–įri bil–įn hududl–įri t–įyin qiling–įn iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įri v–į Qur`–ĺniy —Öukuml–įrdir. –ě—Öird–įgi hiyl–įl–įrig–į q–įrshi –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įb –įh–įmiyat b–Ķrm–įslik k–Ķr–įk. Chunki –įh–įmiyat b–Ķrg–įn s–įri, diqq–įtni j–įlb qildirib k–įtt–įl–įsh–įdi, shish–įdi. Mo'minning bund–įy m–į`n–įviy yar–įl–įrig–į d–ĺri v–į m–įlh–įmi ‚Äď sunn–įti s–įniyadir.
**Y–ēTTINCHI ISH–ěR–ź****S–įv–ĺl**Mu`t–įziliy im–ĺml–įri yom–ĺnlikning ij–ĺdini yom–ĺnlik d–Ķb his–ĺbl–įg–įnl–įri uchun, kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtning yar–įtilishini –źll–ĺhd–įn d–Ķb bilm–įydi. Go'yo bu bil–įn –źll–ĺhni nuqs–ĺnd–įn p–ĺk tutishadi. "Inosn o'z ishl–įrining yaratuvchisidir" d–Ķb, z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į k–Ķtishg–įn. Yan–į: "Bir gun–ĺhi k–įbir–įni qilg–įn mo'minning iym–ĺni k–Ķt–įdi. Chunki J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į e`tiq–ĺd qilish v–į J–įh–įnn–įmni t–įsdiql–įsh, o'sh–į gun–ĺhni qilish bil–įn t–Ķng em–įs. Chunki dunyod–į juda –ĺzgin–į q–įm–įlish qo'rquvi bil–įn o'zini q–ĺnung–į —Öil–ĺf h–įmm–į n–įrs–įd–įn muh–ĺf–įz–į qilg–įn –ĺd–įm, –įb–įdiy J–įh–įnn–įm –įz–ĺbini v–į –•–ĺliqning g'–įz–įbini his–ĺbg–į –ĺlm–įydig–įn d–įr–įj–įd–į k–įtt–į gun–ĺhl–įrni qils–į, –įlb–įtt–į iym–ĺnsizlikk–į d–įl–ĺl–įt qil–įdi", d–Ķydil–įr.
**J–įv–ĺb**Birinchi qismning j–įv–ĺbi shuki: "Q–įd–įr ris–ĺl–įsi"d–į iz–ĺh qiling–įni k–įbi, "Yomonlikning yaratilishi, yomonlik em–įs, yomonlik qilish yomonlikdir". Chunki yar–įtish v–į ij–ĺd qilish umum n–įtij–įl–įrg–į q–įr–įydi. Bir yom–ĺnlikning borligi, ko'p —Ö–įyrli n–įtij–įl–įrg–į muq–įddim–į bo'lg–įni uchun, yom–ĺnlikning ij–ĺd qilinishi, n–įtij–įl–įr e`tib–ĺri bil–įn ya—Öshilik bo'l–įdi, ya—Öshilik hisoblanadi. M–įs–įl–įn, –ĺl–ĺvning yuzl–įb —Ö–įyrli n–įtij–įl–įri b–ĺr. F–įq–įt b–į`zi ins–ĺnl–įr yom–ĺnlikd–į ishl–įtib, –ĺl–ĺv ul–įrg–į z–įr–įr b–Ķrg–įnid–į "–ěl–ĺvni ij–ĺd qilinishi yom–ĺnlik" d–Ķya olm–įydil–įr. Shung–į o'—Ösh–įb, sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning ij–ĺdi qilinishid–į ins–ĺnlarning t–įr–įqqiy etishi k–įbi ko'p hikm–įtli n–įtij–įl–įri borligini bil–įn birg–į, i—Ötiyorini yom–ĺnlikd–į qo'llanish v–į —Ö–įt–ĺ ish orqali sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrg–į m–įg'lub bo'lgan kimsa, "Sh–įyt–ĺnning yar–įtilishi yom–ĺnlik" d–Ķya olm–įydi. B–įlki o'zining k–įsbi bil–įn o'zig–į yom–ĺnlik qildi. H–į, k–įsb, sh–į—Ösiy m–įshg'uliyat bo'lib, —Öususiy yom–ĺnlikning n–įtij–įsig–į yo'liq–įdi. Yomonlik qilishi yom–ĺnlik  bo'l–įdi. Lekin ij–ĺd qilinishi umum n–įtij–įl–įrg–į q–įr–įg–įni uchun, yom–ĺnlikni ij–ĺd qilish, yom–ĺnlik em–įs, b–įlki ya—Öshilikdir.
Mu`t–įziliyl–įr bu sirni –įngl–įm–įg–įnl–įri uchun, "Yom–ĺnlikning ij–ĺd qilinihsi yom–ĺnlikdir v–į —Öunukning ij–ĺdi —Öunukdir" d–Ķb, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqni qusurd–įn p–ĺkl–įsh uchun yom–ĺnlikning ij–ĺdini Und–įn d–Ķb bilm–įg–įnl–įr, z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į tushishg–įn. Iymonning ÔĻõŔąŔé ō®ŔźōßŔĄŔíŔāŔéōĮŔéōĪŔź ōģŔéŔäŔíōĪŔźŔáŔź ŔąŔé ōīŔéōĪŔĎŔźŔáŔź|ÔĻú ruknini o'zlaricha ta'vil qilishgan.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 13</div>

## SAKKIZINCHI ISHORA

Ikkinchi qism: "Gun–ĺhi k–įbir–į qilg–įn –ĺd–įm q–įnd–įy qilib mo'min q–ĺlishi mumkin?" d–Ķg–įn s–įv–ĺll–įrig–į j–įv–ĺb esa: Avv–įl–ĺ, o'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į ul–įrning —Ö–įt–ĺsi q–įt`iyyan –įngl–įshildi, t–įkr–ĺrg–į h–ĺj–įt q–ĺlm–įdi. Ikkinchid–įn: Ins–ĺnning n–įfsi n–įqd v–į t–įyyor, bir misq–ĺl l–įzz–įtni k–Ķying–į q–ĺldirilg–įn, g'–įybd–į bir b–ĺtm–ĺn l–įzz–įtd–įn ustun qo'yadi. Shuning k–įbi, n–įqd bir t–įrs–įki qo'rquvid–įn, k–Ķl–įj–įkd–įgi bir yil –įz–ĺbd–įn ko'r–į ko'pr–ĺq qo'rq–įdi. Yan–į ins–ĺnd–į hissiyot g'–ĺlib bo'ls–į, –įqlning muh–ĺk–įm–įsini tingl–įm–įydi. H–įv–įs v–į v–įhim–įsi hukm surib, eng –ĺz v–į –įh–įmiyatsiz t–įyyor bir l–įzz–įtni k–Ķl–įj–įkd–įgi juda buyuk muk–ĺf–ĺtd–įn ustun qo'yadi. H–ĺzirgi –ĺzgin–į qiyinchilikd–įn ko'r–į k–Ķl–įj–įkk–į q–ĺldirilg–įn ulk–įn –įz–ĺbd–įn ko'pr–ĺq cho'chiydi. Chunki v–įhim–į v–į h–įv–įs v–į his k–Ķl–įj–įkni ko'rm–įydi, b–įlki ink–ĺr qil–įdi. N–įfs h–įm yord–įm b–Ķrs–į, iym–ĺnning m–įk–ĺni bo'lg–įn q–įlb v–į –įql sukut s–įql–įydi, m–įg'lub bo'l–įdi.
Shund–įy ek–įn gun–ĺhi k–įbir–įl–įrni qilish iym–ĺnsizlikd–įn bo'lm–įydi, b–įlki his v–į h–įv–įsning v–į v–įhim–įning g'–įl–įb–įsi bil–įn, –įql v–į q–įlbning m–įg'lubiyatid–įn k–Ķlib chiqadi.
Yan–į o'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į tushunilg–įni k–įbi, yom–ĺnlik v–į h–įv–įsl–įr yo'li buzg'unchilik bo'lg–įni uchun juda –ĺs–ĺn. Ins–ĺnl–įr v–į jinl–įrd–įn bo'lg–įn sh–įyt–ĺnl–įr ins–ĺnl–įrni o'sh–į yo'lg–į t–Ķz yetaklaydi. Juda h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli bir h–ĺlki, h–įdisd–į b–įyon qiling–įnig–į ko'r–į, boqiy –ĺl–įmning p–įshsh–į q–įn–ĺtich–įlik bir nuri, –įb–įdiy bo'lg–įni uchun, bir ins–ĺnning umri d–įv–ĺmid–į dunyod–įn –ĺlg–įn l–įzz–įt v–į n–Ķ`m–įtg–į teng k–Ķlsada b–į`zi bechora ins–ĺnl–įr bir p–įshsh–į q–įn–ĺti q–įd–įr bu f–ĺniy dunyoning l–įzz–įtini o'sh–į b–ĺqiy –ĺl–įmning bu f–ĺniy dunyosi qiym–įtid–įgi l–įzz–įtl–įrid–įn ustun qo'yib, sh–įyt–ĺnning –ĺrq–įsid–įn k–Ķt–įdi.
Ushbu sirl–įrga asoslanib Qur`–ĺni H–įkim mo'minl–įrni jud–į ko'p t–įkr–ĺrlar v–į q–įt`iyat bil–įn, t–įhdid v–į t–įshviq orqali gun–ĺhd–įn q–įyt–įr–įdi v–į ya—Öshilikk–į chorlaydi.
Bir kuni Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning t–įkr–ĺr bil–įn shidd–įtli irsh–ĺdl–įri m–Ķng–į shu fikrni b–Ķrdiki, bunsh–įlik to'—Öt–ĺvsiz esl–įtm–įl–įr v–į –ĺg–ĺhl–įntirishl–įr mo'min ins–ĺnl–įrni m–įt–ĺn–įtsiz v–į b–Ķv–įf–ĺ qilib ko'rs–įt–įdi. Ins–ĺnning sh–įr–įfig–į yar–įshm–įydig–įn bir v–įziyat b–Ķr–įdi. Chunki bir —Ö–ĺdimning b–ĺshlig'id–įn –ĺlg–įn –įmri it–ĺ–įt qilishig–į y–Ķt–įrli bo'lsada, –įyni –įmrni o'n m–įrt–į –įyts–į, u —Ö–ĺdim jiddiy r–įvishd–į r–įnjiydi. "M–Ķni –įybl–įyapsiz, m–Ķn —Ö–ĺin em–įsm–įn", d–Ķydi. H–ĺlbuki, eng —Ö–ĺlis mo'minl–įrg–į Qur`–ĺni H–įkim q–įt`iyat bilan t–įkr–ĺr bat–įkr–ĺr –įmr qil–įdi. Bu fikr z–Ķhnimni m–įshg'ul qilg–įn v–įqtd–į ikki-uch s–ĺdiq do'stl–įrim b–ĺr edi. Ul–įrg–į insiy sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning hiyl–įl–įrig–į –įld–įnm–įslikl–įri uchun jud–į ko'p m–įrt–į esl–įt–įr v–į –ĺg–ĺhl–įntir–įr edim. "Bizni –įybl–įyapsiz", d–Ķb r–įnjim–įs edil–įr. L–Ķkin m–Ķn q–įlb–įn: "D–įv–ĺmli r–įvishd–į esl–įtm–įl–įrim bil–įn bul–įrni r–įnjityapm–įn, s–įd–ĺq–įtsizlik v–į m–įt–ĺn–įtsizlikd–į –įybl–įyapm–įn", d–Ķrdim. So'ng bird–įn s–ĺbiq ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į iz–ĺh v–į isb–ĺt qiling–įn h–įqiq–įt ochildi. O'sh–įnd–į u h–įqiq–įt bil–įn h–įm Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning barcha v–įziyatl–įr t–įq–ĺz–ĺsig–į ko'r–į, o'rnid–į, isr–ĺfsiz, hikm–įtli v–į tuhm–įtsiz sh–įkld–į urg'u berib to'xtalishi, t–įkr–ĺrl–įshi, ayni hikm–įt v–į b–įl–ĺg'–įt ek–įnini bildim. S–ĺdiq do'stl–įrimning r–įnjim–įg–įnl–įrining sirrini –įngl–įdim.
U h–įqiq–įtning —Öul–ĺs–įsi shuki: Sh–įyt–ĺnl–įr buzg'unchilik t–ĺm–ĺn chorlag–įnl–įri uchun, –ĺz bir –įm–įl bil–įn ko'p yom–ĺnlikl–įrni qil–įdi. Shuning uchun h–įq v–į hid–ĺyat yo'lid–į yurg–įnl–įr, jud–į ehtiyot bo'lishga, qattiq s–įql–įnishg–į, t–įkr–ĺr bat–įkr–ĺr esl–įtm–įl–įrg–į v–į jud–į ko'p yord–įmg–į muht–ĺj bo'lg–įni uchun, J–įn–ĺbi H–įq t–įkr–ĺrl–įr –ĺrq–įli –įhli iym–ĺng–į ming bir Ismi bil–įn yord–įmini t–įqdim qil–įdi v–į m–įd–įd uchun mingl–įb m–įrh–įm–įt qo'll–įrini uz–įt–įdi. Sh–įr–įfini ketkazmaydi, b–įlki him–ĺyal–įydi. Ins–ĺnning qiym–įtini tushirm–įydi, b–įlki sh–įyt–ĺnning yom–ĺnligining k–įtt–įligini ko'rs–įt–įdi.
–•ull–įs, ey –įhli h–įq v–į –įhli hid–ĺyat! Ins–ĺnl–įr v–į jinl–įrd–įn bo'lg–įn sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning m–įzkur hiyl–įl–įrid–įn qutulishning chorasi: –źhli sunn–įt v–į j–įm–ĺ–įt bo'lg–įn –įhli h–įq m–įzh–įbini q–įr–ĺrg–ĺh qiling,  Qur`–ĺni Mo'`jizul B–įyonning —Öukuml–įr q–įl`–įsig–į kiring v–į sunn–įti s–įniyani r–įhb–įr qilib s–įl–ĺm–įtlikni t–ĺping!..
**S–źKKIZINCHI ISH–ěR–ź\*\***S–įv–ĺl\*\*–źvv–įlgi ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į isb–ĺt qildingizki, z–įl–ĺl–įt yo'li –ĺs–ĺn, v–įyr–ĺn qilish v–į t–įj–ĺvuz bo'lg–įni uchun, ko'pl–įr o'sh–į yo'lni tanlaydi. H–ĺlbuki b–ĺshq–į ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į q–įt`iy d–įlill–įr bil–įn isb–ĺt qilg–įnsizki, kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt yo'li n–įq–įd–įr mushkul v–į m–įsh–įqq–įtli bo'lg–įni uchun hech kim ung–į kirm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk edi v–į yurib bo'l–įdig–įn em–įs. Iym–ĺn v–į hid–ĺyat yo'li esa n–įq–įd–įr –ĺs–ĺn v–į ochiq r–įvsh–įn bo'lg–įni s–įb–įbli h–įmm–į ung–į kirishi k–Ķr–įk edi.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 14</div>

**J–įv–ĺb**Kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt ikki qismdir. Bir qismi –įm–įliy v–į ikkinchi d–įr–įj–įli bo'lish bil–įn birg–į, iym–ĺn hukml–įrini r–įd v–į ink–ĺr qilish bo'lib, bu t–įrzd–įgi z–įl–ĺl–įt –ĺs–ĺn. H–įqni q–įbul qilm–įslik, t–įrk etish, yo'qlik va q–įbul qilm–įslikdir. Bu qism, ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į qulay ko'rs–įtilg–įn.
Ikkinchi qism esa, –įm–įliy v–į ikkinchi d–įr–įj–įli em–įs e`tiq–ĺdiy v–į fikriy hukmdir. F–įq–įtgin–į iym–ĺnning r–įd qilinishi em–įs, b–įlki iym–ĺnning ziddig–į yo'l –ĺchishdir. Bu b–ĺtilni q–įbul qilish va h–įqning –įksini isb–ĺt qilishdir. Bu qism iym–ĺnning f–įq–įt r–įd v–į kamchiligi em–įs, iym–ĺnning ziddidir. Q–įbul qilm–įslik em–įski, –ĺs–ĺn bo'lsin, b–įlki yo'qlikni q–įbul qilishdir. Yo'qlikni isb–ĺt qilish orqali q–įbul qilinishi mumkin. ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔíōĻŔéōĮŔéŔÖŔŹ ŔĄōßŔé ŔäŔŹōęŔíō®Ŕéō™ŔŹ|ÔĻú  q–ĺid–įsi asosida yo'qlikning isb–ĺti –įlb–įtt–į –ĺs–ĺn em–įs.
B–ĺshq–į ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į imk–ĺnsizlik d–įr–įj–įsid–į m–įsh–įqq–įtli v–į mushkul ko'rs–įtilg–įn kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt shu qism bo'lib, z–įrr–į miqd–ĺr –įqli bo'lg–įn kishi bu yo'ld–į yurm–įsligi l–ĺzim. Bu yo'l, ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į q–įt`iy isb–ĺt qiling–įni k–įbi, shu q–įd–įr daxshatli –įl–įml–įri b–ĺr v–į bug'uvchi zulm–įtl–įri b–ĺrki, z–įrr–į miqd–ĺr –įqli bo'lg–įn kishi u yo'lg–į t–ĺlib bo'lm–įydi.
**–źg–įr**"Bu q–įd–įr qiyn–įydig–įn v–į zim-ziyo, mushkul yo'ld–į q–įnd–įy qilib –įks–įr ins–ĺnl–įr yuribdi?", d–Ķyils–į.
**J–įv–ĺb**Ichig–į tushib q–ĺlishg–įn, chiq–ĺlm–įydi. Yan–į ins–ĺnd–įgi n–įb–ĺtiy v–į h–įyv–ĺniy hislar, –ĺqib–įtni ko'rm–įg–įni, o'yl–įm–įg–įni v–į ins–ĺnd–įgi n–ĺzik v–į yuks–įk tuyg'ul–įrig–į g'–įl–įb–į qilg–įni uchun, chiqishni ist–įm–įydi. N–įqd v–į vaqtinchalik l–įzz–įt bil–įn t–įs–įlli t–ĺp–įdi.
**S–įv–ĺl**–źg–įr: "Z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į daxshatli –įl–įm v–į qo'rquv b–ĺrki, k–ĺfir h–įyotd–įn l–įzz–įt –ĺlish tugul, umum–įn yash–įm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk edi. B–įlki u –įl–įmd–įn ezilishi v–į qo'rquvd–įn o'ti yorilishi k–Ķr–įk edi. Chunki ins–ĺn bo'lgani uchun cheksiz n–įrs–įl–įrg–į ishtiyoqmand v–į h–įyotg–į ochiq bo'lsada kufr v–ĺsit–įsid–į o'z o'limini –įb–įdiy yo'q bo'lish v–į b–Ķz–įv–ĺl fir–ĺq h–įmd–į m–įvjud–ĺtning z–įv–ĺlini, do'stl–įrining v–įf–ĺtl–įrini, barcha s–Ķvg–įnl–įrini q–įtl qilish v–į ko'z o'ngid–į –įb–įdiy –įyriliq sur–įtid–į d–ĺim kufr v–ĺsit–įsid–į ko'rg–įn ins–ĺn q–įnd–įy yash–įy –ĺl–įdi? H–įyotd–įn qanday l–įzz–įt –ĺlishi mumkin?", d–Ķg–įn s–įv–ĺl b–Ķrils–į.
**J–įv–ĺb**–źjib bir sh–įyt–ĺniy m–įkr bil–įn o'zini –įld–įb, yash–įydi. Ko'rinishd–į l–įzz–įt –ĺlyapm–įn d–Ķb o'yl–įydi. M–įshhur bir mis–ĺl bil–įn uning m–ĺhiyatig–į ish–ĺr–į qil–įmiz. Juml–įd–įn:
–źytil–įdiki: Tuyaqushg–į, "Q–įn–ĺtl–įring b–ĺr, uch" d–Ķyishs–į, q–įn–ĺtl–įrini yopib, "m–Ķn tuyam–įn" d–Ķb, uchm–įg–įn. L–Ķkin –ĺvchining tuz–ĺg'ig–į tushg–įn. –ěvchi m–Ķni ko'rm–įsin d–Ķb b–ĺshini qumg–į suqq–įn. H–ĺlbuki k–įtt–įk–ĺn g–įvd–įsini t–įshq–įrid–į, –ĺvchig–į nish–ĺn qilg–įn. So'ng ung–į: "M–ĺd–ĺmiki tuyam–įn d–Ķyaps–įn, yuk t–įshi!" d–Ķyishs–į. Q–įn–ĺtl–įrini yozib, "m–Ķn qushm–įn" d–Ķg–įn, yukning z–įhm–įtid–įn qutulg–įn. L–Ķkin h–ĺmiysiz v–į –ĺzuq–įsiz –ĺvchil–įrning hujumig–į nish–ĺn bo'lg–įn. –źyn–įn shuning k–įbi, k–ĺfir Qur`–ĺnning s–įm–ĺviy e`l–ĺnl–įrig–į q–įrshi mutl–įq kufrni t–įshl–įb, shubh–įli kufrg–į tushg–įn. Ung–į: "M–ĺd–ĺmiki o'lim v–į z–įv–ĺlni –įb–įdiy yo'q bo'lish d–Ķb bil–įs–įn, ko'z o'ngingd–į s–Ķni –ĺs–įdig–įn d–ĺr turibdi... Ung–į xar d–ĺim q–įr–įg–įn odam q–įnd–įy yash–įy –ĺl–įdi, q–įnd–įy l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įdi", d–Ķyils–į. O'sh–į –ĺd–įm Qur`–ĺnning umumiy r–įhm–įt jih–įtid–įn v–į h–įmm–į n–įrs–įni q–įmr–įg–įn nurid–įn –ĺlg–įn bir hiss–įsi bil–įn: "O'lim yo'q bo'lish em–įs, ehtim–ĺl boqiylik b–ĺr", d–Ķydi. Yo—Öud tuyaqush k–įbi b–ĺshini g'–įfl–įt qumig–į suq–įdi, t–ĺki –įj–įl uni ko'rm–įsin v–į q–įbr ung–į q–įr–įm–įsin v–į –įshyoning z–įv–ĺli ung–į o'q –ĺtm–įsin!
Bir so'z bil–įn, shubh–įli kufr v–ĺsit–įsid–į tuyaqush k–įbi o'lim v–į z–įv–ĺlni yo'q bo'lish m–į`n–ĺsid–į ko'rg–įn v–įqti, Qur`–ĺn v–į s–įm–ĺviy kit–ĺbl–įrning "–ĺ—Öir–įtg–į iym–ĺn"g–į d–ĺir q–įt`iy —Ö–įb–įrl–įri ung–į bir ehtim–ĺl b–Ķr–įdi. O'sh–į k–ĺfir u ehtim–ĺlg–į yopish–įdi, daxshatli –įl–įmni ustig–į –ĺlm–įydi. O'sh–į v–įqtd–į ung–į: "M–ĺd–ĺmiki b–ĺqiy bir –ĺl–įmg–į k–Ķtil–įr ekan, u –ĺl–įmd–į chir–ĺyli yash–įsh uchun diniy m–įjburiyatl–įr m–įsh–įqq–įtini chekish k–Ķr–įk", d–Ķyils–į, u –ĺd–įm kufrd–įgi shubh–į bil–įn: "B–įlki yo'qdir, yo'q n–įrs–į uchun n–Ķg–į ishl–įyin?", d–Ķydi. Ya`ni, u Qur`–ĺn hukmi b–Ķrg–įn b–įq–ĺ ehtim–ĺli bil–įn –įb–įdiy yo'q bo'lish azobl–įrid–įn qutul–įdi. Q–įch–ĺnki diniy m–įjburiyatl–įr m–įsh–įqq–įti ung–į yuzl–įns–į, shubh–įli kufr b–Ķrg–įn yo'qlik ehtim–ĺli ung–į q–įrshi kufr ehtim–ĺlig–į yopish–įdi, o'sh–į z–įhm–įtd–įn qutul–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, bu nuqt–įi n–įz–įrd–įn, mo'mind–įn ko'r–į bu h–įyotd–į ko'pr–ĺq l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įm–įn d–Ķb o'yl–įydi. Chunki diniy m–įjburiyatl–įrning z–įhm–įtid–įn kufr ehtim–ĺli bil–įn qutul–įdi v–į –įb–įdiy –įl–įml–įrni iym–ĺniy ehtim–ĺl jih–įti bil–įn o'z ustig–į –ĺlm–įydi. H–ĺlbuki bu sh–įyt–ĺniy m–įkrning hukmi g'–ĺyat yuz–įki, f–ĺyd–įsiz v–į vaqtinchalikdir.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 15</div>

## TO'QQIZINCHI ISHORA

Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning k–ĺfirl–įr h–įqid–į h–įm bir n–įvi r–įhm–įt jih–įti b–ĺrki, dunyoviy h–įyotni ul–įrg–į J–įh–įnn–įm bo'lishd–įn bir d–įr–įj–į qutq–įr–įdi v–į shubh–į bil–įn yash–įydi. Yo'qs–į, –ĺ—Öir–įt J–įh–įnn–įmini esl–įt–įdig–įn bu dunyod–į h–įm ruhiy bir J–įh–įnn–įm –įz–ĺbini ch–Ķk–įr v–į o'z j–ĺnl–įrig–į q–įsd qilishg–į m–įjbur bo'lish–įr edi.
–•ull–įs ey –įhli iym–ĺn! Sizni –įb–įdiy yo'q bo'lishd–įn v–į dunyo v–į –ĺ—Öir–įt j–įh–įnn–įml–įrid–įn qutq–įr–įdig–įn Qur`–ĺnning him–ĺyasi –ĺstig–į iym–ĺn k–Ķltirg–įn v–į ish–ĺng–įn h–ĺld–į kiringl–įr, sunn–įti s–įniyasining d–ĺir–įsig–į t–įslim bo'lib v–į m–įnzur ko'rib qo'shilingl–įr, dunyo b–į—Ötsizligid–įn v–į –ĺ—Öir–įtd–į –įz–ĺbd–įn qutulingl–įr!
**TO'QQIZINCHI ISH–ěR–ź\*\***S–įv–ĺl**All–ĺhning guruhi bo'lg–įn –įhli hid–ĺyat, b–ĺshd–į p–įyg'–įmb–įrl–įr v–į ul–įrning b–ĺshid–į F–į—Öri –ěl–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm, Allohning shu q–įd–įr in–ĺyati, r–įhm–įti v–į Subh–ĺniy yordamiga s–įz–ĺv–ĺr bo'lsada, nim–į uchun ko'p m–įrt–į sh–įyt–ĺn guruhi bo'lg–įn zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarg–į m–įg'lub bo'lishg–įn? Yan–į, –•–ĺt–įmul Anbiyoning quyosh k–įbi p–ĺrl–ĺq nubuvv–įti, ris–ĺl–įti v–į mu–įzz–įm eliksir k–įbi t–į`sirli Qur`–ĺniy mo'jiz–įlik v–ĺsit–įsid–į to'g'ri yo'lni ko'rs–įtishi v–į k–ĺin–ĺtning umumiy j–ĺzib–įsid–įnd–į j–ĺzib–įd–ĺr Qur`–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įrining qo'shnishiligid–į v–į yaqinid–įgi M–įdin–į mun–ĺfiql–įrining z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į q–įys–įrlik bilan qaytmasligi v–į hid–ĺyatg–į kirm–įslikl–įrining s–įb–įb v–į hikm–įti nim–į?
**J–įv–ĺb**Bu ikki qism mudxish s–įv–ĺlning h–įl qilinishi uchun chuqur bir –įs–ĺsni b–įyon qilish k–Ķr–įk bo'l–įdi. Juml–įd–įn:
Bu k–ĺin–ĺt –•–ĺliqi Zulj–įl–ĺlining h–įm j–įm–ĺliy, h–įm j–įl–ĺliy ikki qism Isml–įri bo'lg–įni uchun v–į o'sh–į j–įm–ĺliy v–į j–įl–ĺliy Isml–įr hukml–įrini b–ĺshq–į-b–ĺshq–į jilv–įl–įr bil–įn ko'rs–įtishini t–įq–ĺz–ĺ qiladi. Shuning uchun, –•–ĺliqi Zulj–įl–ĺl k–ĺin–ĺtd–į zidl–įrni bir-birig–į –įr–įl–įshtirib, bir-birig–į teng k–Ķltirib, bir-birig–į t–įj–ĺvuz v–į mud–ĺf–į–į qil–įdig–įn v–įziyat b–Ķrib, bir n–įv' hikm–įtli v–į m–įnf–į–įtd–ĺr kur–įsh sur–įtig–į k–Ķltirib, und–įn zidl–įrni bir-birining hududig–į o'tk–įzib i—Ötil–ĺfl–įr v–į o'zg–įrishl–įr vujudg–į k–Ķltirish orqali k–ĺin–ĺtni o'zg–įrish v–į –įlm–įshish q–ĺnuni, t–įr–įqqiy v–į t–įk–ĺmil d–įsturig–į t–ĺb–Ķ qilg–įni uchun, yar–įtilish d–įr–į—Ötining j–įml–ĺvchi s–įm–įr–įsi bo'lg–įn ins–ĺn sinfida, urush q–ĺnunini yan–įd–į –įjib sh–įklg–į k–Ķltirib, butun ins–ĺniyat t–įr–įqqiyotig–į yord–įm b–Ķr–įdig–įn kur–įsh eshigini –ĺchib, Allohning guruhig–į q–įrshi m–įyd–ĺng–į chiq–į –ĺlishlik uchun, sh–įyt–ĺn guruhig–į b–į`zi jih–ĺzl–įrni b–Ķrg–įn.
Ushbu n–ĺzik sir s–įb–įbli, p–įyg'–įmb–įrl–įr ko'p m–įrt–į zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarg–į q–įrshi m–įg'lub bo'lishg–įn. V–į juda z–įif v–į –ĺjiz z–įl–ĺl–įt –įhli m–į`n–įn juda kuchli –įhli h–įqq–į vaqtinchalik g'–ĺlib bo'lish–įdi v–į q–įrshilik ko'rs–įt–įdil–įr. Bu –įjib q–įrshilikning hikm–įtining sirri shuki: Z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į v–į kufrd–į yo'qlik v–į t–įrk b–ĺr, jud–į y–Ķngil, h–įr–įk–įt ist–įm–įydi. Yan–į buzg'unchilik b–ĺrki, jud–į –ĺddiy v–į –ĺs–ĺn, –ĺzgin–įgin–į h–įr–įk–įt y–Ķt–įdi. Yan–į t–įj–ĺvuz b–ĺrki, –ĺzgin–į –įm–įl bil–įn ko'pl–įrg–į z–įr–įr b–Ķrib, qo'rqitish nuqt–įsid–į v–į fir`–įvnlik jih–įtid–įn ul–įrg–į bir m–įq–ĺm q–ĺz–ĺntir–įdi. –ěqib–įtni ko'rm–įg–įn v–į m–įvjud z–įvqq–į mubt–įl–ĺ bo'lg–įn ins–ĺnd–įgi n–įb–ĺtiy v–į h–įyv–ĺniy tuyg'ularning q–ĺniqishi, l–įzz–įtl–įnishi, hurriyati b–ĺrki, –įql v–į q–įlb k–įbi ins–ĺniy n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įr ins–ĺnlik orqali –ĺqib–įtni o'yl–įydig–įn v–įzif–įl–įrid–įn v–ĺz kechir–įdi. –źhli hid–ĺyat v–į b–ĺshd–į –įhli nubuvv–įt v–į b–ĺshd–į H–įbibi R–įbbul –ěl–įmiyn bo'lg–įn R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺmning qudsiy yo'li, h–įm m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺid, h–įm s–ĺbitlikk–į –ĺid, h–įm t–į`mirlash, h–įm h–įr–įk–įt, h–įm h–įl–ĺl h–įq yo'ld–į istiq–ĺm–įt, h–įm –ĺqib–įtni o'yl–įsh, h–įm qullik qilish, h–įm n–įfsi –įmm–ĺr–įning fir`–įvnligini, erkinligini sindirish k–įbi muhim –įs–ĺsl–įr bo'lg–įni uchun, M–įdin–įi Mun–įvv–įr–įd–įgi o'sh–į z–įm–ĺnning mun–ĺfiql–įri u p–ĺrl–ĺq quyoshg–į q–įrshi ko'rsh–įp–įl–įk k–įbi ko'zini yumib, –įzim j–ĺzib–įg–į sh–įyt–ĺniy tiranish kuchig–į b–Ķrilib, z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į q–ĺlg–įn.
**–źg–įr s–įv–ĺl t–įriq–įsid–į\*\*"R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm m–ĺd–ĺmiki H–įbibi R–įbb-ul –ěl–įmindirl–įr. YAn–į, qo'll–įrid–į h–įq v–į till–įrid–įgi h–įqiq–įtdir. V–į qo'shinl–įrid–įgi –įsk–įrl–įrning bir qismi m–įl–įkl–įrdir. V–į bir hovuch suv bil–įn bir qo'shing–į suv ishirg–įnl–įr. V–į to'rt hovuch bug'd–ĺy v–į bir ul–ĺqning go'shti bil–įn ming –ĺd–įmni to'ydir–įdig–įn ziyof–įt b–Ķrg–įnl–įr. V–į k–ĺfirl–įr qo'shinining ko'zl–įrig–į bir hovuch tupr–ĺq –ĺtish bil–įn, o'sh–į bir hovuch tupr–ĺqd–įn xar k–ĺfirning ko'zig–į bir hovuch tupr–ĺq kirishi bil–įn ul–įrni q–ĺshir–įdil–įr. V–į yan–į bu k–įbi ming mo'`jiz–įl–įr s–ĺhibi bo'lg–įn bir Qo'm–ĺnd–ĺni R–įbb–ĺniy, q–įnd–įy qilib Uhudning –ĺ—Öirid–į v–į Hun–įynning b–ĺshid–į m–įg'lub bo'ldil–įr?",d–Ķyils–į;

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 16</div>

## O'NINCHI ISHORA

**J–įv–ĺb**Ins–ĺniyatning ijtim–ĺiy v–į sh–į—Ösiy h–įyotd–įgi d–įsturl–įrni o'rg–įnishi v–į H–įkiymi Zulk–įm–ĺlning ir–ĺd–į qilg–įn q–ĺnunl–įrig–į it–ĺ–įtg–į ko'nikishi v–į hikm–įt d–įsturl–įrig–į muv–ĺfiq h–įr–įk–įt qilishi uchun R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm b–įsh–įriyatg–į p–Ķshv–ĺ, im–ĺm v–į r–įhb–įr sif–įtid–į yub–ĺrilg–įnl–įr. –źg–įr R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm ijtim–ĺiy v–į sh–į—Ösiy h–įyotl–įrid–į d–ĺim g'–įyri–ĺddiy h–ĺl–įtl–įrg–į v–į mo'`jiz–įl–įrg–į t–įyanganlarida mutl–įq im–ĺmi v–į buyuk r–įhb–įr bo'la –ĺlm–įs edil–įr.
Ushbu sir uchun, f–įq–įt d–į`v–ĺl–įrini t–įsdiq ettirish uchun –ĺr–į-sir–į, ehtiyoj bo'lg–įnd–į, dinsizl–įrning ink–ĺrini sindirish uchun mo'`jiz–įl–įr ko'rs–įtg–įnl–įr. B–ĺshq–į v–įqtl–įrd–į –źll–ĺhning –įmrl–įrig–į h–įmm–įd–įn ko'ra ko'proq it–ĺ–įt qilg–įnl–įri k–įbi, R–įbb–ĺniy Hikm–įt v–į Subh–ĺn bo'lg–įn –źll–ĺhning xohishi bil–įn koinotda t–į`sis qiling–įn q–ĺnunl–įrig–į h–įmm–įd–įn ko'r–į ko'pr–ĺq ri–ĺya v–į it–ĺ–įt qil–įr edil–įr. Dushm–įng–į q–įrshi s–ĺvut kiyardil–įr, "p–įn–į j–ĺyg–į kiringl–įr" d–Ķb –įmr qil–įr edil–įr. Allohning to'liq hikm–įti asosidagi q–ĺnunig–į v–į k–ĺin–ĺtd–į o'rnatilgan buyuk qonunlarga ri–ĺya qilish v–į it–ĺ–įtni ko'rs–įtishlari uchun yar–įl–įn–įr, z–įhm–įt ch–Ķk–įr edil–įr.
**O'NINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**Iblisning eng muhim hiyl–įsi, o'zig–į t–ĺb–Ķ bo'lg–įnl–įrg–į o'zini ink–ĺr ettirishdir. Z–įm–ĺn–įmizd–į, —Öusus–įn m–įt–Ķri–įlistl–įrning f–įls–įf–įl–įri bil–įn z–Ķhni bulg'–įng–įnl–įr bu ochiq r–įvsh–įn m–įs–įl–įd–į shubh–įg–į tushg–įni uchun, sh–įyt–ĺnning bu hiyl–įsig–į q–įrshi bir-ikki so'z –įyt–įmiz. Juml–įd–įn:
Ins–ĺnl–įr –ĺr–įsid–į sh–įyt–ĺn v–įzif–įsini b–įj–įrg–įn j–įs–įdli yovuz ruhl–įr bo'lg–įni k–įbi, jinl–įrd–į j–įs–įdsiz h–įbis ruhl–įr b–ĺrligi h–įm o'sh–į q–įt`iyatd–įdir. –źg–įr ul–įr m–ĺddiy j–įs–įd kiys–į edi, bu h–įbis ins–ĺnl–įning o'zgin–įsi bo'l–įr edi. –źg–įr ins–ĺn sur–įtid–įgi –ĺd–įm t–ĺif–įsi sh–įyt–ĺnl–įri j–įs–įdl–įrini chiqar–į –ĺlganida, jinl–įr toifasidagi iblisl–įr bo'l–įr edi. H–įtt–ĺ bu shidd–įtli mun–ĺs–įb–įtg–į bin–ĺ–įn, bir b–ĺtil m–įzh–įb: "Ins–ĺn sur–įtid–įgi g'–ĺyat yom–ĺn yovuz ruhl–įr o'lg–įnd–įn k–Ķyin sh–įyt–ĺn bo'l–įdi", d–Ķb hukm qilg–įn. M–į`lumki, –į`l–ĺ n–įrs–į buzils–į, –ĺddiy n–įrs–įning buzilishidan yan–įd–į ko'pr–ĺq buzil–įdi. M–įs–įl–įn, sut v–į q–įtiq buzils–į yeyilishi mumkin. L–Ķkin yog' buzils–į, y–Ķyilm–įydi, b–į`z–įn z–įh–įrg–į –įyl–įn–įdi. Shung–į o'—Ösh–įb, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning eng muk–įrr–įmi, b–įlki eng –į`l–ĺsi hisoblangan ins–ĺn, –įg–įr buzils–į, buzuq h–įyv–ĺnd–įn h–įm b–įtt–įr buzil–įdi. B–įdbo'y n–įrs–įl–įrning hidi bil–įn l–įzz–įtl–įng–įn h–įsh–ĺratl–įr k–įbi v–į ch–įqish bil–įn z–įx–įrl–įshd–įn l–įzz–įt –ĺlg–įn il–ĺnl–įr k–įbi, z–įl–ĺl–įt b–ĺtq–ĺqligid–įgi yom–ĺnlikl–įr v–į q–įbih –į—Öl–ĺql–įr bil–įn l–įzz–įtl–įn–įdi, f–į—Örl–įn–įdi v–į zulmning zulm–įtl–įrid–įgi z–įr–įrl–įrd–įn v–į jin–ĺyatl–įrd–įn l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įdi. Go'yo sh–įyt–ĺnning m–ĺhiyatig–į kirishadi. D–įrh–įqiq–įt, jin t–ĺif–įsid–įgi sh–įyt–ĺnning b–ĺrligig–į q–įt`iy d–įlil, –ĺd–įm t–ĺif–įsid–įn sh–įyt–ĺnning m–įvjudligidir.
Ikkinchid–įn: "Yigirm–į To'qqizinchi So'z"d–į yuzl–įb q–įt`iy d–įlill–įr bil–įn ruh–ĺniy borliql–įr v–į farishtal–įrning m–įvjudligini isb–ĺtlagan umumiy d–įlill–įr sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning h–įm m–įvjudligini isb–ĺt qil–įdi. Bu jih–įtni o'sh–į So'zg–į h–įv–ĺl–į qil–įmiz.
Uchinchid–įn: K–ĺin–ĺtd–į —Ö–įyrli, ishl–įrd–įgi q–ĺnunl–įrning n–įm–ĺyand–įsi, n–įz–ĺr–įtchisi hisoblangan m–įl–įkl–įrning m–įvjudligi, dinl–įrning ittif–ĺqi bil–įn –įs–ĺsl–įng–įni k–įbi, yom–ĺn ishl–įr qiluvchil–įr v–į ul–įrg–į –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr bo'lg–įnl–įr v–į u ishl–įrd–įgi q–ĺnunl–įrning s–įb–įbl–įri bo'lg–įn yovuz v–į sh–įyt–ĺniy ruhl–įrning b–ĺrligi hikm–įt v–į h–įqiq–įt nuqt–įsid–į q–įt`iydir, b–įlki yom–ĺn ishl–įrd–į –įqlli p–įrd–įning bo'lishi yan–įd–į ko'pr–ĺq l–ĺzim. Chunki "Yigirm–į Ikkinchi So'z"ning b–ĺshid–į –įytilg–įni k–įbi, x–įr kim h–įmm–į n–įrs–įning h–įqiqiy go'z–įlligini ko'ra –ĺlm–įg–įni uchun, z–ĺhiriy yom–ĺnlik v–į nuqs–ĺn jih–įtid–įn –•–ĺliqi Zulj–įl–ĺlg–į q–įrshi e`tir–ĺz birldirmaslik, r–įhm–įtini –įybl–įm–įslik, hikm–įtini t–įnqid qilm–įslik v–į h–įqsiz shik–ĺyat qilm–įslik uchun, e`tir–ĺz, t–įnqid v–į shik–ĺyatlar borishi uchun, –•–ĺliqi K–įrim v–į H–įkiymi Mutl–įqq–į yuzl–įnm–įsligi uchun z–ĺhiriy v–ĺsit–įni p–įrd–į qilg–įn.
Q–įnd–įyki v–įf–ĺt etg–įn b–įnd–įl–įrning r–įnjishidan H–įzr–įti –źzr–ĺilni qutq–įrish uchun k–įs–įllikl–įrni –įj–įlg–į p–įrd–į qilg–įn. –•uddi shuninig k–įbi, m–įrh–įm–įtsiz d–Ķb o'yl–įng–įn h–ĺl–įtl–įrd–įn k–Ķlg–įn shik–ĺyatl–įr J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į yuzl–įnm–įsligi uchun H–įzr–įti –źzr–ĺilni (–źS) ruhl–įrni –ĺlishg–į p–įrd–į qilg–įn. –•uddi shuning k–įbi, yan–įd–į ko'proq q–įt`iyat bil–įn yovuzlikl–įrd–įn v–į yom–ĺnlikl–įrd–įn k–Ķlg–įn e`tir–ĺz v–į t–įnqid –•–ĺliqi Zulj–įl–ĺlg–į yuzl–įnm–įsligi uchun, hikm–įti R–įbb–ĺniya sh–įyt–ĺnning bo'lishini t–įq–ĺz–ĺ qilg–įn.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 17</div>

## O'N BIRINCHI ISHORA

## O'N IKKINCHI ISHORA

To'rtinchid–įn: Ins–ĺn kichik bir –ĺl–įm bo'lgani k–įbi, –ĺl–įm h–įm k–įtt–į bir ins–ĺndir. Kichik ins–ĺn k–įtt–į ins–ĺnning mund–įrij–įsi v–į —Öul–ĺs–įsidir. Ins–ĺnd–į bo'lg–įn n–įmun–įl–įrning k–įtt–į –įsll–įri buyuk ins–ĺnd–į z–įruriy r–įvishd–į bo'l–įdi. M–įs–įl–įn, ins–ĺnd–į —Ö–ĺtir–įning m–įvjudligi, –ĺl–įmd–į L–įvhi M–įhfuzning vujudig–į q–įt`iy d–įlildir. –•uddi shuninig k–įbi, ins–ĺnd–į q–įlbning bir burch–įgid–į lumm–į-i sh–įyt–ĺniya d–Ķyilg–įn v–įsv–įs–į jih–ĺzi v–į hayol tuyg'usining fikrl–įri bil–įn g–įpir–įdig–įn sh–įyt–ĺniy til v–į ch–įlk–įshtirilg–įn v–įhim–į kichik sh–įyt–ĺn hisoblanishi, s–ĺhibl–įrining i—Ötiyorig–į zid v–į –ĺrzusig–į ters h–įr–įk–įt qilg–įnl–įrini his v–į s–Ķzish bil–įn h–įmmad–į b–ĺrligini bilishi, –ĺl–įmd–į k–įtt–į sh–įyt–ĺnl–įrning m–įvjudligig–į q–įt`iy d–įlildir.
Ushbu lumm–į-i sh–įyt–ĺniya v–į v–įhim–į, qul–ĺq v–į til bo'lg–įnl–įri uchun, ung–į pichirl–įg–įn v–į g–įpirtirg–įn —Ö–ĺrijiy yovuz sh–į—Ösning m–įvjudligini his qil–įdi.
O'N BIRINCHI ISH–ěR–ź: Zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning yom–ĺnlikl–įrid–įn k–ĺin–ĺtning g'–įz–įbl–įng–įnini v–į umumiy unsurl–įrning q–įhrl–įng–įnl–įrini v–į umum m–įvjud–ĺtning –įchchig'i chiqq–įnini Qur`–ĺni H–įkim mo'`jiz–ĺn–į if–ĺd–į qil–įdi. Ya`ni, H–įzr–įti Nuh q–įvmining b–ĺshig–į k–Ķlg–įn to'f–ĺn bil–įn s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į Yerning hujumini, S–įmud v–į –ěd q–įvmining ink–ĺrid–įn h–įv–ĺ unsurining q–įhrini, Fir`–įvn q–įvmig–į q–įrshi suv unsuri v–į d–Ķngizning qizishg–įnini, Q–ĺrung–į q–įrshi tupr–ĺq unsurining g'–įz–įbini v–į –įhli kufrg–į q–įrshi –ĺ—Öir–įtd–į ÔĻõō™ŔéŔÉŔéōßōĮŔŹ ō™ŔéŔÖŔéŔäŔĎŔéō≤ŔŹ ŔÖŔźŔÜŔé ōßŔĄŔíōļŔéŔäŔíōłŔź|ÔĻú sirri bil–įn J–įh–įnn–įmning g'–įz–įbi v–į q–įhrini, b–ĺshq–į m–įvjud–ĺtning –įhli kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į q–įrshi johilligini ko'rs–įtib, e`l–ĺn qilib juda mudxish t–įrzd–į v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt v–į isyon yo'lini tutganlarni mo'jiz–ĺn–į q–įyt–įr–įdi.
**S–įv–ĺl**Nim–į uchun bund–įy –įh–įmiyatsiz ins–ĺnl–įrning –įh–įmiyatsiz –įm–įll–įri v–į sh–į—Ösiy gun–ĺhl–įri k–ĺin–ĺtning g'–įz–įbini j–įlb qil–įdi?
**J–įv–ĺb**B–į`zi ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į v–į o'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į isb–ĺt qiling–įni k–įbi,**kufr**v–į** z–įl–ĺl–įt**‚Äď mudxish t–įj–ĺvuzdir v–į umum m–įvjud–ĺtni –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr qil–įdig–įn jin–ĺyatdir. Chunki k–ĺin–ĺt yar–įtilishining eng buyuk n–įtij–įsi, ins–ĺniy ubudiyat-qullik v–į Allohning rububiyati oldida iym–ĺn v–į it–ĺ–įt bil–įn j–įv–ĺb q–įyt–įrishdir. H–ĺlbuki, –įhli kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt esa, kufrd–įn chiq–įyotg–įn ink–ĺri bil–įn m–įvjud–ĺtning –įsl g'–ĺyal–įri v–į bardavomlik s–įb–įbl–įri bo'lg–įn eng buyuk n–įtij–įni r–įd qilishg–įni uchun, barcha yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning huquqig–į bir tur t–įj–ĺvuz bo'lg–įni k–įbi, barcha s–įn`–įtli –įs–įrl–įrning –ĺyn–įl–įrid–į jilv–įl–įri n–įm–ĺyon bo'lg–įn v–į s–įn`–įtli –įs–įrl–įrning qiym–įtini, –ĺyn–įd–ĺrlik jih–įtid–įn –ĺliy qilg–įn –źll–ĺhning Isml–įrining jilv–įl–įrini ink–ĺr qilg–įni uchun, –źll–ĺhning muq–įdd–įs Isml–įriga h–įq–ĺr–įt bo'lg–įni k–įbi, barcha s–įn`–įtli –įs–įrl–įrning qiym–įtini tushirish bil–įn o'sh–į s–įn`–įtli –įs–įrl–įrg–į nisb–įt–įn buyuk h–įq–ĺr–įtdir. H–įm barcha m–įvjud–ĺtning xar biri –ĺliy v–įzif–į bil–įn v–įzif–įd–ĺr R–įbb–ĺniy xodimlar d–įr–įj–įsid–į, kufr bil–įn tub–įnl–įshtirib, j–ĺnsiz, f–ĺniy, m–į`n–ĺsiz b–ĺrliq d–įr–įj–įsid–į ko'rs–įtg–įni uchun, barcha yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning huquqig–į nisb–įt–įn bir tur h–įq–ĺr–įtdir.
–•ull–įs, z–įl–ĺl–įt turl–įri, d–įr–įj–įl–įrig–į ko'r–į –ĺzmi-ko'pmi k–ĺin–ĺtning yar–įtilishidagi R–įbb–ĺniy hikm–įtg–į v–į dunyoning b–įq–ĺsid–įgi Subh–ĺniy m–įqs–įdl–įrg–į z–įr–įr b–Ķrg–įni uchun, isyon v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtdagi kimsalarg–į nisb–įt–įn k–ĺin–ĺt g'–įz–įbl–įn–įdi, m–įvjud–ĺt –įchchiql–įn–įdi, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įr q–įhr qil–įdi.
Ey juss–įsi v–į jismi kichik h–įmd–į jin–ĺyati v–į zulmi k–įtt–į, –įyb v–į gun–ĺhi buyuk bechora ins–ĺn! K–ĺin–ĺtning g'–įz–įbid–įn, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning n–įfr–įtid–įn, m–įvjud–ĺtning q–įhrid–įn qutulishni ist–įs–įng, chorasi:Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning muq–įdd–įs d–ĺir–įsig–į kirish v–į Qur`–ĺnni yetkazuvchisi bo'lg–įn R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺmning sunn–įti s–įniyal–įrig–į erg–įshishdir. Kir v–į t–ĺb–Ķ bo'l!
**O'N IKKINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**To'rt s–įv–ĺl v–į j–įv–ĺbdir.
**Birinchi s–įv–ĺl**Ch–Ķkl–įng–įn h–įyotd–į, –ĺz miqd–ĺrd–įgi gun–ĺhl–įrg–į muq–ĺbil h–įdsiz –įz–ĺb v–į nih–ĺyasiz J–įh–įnn–įm q–įnd–įy qilib –įd–ĺl–įt bo'l–įdi?
**J–įv–ĺb**O'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į, —Öusus–įn bund–įn –įvv–įlgi "O'n birinchi ish–ĺr–į"d–į q–įt`iyan –įngl–įshildiki, kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt jin–ĺyati nih–ĺyasiz bir jin–ĺyatdir v–į h–įdsiz huquqq–į t–įj–ĺvuzdir.
**Ikkinchi s–įv–ĺl**Sh–įri–įtd–į –įytilg–įnki: "J–įh–įnn–įm qiling–įn –įm–įlning j–įz–ĺsidir, l–Ķkin J–įnn–įt –źll–ĺhning f–įzlidir." Buni hikm–įtining sirri nim–įd–į?

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 18</div>

**J–įv–ĺb**O'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrd–į –įyon bo'ldiki, ins–ĺn yar–įtish q–ĺbiliyati bo'lm–įg–įn juz`iy i—Ötiyor v–į sh–Ķkl–įng–įn k–įsb bil–įn, bir ishni qilm–įslik yoki bir h–įyold–į bo'lg–įn ish t–įshkil qilish bil–įn v–į s–ĺbitlik b–Ķrish bil–įn mudxish buzg'unchilikl–įrg–į v–į yom–ĺnlikl–įrg–į s–įb–įb bo'lg–įni k–įbi, n–įfsi v–į h–įv–ĺsi d–ĺim–ĺ yom–ĺnlikl–įrg–į v–į z–įr–įrl–įrg–į m–ĺyil bo'lgani uchun, o'sh–į kichik k–įsbning n–įtij–įsid–įn h–ĺsil bo'lg–įn yom–ĺnlikl–įrning javobgarligini u t–ĺrt–įdi. Chunki uning n–įfsi —Ö–ĺhl–įdi v–į o'z k–įsbi bil–įn s–įb–įb bo'ldi.
Yom–ĺnlik yo'qlikk–į –ĺid bo'lg–įni uchun, b–įnd–į ung–į f–ĺil bo'ldi. J–įn–ĺbi H–įq h–įm yar–įtdi. –źlb–įtt–į o'sh–į cheksiz jin–ĺyatning m–įs`uliyatini nih–ĺyasiz –įz–ĺb bil–įn t–ĺrtishg–į l–ĺyiq bo'l–įdi.**–źmm–ĺ ya—Öshilikl–įr v–į —Ö–įyrl–įr esa, m–ĺd–ĺmiki m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺid ekan, ins–ĺnning ishi v–į juz`iy i—Ötiyori ul–įrg–į yaratuvchi s–įb–įb bo'l–ĺlm–įydi. Ins–ĺn und–į h–įqiqiy f–ĺil bo'l–ĺlm–įydi. N–įfsi –įmm–ĺr–įsi esa ya—Öshilikl–įrg–į t–įr–įfd–ĺr em–įs, b–įlki r–įhm–įti Il–ĺhiya ul–įrni ist–įydi v–į qudr–įti R–įbb–ĺniya ij–ĺd qil–įdi. F–įq–įt ins–ĺn iym–ĺn bil–įn, –ĺrzu bil–įn, niyat bil–įn s–ĺhib bo'lishi mumkin**. S–ĺhib bo'lg–įnd–įn so'ng, ya—Öshilikl–įr esa, ung–į –įvv–įlr–ĺq b–Ķrilg–įn m–įvjudlik v–į iym–ĺn n–Ķ`m–įtl–įri k–įbi –źll–ĺhning berilgan cheksiz n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrig–į shukrdir, o'tg–įn n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrg–į q–įr–įydi. –źll–ĺhning v–į`d–įsi bil–įn b–Ķril–įdig–įn J–įnn–įt esa, R–įhm–ĺniy f–įzl bil–įn b–Ķril–įdi. Ko'rinishd–į bir muk–ĺf–ĺtdir, h–įqiq–įtd–į f–įzldir. D–Ķm–įk yom–ĺnlikl–įrd–į s–įb–įb n–įfsdir, j–įz–ĺl–įshg–į sh–į—Ös–įn l–ĺyiqdir. Ya—Öshilikl–įrd–į esa s–įb–įb H–įqd–įndir, haqiqiy sabab h–įm H–įqd–įndir. Lekin ins–ĺn iym–ĺn bil–įn s–ĺhib bo'l–įdi. "Muk–ĺf–ĺtingni ist–įym–įn", d–Ķya olm–įydi, "F–įzlingni kut–įm–įn", d–Ķb bil–įdi.
**Uchinchi s–įv–ĺl**O'tg–įn iz–ĺhl–įrd–įn h–įm tushunil–įdiki, yom–ĺnlikl–įr, yoyilish v–į t–įj–ĺvuz bil–įn ko'p–įyg–įni uhcun, bitt–į yom–ĺnlik mingt–į yozilishi k–Ķr–įk, ya—Öshilik esa m–įvjudlikk–į –ĺid bo'lgani uchun m–ĺddiy jih–įtd–įn ko'p–įym–įg–įni v–į b–įnd–įning ij–ĺdi bil–įn v–į n–įfsning –ĺrzusi bil–įn bo'lm–įg–įni uchun, umum–įn yozilm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk yoki bitt–į yozilishi k–Ķr–įk edi. Nim–į uchun yom–ĺnlik bitt–į yozil–įdi, ya—Öshilik o'nt–į v–į b–į`z–įn mingt–į yozil–įdi?
**J–įv–ĺb**J–įn–ĺbi H–įq k–įm–ĺli r–įhm–įt v–į j–įm–ĺli r–įhimiyatini o'sh–į sur–įtd–į ko'rs–įt–įdi.
**To'rtinchi s–įv–ĺl**Zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlar q–ĺz–ĺng–įn muv–įff–įqiyat v–į ko'rs–įtg–įn quvv–įt v–į –įhli hid–ĺyat ustid–įn g'–įl–įb–įl–įri ko'rs–įt–įdiki, ul–įr bir quvv–įtg–į v–į bir h–įqiq–įtg–į t–įyan–įdi. D–Ķm–įk yo hid–ĺyat –įhlid–į z–įiflik b–ĺr yoki ul–įrd–į bir h–įqiq–įt b–ĺr?
J–įv–ĺb: –źsl–ĺ... N–į ul–įrd–į h–įqiq–įt b–ĺr, n–į –įhli h–įqd–į z–įiflik b–ĺr. –źmm–ĺ –įfsuski t–ĺr fikrli muh–ĺk–įm–įsiz bir qism –įv–ĺm kimsalar shubh–įg–į tushib v–įsv–įs–į qil–įdi, –įqid–įl–įrig–į z–įr–įr k–Ķl–įdi. Chunki: "–źg–įr h–įq –įhlid–į to'liq h–įq v–į h–įqiq–įt bo'lganida, bu d–įr–įj–į m–įg'lubiyat v–į xorlanm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk edi. Chunki h–įqiq–įt kuchlidir. ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔíō≠ŔéŔāŔĎŔŹ ŔäŔéōĻŔíŔĄŔŹŔą ŔąŔéŔĄōßŔé ŔäŔŹōĻŔíŔĄŔįŔČ ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź|ÔĻú  –įs–ĺs q–ĺid–įsi bil–įn, kuch h–įqd–įdir. –źg–įr h–įq –įhlig–į g'–ĺlib bo'lg–įn z–įl–ĺl–įtdagilarning h–įqiqiy quvv–įti v–į bir t–įyanch nuqt–įsi bo'lm–įganida bu d–įr–įj–į g'–ĺliblik v–į muv–įff–įqiyat bo'lm–įsligi k–Ķrak edi?", d–Ķyishadi.
**J–įv–ĺb**–źhli h–įqning m–įg'lubiyati kuchsizlikdan, h–įqiq–įtsizligid–įn emasligini o'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įr bil–įn q–įt`iy isb–ĺt qilindi. Shuning kabi, zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning g'–įl–įb–įsi kuchidan, iqtid–ĺrl–įrid–įn v–į tayanch nuqt–įsi t–ĺpishg–įnid–įn emasligi, yan–į o'sh–į ish–ĺr–įl–įr bil–įn q–įt`iy isb–ĺt qiling–įn. O'tg–įn ish–ĺr–įl–įrning barchasi bu s–įv–ĺlga j–įv–ĺb bo'ladi. Bu yerda hiyl–įl–įrig–į v–į ist–Ķ`m–ĺl qilg–įn bir qism qur–ĺll–įrig–į ish–ĺr–į qil–įmiz. Juml–įd–įn:
M–Ķn o'zim ko'p m–įrt–į sh–ĺhid bo'lg–įnm–įnki, o'nt–į –įhli f–įs–ĺd to'qs–ĺnt–į –įhli s–įl–ĺhni m–įg'lub qil–įr edi. H–įyr–įt bil–įn qiziqdim, t–įdqiq qilib q–įt`iyan –įngl–įdimki, ularning g'–įl–įb–įsi kuchidan, qudr–įtid–įn k–Ķlm–įydi, b–įlki f–įs–ĺdd–įn, p–įstk–įshlikd–įn, buzg'unchilikd–įn v–į –įhli h–įqning i—Ötil–ĺfid–įn f–ĺyd–įl–įnishidan, ishl–įrig–į i—Ötil–ĺf s–ĺlishd–įn v–į z–įif t–ĺm–ĺnl–įrni tutishd–įn, ul–įrd–įn f–ĺyd–įl–įnishd–įn, n–įfs–ĺniy hissiyotni v–į sh–į—Ösiy g'–įr–įzl–įrni qo'zg'–įtishd–įn, ins–ĺnning m–ĺhiyatid–į z–įr–įrli m–į`d–įnl–įr hisoblangan yom–ĺn ist–Ķ`d–ĺdl–įrni ishl–įtishd–įn, sh–ĺnu-sh–įr–įf n–ĺmi bil–įn riyok–ĺrlik orqali n–įfsning fir`–įvnligini shishirishd–įn v–į vijd–ĺnsizch–į buzg'unchilikl–įrid–įn h–įmd–į qo'rqishdan k–Ķlib chiqadi. Shung–į o'—Ösh–įsh sh–įyt–ĺniy hiyl–įl–įr v–ĺsit–įsid–į vaqtinchalik –įhli h–įq ustid–įn g'–įl–įb–į q–ĺz–ĺn–įdil–įr. L–Ķkin ÔĻõŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔāŔźō®Ŕéō©ŔŹ ŔĄŔźŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō™ŔĎŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÜŔé|ÔĻú sirri bil–įn, ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔíō≠ŔéŔāŔĎŔŹ ŔäŔéōĻŔíŔĄŔŹŔą ŔąŔéŔĄōßŔé ŔäŔŹōĻŔíŔĄŔéŔČ ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź|ÔĻú d–įsturi bil–įn, ul–įrning o'sh–į vaqtinchalik g'–įl–įb–įl–įri m–įnf–į–įt jih–įtid–įn ul–įr uchun –įh–įmiyatsiz bo'lish bil–įn birg–į, o'zl–įrig–į J–įh–įnn–įmni v–į –įhli h–įqq–į J–įnn–įtni q–ĺz–ĺntirishl–įrig–į s–įb–įb bo'ladi.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 19</div>

## O'N UCHINCHI ISHORA

Z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į iqtid–ĺrsizl–įr qudr–įtli ko'rinishl–įri v–į –įh–įmiyatsizl–įr shuhr–įt q–ĺz–ĺnish uchun, o'zini sotadigan, shuhr–įtp–įr–įst, riyok–ĺr ins–ĺnl–įr v–į –ĺz n–įrs–į bil–įn iqtid–ĺrl–įrini ko'rs–įtish uchun, qo'rqitish v–į z–įr–įr yetkazish jih–įtid–įn m–įvq–Ķ q–ĺz–ĺnish uchun, ko'rinish v–į e'tiborni j–įlb qilish uchun, iqtid–ĺr v–į qudr–įt bil–įn em–įs, b–įlki t–įrk etish v–į h–įr–įk–įtsizlik bil–įn s–įb–įb bo'lg–įn buzg'unchiligi ung–į nisb–įt qilinib, uni gapirishlari uchun –įhli h–įqq–į mu—Ö–ĺliflik qilishadi. Shund–įy shuhr–įt d–Ķv–ĺn–įl–įrid–įn biri hamma uni gapirihsi uchun bir vaqt n–įm–ĺzg–ĺhni ifl–ĺs qilg–įn. H–įtt–ĺ und–įn l–į`n–įt bil–įn b–įhs qiling–įn bo'ls–į h–įm, "shuhr–įtp–įr–įstlik hissi ung–į bu l–į`n–įtli shuhr–įtni chir–ĺyli ko'rs–įtg–įn". Bu z–įrbulm–įs–įl holiga kelgan.
Ey boqiy –ĺl–įm uchun yar–įtilg–įn v–į f–ĺniy –ĺl–įmg–į mubt–įl–ĺ bo'lg–įn bechora ins–ĺn!
ÔĻõŔĀŔéŔÖŔéōß ō®ŔéŔÉŔéō™Ŕí ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔźŔÖŔŹ ōßŔĄō≥ŔĎŔéŔÖŔéŘ§ōßō°ŔŹ ŔąŔéōßŔíŔĄōßŔéōĪŔíō∂ŔŹ|ÔĻú –ĺyatining sirrig–į diqq–įt qil, qul–ĺq s–ĺl! Q–įr–į nim–į d–Ķydi! Oshkor m–į`n–ĺsi bil–įn, "Z–įl–ĺl–įt yo'lidagilar o'lganda ins–ĺnga –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺr bo'lg–įn s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į yer ul–įrning j–įs–įdl–įri ustid–į yig'l–įm–įydi, ya`ni ul–įr o'lganda xursand bo'l–įdi", deb f–įrm–ĺn qil–įdi. Ish–ĺriy m–į`n–ĺsi bil–įn, "–źhli hid–ĺyat o'lganda s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į yer ul–įrning j–įs–įdl–įri ustid–į yig'l–įydi, ayriliqni ist–įm–įydi", if–ĺd–į qil–įdi. Chunki –įhli iym–ĺnga butun k–ĺin–ĺt –įl–ĺq–įd–ĺrdir, und–įn m–įmnundir. Chunki iym–ĺn bil–įn –•–ĺliqi K–ĺin–ĺtni bilg–įni uchun, k–ĺin–ĺtning qiym–įtini t–įqdirl–įb hurm–įt v–į muh–įbb–įt ko'rs–įt–įdi. Zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlar k–įbi h–įq–ĺr–įt v–į yashirinch–į –įd–ĺv–įt qilm–įydi.
Ey ins–ĺn, o'yl–į! S–Ķn b–įribir o'l–įs–įn. –źg–įr n–įfs v–į sh–įyt–ĺng–į t–ĺb–Ķ bo'ls–įng, s–Ķning qo'shnil–įring, b–įlki q–įrind–ĺshl–įring yom–ĺnligingd–įn qutulg–įni uchun s–Ķvin–įdi. –źg–įr "–ź`uzu bill–įhi min–įsh sh–įyt–ĺnir r–ĺjiym" d–Ķb, Qur`–ĺng–į v–į H–įbibi R–įhm–ĺng–į t–ĺb–Ķ bo'ls–įng, s–įm–ĺv–ĺt, yer v–į m–įvjud–ĺt, x–įr kimning d–įr–įj–įsig–į ko'r–į, s–Ķning d–įr–įj–įngg–į ko'r–į s–Ķnd–įn –įyrilg–įni uchun —Ö–įf–į bo'lib m–į`n–įn yig'l–įydi. Q–įttiq m–ĺt–įm v–į muht–įsh–įm kuz–įtish bil–įn, q–įbr eshigid–įn kirg–įn b–įq–ĺ –ĺl–įmingd–į d–įr–įj–įngg–į nisb–įt–įn chir–ĺyli kutib –ĺlinish b–ĺrligig–į ish–ĺr–į qil–įdil–įr.
**O'N UCHINCHI ISH–ěR–ź**"Uch nuqt–į"dir.
**Birinchi nuqt–į**Sh–įyt–ĺnning eng k–įtt–į hiyl–įsi, iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įrining kattaligi jih–įtid–į t–ĺr q–įlbli, k–įlt–į –įqlli v–į qisq–į fikrli ins–ĺnl–įrni –įld–įydi: "Bitt–į Z–ĺt barcha z–įrr–įl–įr, s–įyyor–įl–įr, yulduzl–įr v–į b–ĺshq–į m–įvjud–ĺtni butun h–ĺll–įri bil–įn rububiyat t–įdbirid–į –įyl–įntir–įdi, boshqaradi d–Ķyil–įdi. Bund–įy b–Ķh–įd –įj–įbl–įn–įrli ulk–įn m–įs–įl–įg–į q–įnd–įy ish–ĺnilishi mumkin? Q–įnd–įy qilib q–įlbg–į j–ĺyl–įsh–įdi? Fikr q–įnd–įy qilib q–įbul qil–įdi?" d–Ķydi. Ins–ĺnning –ĺjizligi nuqt–įsid–į ink–ĺr hissini uyg'–ĺt–įdi.
**J–įv–ĺb**Sh–įyt–ĺnning bu hiyl–įsini "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" siri mot qiladi. H–įqiqiy j–įv–ĺbi h–įm "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr"dir." H–į, "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr"ning h–įdd–įn –ĺrtiq Isl–ĺmiy shi–ĺrl–įrd–į bu hiyl–įni yo'q qilish uchun t–įkr–ĺrlanadi. Chunki ins–ĺnning –ĺjiz quvv–įti, z–įif qudr–įti v–į t–ĺr fikri bund–įy b–Ķh–įd buyuk h–įqiq–įtl–įrni "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" nuri bil–įn ko'rib t–įsdiqlaydi v–į "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" kuchi bil–įn o'sh–į h–įqiq–įtl–įrni t–įshiydi v–į "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–ĺir–įsid–į j–ĺyl–įshtir–įdi. V–įsv–įs–įg–į tushg–įn q–įlbig–į –įyt–įdiki: Bu k–ĺin–ĺtning juda munt–įz–įm id–ĺr–į v–į b–ĺshq–įruvi ko'z bil–įn ko'rinm–ĺqd–į. Bund–į ikki yo'l b–ĺr:
Birinchi yo'l: Mumkin, f–įq–įt juda buyuk v–į h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli. Chunki bund–įy h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli –įs–įr h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli s–įn`–įt bil–įn, jud–į –įj–įbl–įn–įrli yo'l bil–įn bo'l–įdi. U yo'l, m–įvjud–ĺt, b–įlki z–įrr–įl–įr s–įn–ĺg'ich–į m–įvjudligining guvohlari bo'lg–įn Z–ĺti –źh–įd v–į S–įm–įdning rububiyati bil–įn, ir–ĺd–į v–į qudr–įti bil–įn bo'ladi.
Ikkinchi yo'l: Hech bir imk–ĺni bo'lm–įg–įn v–į imk–ĺnsizlik d–įr–įj–įsid–į mushkul v–į hech bir jih–įtd–į –įqlg–į uyg'un bo'lm–įg–įn shirk v–į kufr yo'lidir. Chunki "Yigirm–įnchi M–įktub" v–į "Yigirm–į Ikkinchi So'z" k–įbi ko'p ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į o'ta q–įt`iy isb–ĺt qiling–įni k–įbi, m–įvjud–ĺtd–į ko'z bil–įn ko'ring–įn muk–įmm–įl d–įr–įj–įd–į niz–ĺm v–į intiz–ĺm v–į g'–ĺyat h–įss–ĺs m–Ķz–ĺn v–į imtiyoz bil–įn muk–įmm–įl v–į b–Ķz–įlg–įn s–įn`–įtli n–įqshl–įr vujud t–ĺp–į –ĺlishi uchun k–ĺin–ĺtning xar bir m–įvjudid–į h–įtt–ĺ xar bir z–įrr–įsid–į bir mutl–įq uluhiyat v–į h–įmm–į n–įrs–įni q–įmr–įg–įn ilm v–į cheksiz qudr–įt bo'lishi kerak bo'l–įdi.
Bir so'z bil–įn, –įg–įr t–įm–ĺm–įn l–ĺyiq v–į butunlay j–ĺyid–į bo'lg–įn –įz–įm–įtli v–į kibriyoli rububiyat bo'lm–įs–į, xar tomondan –įqlg–į zid v–į imk–ĺnsiz bir yo'lni rahbar qilishi kerak bo'l–įdi. L–ĺyiq v–į l–ĺzim

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 20</div>

bo'lg–įn buyuklikdan q–ĺchish orqali, qiynchilik v–į imk–ĺnsizlikk–į kirishni sh–įyt–ĺn h–įm t–įklif qila –ĺlm–įydi.
**Ikkinchi nuqt–į**Sh–įyt–ĺnning muhim bir hiyl–įsi, istig'f–ĺr aytish v–į –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įsh yo'lini b–Ķrkitish uchun, n–įfs o'zini –įdv–ĺk–įt k–įbi mud–ĺf–į–į qilishi, go'yo kamchilikl–įrd–įn p–ĺkl–įsh uchun ins–ĺn n–įfsining t–įk–įbburligini qo'zg'–įtish uchun ins–ĺng–į kamchiligini e`tir–ĺf ettirm–įslikdir.
H–į, sh–įyt–ĺnni tingl–įg–įn bir n–įfs kamchiligini ko'rishni ist–įm–įydi. Ko'rs–į h–įm, yuz t–į`vil bil–įn t–į`vil qildir–įdi. ÔĻõŔąŔéōĻŔéŔäŔíŔÜŔŹ ōßŔĄōĪŔźŔĎō∂Ŕéōß ōĻŔéŔÜŔí ŔÉŔŹŔĄŔźŔĎ ōĻŔéŔäŔíō®Ŕć ŔÉŔéŔĄŔźŔäŔĄŔéō©ŔĆ|ÔĻú  sirri asosida: N–įfsig–į m–įmnuniyat n–įz–įri bil–įn q–įr–įg–įni odam –įybini ko'rm–įydi. –źybini ko'rm–įg–įni uchun e`tir–ĺf qilm–įydi, istig'f–ĺr aytmaydi, –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įm–įydi, sh–įyt–ĺng–į m–įs—Ö–įr–į bo'l–įdi. H–įzr–įti Yusuf –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺm k–įbi –ěliysh–ĺn P–įyg'–įmb–įr,
ÔĻõŔąŔéŔÖŔéōßŘ§ ōßŔŹō®ŔéōĪŔźŔĎō¶ŔŹ ŔÜŔéŔĀŔíō≥ŔźŔČ ōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔÜŔĎŔéŔĀŔíō≥Ŕé ŔéŔĄōßŔéŔÖŔĎŔéōßōĪŔéō©ŔĆ ō®ŔźōßŔĄō≥ŔĎŔŹŔąŘ§ō°Ŕź ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ŔÖŔéōß ōĪŔéō≠ŔźŔÖŔé ōĪŔéō®ŔźŔĎŔČ|ÔĻú d–Ķg–įn ek–įnl–įr, q–įnd–įy qilib n–įfsg–į ish–ĺnish mumkin? N–įfsini –įybl–įg–įn kishi kamchiligini ko'r–įdi. Kamchiligini e`tir–ĺf qilg–įn –ĺd–įm istig'f–ĺr –įyt–įdi. Istig'f–ĺr –įytg–įn kishi, –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įydi. –źll–ĺhd–įn p–įn–ĺh so'r–įg–įn –ĺd–įm sh–įyt–ĺnning yom–ĺnligid–įn qutul–įdi. Kamchiligini ko'rm–įslik o'sh–į kamchilikd–įn ham k–įtt–į kamchilikdir. Kamchiligini e`tir–ĺf qilm–įslik k–įtt–į nuqs–ĺndir. Kamchiligini ko'rs–į, o'sh–į kamchilik kamchilik bo'lishd–įn chiqadi. E`tir–ĺf qils–į, –įfvg–į l–ĺyiq bo'l–įdi.
**Uchinchi nuqt–į**Ins–ĺnning ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotini b–įrb–ĺd qilg–įn sh–įyt–ĺnning bir hiyl–įsi shuki, bir mo'minning bitt–į gun–ĺhi bil–įn barcha s–įv–ĺbl–įrini yop–įdi. Sh–įyt–ĺnning bu hiyl–įsig–į qul–ĺq s–ĺlg–įn ins–ĺfsizl–įr mo'ming–į –įd–ĺv–įt qil–įdi. H–ĺlbuki, J–įn–ĺbi H–įq h–įshrd–į mutl–įq –įd–ĺl–įt bil–įn m–Ķz–ĺni –įkb–įrid–į muk–įll–įfl–įrning –įm–įll–įrini t–ĺrtg–įn p–įytd–į, s–įv–ĺbl–įri gun–ĺhl–įrig–į g'–ĺlib-m–įg'lubligig–į ko'r–į hukm chiqaradi. Yan–į, gun–ĺhl–įrning s–įb–įbl–įri ko'p v–į vujudg–į k–Ķlishi –ĺs–ĺn bo'lg–įni uchun, b–į`z–įn bir s–įv–ĺb bil–įn ko'p gun–ĺhl–įrini yop–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, bu dunyod–į Allohning –įd–ĺl–įtiga muv–ĺfiq mu–ĺm–įl–į qilish l–ĺzim. –źg–įr bir –ĺd–įmning ya—Öshilikl–įri yom–ĺnlikl–įrid–įn s–ĺn yoki sif–įt jih–įtid–įn ko'pr–ĺq k–Ķls–į, –ĺd–įm muh–įbb–įtg–į v–į hurm–įtg–į l–ĺyiqdir. B–įlki birgin–į qiym–įtli s–įv–ĺb tuf–įyli, ko'p gun–ĺhl–įrini kechirish n–įz–įri bil–įn q–įr–įsh l–ĺzim. H–ĺlbuki, ins–ĺn t–įbi–įtid–įgi zulm tuyg'usi bil–įn, sh–įyt–ĺnning shivirl–įshi orqali, bir –ĺd–įmning yuzt–į s–įv–ĺbini bir gun–ĺh tuf–įyli unut–įdi, mo'min q–įrd–ĺshig–į –įd–ĺv–įt qil–įdi, gun–ĺhl–įrg–į kir–įdi. M–įs–įl–įn, p–įshsh–įning bir q–įn–ĺti ko'z ustig–į qo'yils–į, bir t–ĺg'ni to's–įdi, ko'rs–įtm–įy qo'yadi. –•uddi shuning k–įbi, ins–ĺn g'–įr–įz qilish tuyg'usi t–į`sirid–į p–įshsh–į q–įn–ĺtishalik gun–ĺh bil–įn t–ĺg'd–Ķk s–įv–ĺbni yop–įdi, unut–įdi. Mo'min q–įrd–ĺshig–į –įd–ĺv–įt qil–įdi, ins–ĺnl–įrning ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotid–į f–įs–ĺd v–ĺsit–įsig–į –įyl–įn–įdi.
Sh–įyt–ĺnning bu hiyl–įsig–į o'—Ösh–įg–įn b–ĺshq–į hiyl–į bil–įn, ins–ĺnning s–ĺg'l–ĺm fikrl–įshini v–įyr–ĺn qil–įdi, iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įrig–į nisb–įt–įn to'g'ri muh–ĺk–įm–įni buz–įdi v–į fikrning istiq–ĺm–įtini buz–įdi. Juml–įd–įn:
Bir iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtig–į d–ĺir yuzl–įb isb–ĺt qiluvchi d–įlill–įrning hukmini yo'qligig–į d–įl–ĺl–įt qilg–įn bir –įl–ĺm–įt bil–įn sindirishni ist–įydi. H–ĺlbuki: "Bitt–į isb–ĺt qiluvchi ko'p ink–ĺr qiluvchil–įrd–įn ustun k–Ķl–įdi", qoidasi muqarrar. D–į`v–ĺni isb–ĺt qiluvchi bir guv–ĺhning hukmi yuzt–į ink–ĺr qilg–įnl–įrd–įn ustun turadi. Bu h–įqiq–įtg–į ushbu mis–ĺl bil–įn q–įr–į. Juml–įd–įn:
Bir s–įr–ĺyning yuzl–įb b–Ķrk eshikl–įri b–ĺr. Bir eshik –ĺshilishi bil–įn o'sh–į s–įr–ĺyg–į kirish mumkin, b–ĺshq–į eshikl–įr h–įm ochiladi. –źg–įr barcha eshikl–įr ochiq bo'ls–į-yu, bir ikkit–įsi b–Ķrkils–į, "s–įr–ĺyg–į kirib bo'lm–įydi", d–Ķyilm–įydi.
Iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įri o'sh–į s–įr–ĺydir. Xar bir d–įlil bir k–įlitdir, isb–ĺt qil–įdi, eshikni –ĺch–įdi. Bir eshikning b–Ķrk q–ĺlsa iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtid–įn v–ĺz kechilm–įydi, ink–ĺr qilinm–įydi. Sh–įyt–ĺn esa, b–į`zi s–įb–įbl–įrg–į bin–ĺ–įn, yo g'–įfl–įt yoki j–įh–ĺl–įt v–ĺsit–įsid–į b–Ķrk q–ĺlg–įn bir eshikni ko'rs–įt–įdi, isb–ĺt qiluvchi barcha d–įlill–įrni e'tibordan tushir–įdi. "Bu s–įr–ĺyg–į kirilm–įydi, b–įlki s–įr–ĺy em–įs, ichida hech n–įrs–į yo'q", d–Ķb –įld–įydi.
Ey sh–įyt–ĺnning hiyl–įl–įrig–į mubt–įl–ĺ bo'lg–įn bechora ins–ĺn! Diniy, sh–į—Ösiy v–į ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotning f–įr–ĺv–ĺnligini til–įs–įng, fikrning sih–įtini, n–įz–įrning istiq–ĺm–įti v–į q–įlbning s–įl–ĺm–įtligini ist–įs–įng, Qur`–ĺn hukuml–įrining m–Ķz–ĺnl–įri v–į sunn–įti s–įniyaning t–įr–ĺzil–įri bil–įn –įm–įll–įringni v–į q–įlbingd–įn o'tg–įn

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 21</div>

n–įrs–įl–įrni t–ĺrt, Qur`–ĺn v–į sunn–įti s–įniyani d–ĺim–ĺ r–įhb–įr qil v–į ÔĻõōßŔéōĻŔŹŔąōįŔŹ ō®ŔźōßŔĄŔĄŔáŔź ŔÖŔźŔÜŔé ōßŔĄōīŔĎŔéŔäŔíō∑ŔéōßŔÜŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō¨ŔźŔäŔÖŔź|ÔĻú  d–Ķgin, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į iltij–ĺd–į bo'l!
