## O'n Yettinchi Yog'du

## BIRINCHI MULOHAZA

## IKKINCHI MULOHAZA

## UCHINCHI MULOHAZA

O'n Yettinchi Yog'du

### ("Zuhr–į"d–įn k–Ķlg–įn "O'n B–Ķsh Mul–ĺh–įz–į"d–įn ib–ĺr–įt)

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ō®Ŕźō≥ŔíŔÖŔź ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠ŔíŔÖŔįŔÜŔź ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≠ŔźŔäŔÖŔź</div>

MUQ–źDDIM–ź
O'n ikki yil –įvv–įl**(\*)‚ąę O'n ikki yil avval deyilgan sana, hijriy 1340, milodiy 1921 yillaridir**R–įbb–ĺniy in–ĺyat bil–įn Allohning m–į`rif–įtida fikriy h–įr–įk–įtda, q–įlbiy s–įyoh–įt v–į ruhiy yuks–įlishl–įrd–į n–įm–ĺyon bo'lg–įn b–į`zi t–įvhid yog'dul–įrini –įr–įb tilida "Mul–ĺh–įz–įl–įr" sur–įtid–į "Zuhr–į", "Shu`l–į", "Urug'", "Sh–įmm–į", "Z–įrr–į", "Tomchi" k–įbi ris–ĺl–įl–įrd–į q–įyd qilg–įn edim. Uzun h–įqiq–įtning f–įq–įt bir uchini ko'rs–įtish v–į p–ĺrl–ĺq nurning f–įq–įt bir shu`l–įsini n–įm–ĺyon qilish t–įrzid–į yozilg–įni b–ĺis, f–įq–įt o'zim uchun bir —Ö–ĺtir–į v–į bir esl–įtm–į sh–įklid–į bo'lg–įni uchun, b–ĺshq–įl–įrning tushunishi ch–Ķkl–įng–įn edi. –•usus–įn, eng s–įr–į v–į eng yaqin q–įrd–ĺshl–įrimning –įks–įriyati –įr–įbch–į o'qim–įg–įn. Ul–įrning q–įttiq iltim–ĺsi v–į qist–ĺvi bil–įn o'sh–į mul–ĺh–įz–įl–įrning, yog'dul–įrning qism–įn iz–ĺhli v–į qism–įn qisq–į m–į`n–ĺsini turkch–įd–į yozishg–į m–įjbur bo'ldim. Shu mul–ĺh–įz–įl–įr v–į arabcha ris–ĺl–įl–įr Yangi S–įidning eng –įvv–įl h–įqiq–įt ilmid–įn bir d–įr–įj–į sh–ĺhid bo'lish sur–įtid–į ko'rg–įni uchun o'zg–įrtirilm–įsd–įn m–į`n–ĺl–įri yozildi. Shuning uchun b–į`zi juml–įl–įr b–ĺshq–į "So'zl–įr"d–į h–įm zikr qilinish bil–įn birg–į, bu yerda h–įm zikr qilin–įdi. Bir qismi siqilg–įn bo'lishi bil–įn birg–į, –įsliy l–įt–ĺf–įtini yo'q–ĺtm–įsligi iz–ĺhlanm–įydi.
**BIRINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**O'z n–įfsimg–į —Öit–ĺb–įn, "Ey g'–ĺfil S–įid! Bilginki:
‚ÄĘ Shu –ĺl–įmning f–įn–ĺsid–įn so'ng s–Ķng–į h–įmr–ĺhlik qilm–įg–įn,
‚ÄĘ dunyoning —Ö–įr–ĺb bo'lg–įnid–įn k–Ķyin, s–Ķnd–įn –įyrilg–įn n–įrs–įg–į q–įlbingni b–ĺg'l–įsh s–Ķng–į l–ĺyiq em–įs.
‚ÄĘ –•usus–įn s–Ķning –įsringning inqir–ĺzi orqali s–Ķni t–įrk etib yuz o'girg–įn,
‚ÄĘ –įyniqs–į b–įrz–ĺh s–įf–įrid–į yo'ld–ĺsh bo'lm–įg–įn,
‚ÄĘ —Öusus–įn s–Ķni q–įbr eshigig–į q–įd–įr kuz–įtib qo'ym–įg–įn,
‚ÄĘ —Öusus–įn bir-ikki yil m–ĺb–įynid–į –įb–įdiy fir–ĺq bil–įn s–Ķnd–įn –įyrilib gun–ĺhini s–Ķning bo'yningg–į yuklagan,
‚ÄĘ —Öusus–įn s–Ķng–į —Öil–ĺf r–įvishd–į h–ĺsil bo'lish p–įytid–į s–Ķni t–įrk etgan f–ĺniy n–įrs–įl–įrga q–įlbingni b–ĺg'l–įsh –įqlg–į muv–ĺfiq ish em–įs.
–źg–įr –įqling bo'ls–į, –ĺhir–įtig–į –ĺid inqil–ĺbl–įringd–į, b–įrz–į—Öiy h–ĺll–įringd–į v–į dunyoviy inqil–ĺbl–įringning to'qn–įshuvl–įri –ĺstid–į ezilg–įn, buzilg–įn v–į –įb–įdiy s–įf–įrd–į s–Ķng–į yo'ld–ĺsh bo'lishg–į iqtid–ĺri bo'lm–įg–įn ishl–įrni t–įshl–į, –įh–įmiyat b–Ķrm–į, ul–įrning z–įv–ĺl topishid–įn q–įyg'urm–į. S–Ķn o'z m–ĺhiyatingg–į q–įr–į, n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įring ichida shund–įylari b–ĺrki, –įb–įdd–įn v–į –įb–įdiy Z–ĺtd–įn b–ĺshq–įsig–į r–ĺzi em–įs. Und–įn b–ĺshq–įsig–į yuzl–įnm–įydi, yar–įtilg–įn –įs–įrl–įrig–į yuzlanib o'zini —Öo'rl–įm–įydi. Ung–į butun dunyoni b–Ķrs–įng h–įm, o'sh–į t–įbiiy ehtiyojni q–ĺndira –ĺlm–įydi. U n–įrs–į, s–Ķning hisl–įringning v–į n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įringning sult–ĺnidir. F–ĺtiri H–įkiymning –įmrig–į it–ĺ–įtk–ĺr sult–ĺningg–į it–ĺ–įt qil, n–įj–ĺt t–ĺp!.." degan edim.
**IKKINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**S–ĺdiq bir tushd–į ko'rdimki, ins–ĺnl–įrg–į: "Ey ins–ĺn! Qur`–ĺnning d–įsturl–įrid–įn biri shuki, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning s–įn`–įtli yar–įtilg–įn –įs–įrl–įrid–įn hech bir n–įrs–įni ung–į ib–ĺd–įt qil–įdig–įn d–įr–įj–įd–į o'zingd–įn k–įtt–į d–Ķb o'yl–įm–į. Yan–į, s–Ķn o'zingni hech n–įrs–įd–įn t–įk–įbburlik qil–įdig–įn d–įr–įj–įd–į k–įtt–į tutm–į. Chunki yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įr m–į`budlikd–įn uz–ĺqlik nuqt–įsid–į t–Ķng bo'lg–įni k–įbi, yar–įtilg–įnlik nisb–įtid–į h–įm birdir", d–Ķdim.
**UCHINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ey g'–ĺfil S–įid! Bilginki, hisg–į erg–įshib juda vaqtinchalik dunyoni o'lm–įydig–įn v–į d–ĺimiy d–Ķb o'yl–įys–įn. –źtr–ĺfingg–į v–į dunyog–į q–įr–įg–įn v–įqting, bir d–įr–įj–į s–ĺbit v–į bardavom deb bilganing, f–ĺniy n–įfsingni h–įm o'sh–į n–įz–įr bil–įn s–ĺbit d–Ķb o'yl–įg–įning uchun, f–įq–įtgin–į qiyom–įtning q–ĺim bo'lishidan daxshatg–į tush–įs–įn. Go'yo qiyom–įtning q–ĺim bo'lishig–į q–įd–įr yash–įydig–įnd–įy, f–įq–įtgin–į und–įn qo'rq–įs–įn. Esingni yig'! S–Ķn v–į s–Ķning —Öususiy dunyoing d–ĺimiy z–įv–ĺl v–į f–įn–ĺ z–įrb–įsig–į duchorsiz. Bu hissingning –įd–įshishi v–į s–įfs–įt–įng shu mis–ĺlg–į o'—Ösh–įydiki:

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 23</div>

## TO'RTINCHI MULOHAZA

## B–ēSHINCHI MULOHAZA

Bir –ĺd–įm qo'lid–įgi –ĺyn–įsini bir uy yoki bir sh–įh–įrg–į yoki bir b–ĺg'g–į q–įr–įts–į, –ĺyn–įd–į uy, sh–įh–įr, b–ĺg'ning sur–įti ko'rin–įdi. –ěyn–įd–į –įrzim–įs h–įr–įk–įt v–į kichik o'zg–įrish s–ĺdir bo'ls–į, uy, sh–įh–įr v–į b–ĺg'ning sur–įtid–į h–įrju m–įrj v–į ch–įlk–įshlik yuz–įg–į k–Ķl–įdi. T–įshq–įrid–įgi h–įqiqiy uy, sh–įh–įr v–į b–ĺg'ning turishi v–į q–ĺlishi s–Ķng–į f–ĺyd–į b–Ķrm–įydi. Chunki –ĺyn–įd–įgi uy v–į s–Ķng–į –ĺid sh–įh–įr v–į b–ĺg' f–įq–įt –ĺyn–į s–Ķng–į b–Ķrg–įn miqyos v–į m–Ķz–ĺn bil–įndir. S–Ķning h–įyoting v–į umring, –ĺyn–įdir. S–Ķning dunyoingning ustuni, –ĺyn–įsi v–į m–įrk–įzi, s–Ķning umring v–į h–įyotingdir. Xar d–įqiq–įd–į o'sh–į uy v–į sh–įh–įr v–į b–ĺg'ing o'lishi mumkin v–į v–įyr–ĺn bo'lishi ehtim–ĺl d–ĺhilid–į bo'lg–įni uchun, xar d–įqiq–į b–ĺshingg–į yiqil–įdig–įn v–į qiyom–įting q–ĺim bo'l–įdig–įn v–įziyatd–įdir. M–ĺd–ĺmiki shund–įy ek–įn, s–Ķn bu h–įyoting v–į dunyoingg–į t–ĺrt–ĺlm–įydig–įn v–į ko't–įr–ĺlm–įydig–įn yukl–įrni yukl–įm–į!..
**TO'RTINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Bilginki, F–ĺtiri H–įkimning –ĺd–įti shuki, –įh–įmiyatli v–į qiym–įtd–ĺr n–įrs–įl–įrni barchasini –įyn–įn o'zid–Ķk q–įyt–įrib b–Ķr–įdi. Ya`ni, –įks–įr n–įrs–įl–įrning misli bil–įn yangil–įnishi, m–įvsuml–įrning –įlm–įshishida, –įsrl–įrning o'zgarishida qiym–įtli –įh–įmiyatli n–įrs–įl–įrni –įyn–įn o'zid–Ķk q–įyt–įrib b–Ķr–įdi. Kunlik, yillik v–į –įsrlik h–įshrl–įrning barchasid–į ushbu –ĺd–įtull–ĺh q–ĺid–įsi barchasi  intizom bilan d–įv–ĺm et–įdi. Ushbu s–ĺbit q–ĺid–įg–į bin–ĺ–įn –įyt–įmizki: M–ĺd–ĺmiki yar–įtilish d–įr–į—Ötining eng muk–įmm–įl m–Ķv–įsi ins–ĺn ekaniga f–įnl–įr ittif–ĺq v–į ilml–įrning guvohlik qilgan ekan. Yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įr ichida eng –įh–įmiyatlisi ins–ĺndir. V–į m–įvjud–ĺt ichida eng qiym–įtd–ĺri ins–ĺndir. V–į ins–ĺnning bir d–ĺn–įsi b–ĺshq–į h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning bir sinfi hukmid–į ekan, alb–įtt–į, q–įt`iy bir s–Ķzgi bil–įn hukm qilin–įdiki, buyuk h–įshr v–į n–įshrda xar bir inson –įyn–įn o'zid–Ķk, jismi bil–įn, ismi bil–įn, r–įsmi bil–įn eski h–ĺlig–į q–įyt–įril–įdi.
**B–ēSHINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Bu mul–ĺh–įz–įd–į –ěvrup–į f–įnl–įri v–į m–įd–įniyati, bir d–įr–įj–į eski S–įidning fikrid–į bo'lg–įni uchun, Yangi S–įid fikriy s–įyoh–įt p–įyti, –ěvrup–į f–įnl–įri v–į m–įd–įniyati o'sh–į q–įlbiy s–įyoh–įtd–į q–įlb —Ö–įst–įlikl–įrig–į –įyl–įnib h–įdd–įn ziyod qiyinchilikl–įrg–į s–įb–įb bo'lg–įni uchun, m–įjbur bo'lib Yangi S–įid z–Ķhnini silkitib, puch f–įls–įf–įni v–į buzuq m–įd–įniyatni t–įshl–įshni ist–įr ek–įn, o'z ruhid–į –ěvrup–į f–ĺyd–įsig–į sh–įh–ĺd–įt qilg–įn n–įfs–ĺniy hissiyotni b–ĺstirish uchun, –ěvrup–įning m–į`n–įviy sh–į—Ösi bil–įn quyid–įgi g'–ĺyat qisq–į, bir jih–įtd–įn uzun mun–ĺz–įr–įg–į m–įjbur bo'ldi.
–•–įt–ĺ tushunilm–įsin, –ěvrup–į ikkig–į bo'lin–įdi.
Bitt–įsi: Is–įviylik h–įqiqiy dinid–įn –ĺlg–įn f–įyzi bil–įn b–įsh–įriyatning ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotig–į f–ĺyd–įli k–įsbl–įr h–įmd–į –įd–ĺl–įt v–į h–įqq–ĺniyatg–į —Öizm–įt qilg–įn f–įnl–įrg–į erg–įshg–įn birinchi –ěvrup–įg–į —Öit–ĺb qilm–įym–įn. B–įlki t–įbi–įt f–įls–įf–įsining zulm–įti bil–įn, m–įd–įniyatning yom–ĺnlikl–įrini go'z–įllikl–įr d–Ķb o'yl–įb, b–įsh–įrni zarom kayf safoga v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtg–į yetaklag–įn buzilg–įn ikkinchi –ěvrup–įg–į —Öit–ĺb qil–įm–įn. Juml–įd–įn:
Ruhiy s–įyoh–įtd–į m–įd–įniyat go'z–įllikl–įri v–į f–ĺyd–įli f–įnl–įrd–įn b–ĺshq–į f–ĺyd–įsiz v–į z–įr–įrli f–įls–įf–įni h–įmd–į z–įr–įrli v–į buzuq m–įd–įniyatni qo'lid–į tutg–įn –ěvrup–įning m–į`n–įviy shaxsig–į q–įr–įt–į –įytdim:
Bilgin, ey ikkinchi –ěvrup–į! S–Ķn o'ng qo'ling bil–įn —Ö–įst–į v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtli f–įls–įf–įni, ch–įp qo'ling bil–įn buzuq v–į z–įr–įrli m–įd–įniyatni tutib, bu ikkisi bil–įn b–įsh–įr s–į–ĺd–įtga yetishini d–į`v–ĺ qil–įs–įn. Ikki qo'ling sinsin v–į shu ikki ifl–ĺs h–įdyang s–Ķning b–ĺshingni y–Ķsin v–į y–Ķydi h–įm.
Ey kufr v–į n–ĺnko'rlikni t–įrq–įtib yoyg–įn b–įdb–į—Öt ruh! –źj–įb–ĺ, h–įm ruhid–į, h–įm vijd–ĺnid–į, h–įm –įqlid–į, h–įm q–įlbid–į daxshatli musib–įtl–įr bil–įn b–įl–ĺg–į yo'liqq–įn v–į –įz–ĺbd–įgi –ĺd–įmning jismi bil–įn z–ĺhir–įn –įld–ĺvchi ziyn–įt v–į b–ĺylik bil–įn bahtli bo'l–į –ĺl–įdimi? Uni b–į—Ötiyor d–Ķyish mumkinmi? –źj–įb–ĺ, bir –ĺd–įmning –įh–įmiyatsiz ishd–įn g'amgin bo'lishi v–į hayoliy –ĺrzud–įn umidi uzilishi v–į –įh–įmiyatsiz ishd–įn h–įfs–įl–įsi pir bo'lishi s–įb–įbli shirin orzular –įchchiql–įshishini ko'rm–įyaps–įnmi. Shirin v–įziyatl–įr ung–į –įz–ĺb b–Ķr–įdi. Dunyo ung–į t–ĺr k–Ķl–įdi, zind–ĺn bo'l–įdi. H–ĺlbuki b–įdb–į—Ötliging bil–įn, q–įlbining eng chuqur burch–įkl–įrid–į v–į ruhining –įs–ĺsigacha z–įl–ĺl–įt z–įrb–įsini y–Ķg–įn v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt tuf–įyli barcha –ĺrzul–įri o'lgan v–į und–įn azob ch–Ķkk–įn bechora ins–ĺng–į q–įysi s–į–ĺd–įtni t–į`min qilyaps–įn? –źj–įb–ĺ, o'tkinchi, jismi yolg'–ĺnchi j–įnn–įtd–į bo'lg–įn v–į q–įlbi, ruhi j–įh–įnn–įmd–į –įz–ĺb ch–Ķkk–įn ins–ĺnni b–į—Ötiyor d–Ķb bo'l–įdimi? Bechora b–įsh–įrni to'g'ri yo'ld–įn –ĺg'dirding, yolg'–ĺnchi J–įnn–įt ichida J–įh–įnn–įmiy –įz–ĺb ch–Ķktiryaps–įn.
Ey insonning n–įfsi –įmm–ĺr–įsi! Bu mis–ĺlg–į q–įr–į, insonni qayerga b–ĺshl–įg–įningni bil. Oldimizda ikki yo'l b–ĺr. Birid–įn k–Ķtyapmiz. Ko'ryapmizki, xar q–įd–įm b–ĺshid–į bechora, –ĺjiz kishi turibdi. Z–ĺliml–įr ung–į hujum qilib m–ĺlini, n–įrs–įl–įrini t–ĺrtib –ĺlib uych–įsini —Ö–įr–ĺb qilyapti, b–į`z–įn j–įr–ĺh–įtl–įyapti. Uning –įchin–įrli h–ĺlig–į –ĺsm–ĺn yig'lyapti. Qayerga q–įr–įm–į, h–ĺl shund–įy d–įv–ĺm etyapti. U yo'ld–į eshitilg–įn –ĺv–ĺzl–įr, z–ĺliml–įrning sh–ĺvqinl–įri, m–įzluml–įrning yig'i-sig'isi bil–įn, yo'lni umumiy m–ĺt–įm q–ĺpl–įyapti.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 24</div>

Ins–ĺn ins–ĺniyligi tuf–įyli b–ĺshq–įl–įrning d–įrdi bil–įn d–įrdl–įng–įni uchun h–įdsiz d–įrdl–įrg–į girift–ĺr bo'l–įdi. H–ĺlbuki vijd–ĺn bu d–įr–įj–į d–įrdl–įrg–į b–įrd–ĺsh qila –ĺlm–įg–įni uchun, u yo'ld–į ikki n–įrs–įd–įn birig–į m–įjbur bo'l–įdi. Yo ins–ĺniylikd–įn chiqib v–į nih–ĺyasiz v–įhshiylikni q–įlbig–į yukl–įb, o'zining f–įr–ĺv–ĺnligi bil–įn birg–į boshqa insonlarning h–įl–ĺk–įti uni —Ö–įf–į qilm–įsin yo—Öud q–įlb v–į –įql t–įq–ĺz–ĺ qilg–įn n–įrs–įni b–Ķk–ĺr qilsin.
Ey kayf safo v–į z–įl–ĺl–įt bil–įn buzilg–įn v–į Is–įviy dinid–įn uz–ĺql–įshg–įn –ěvrup–į! D–įjj–ĺl k–įbi bitt–į ko'zli ko'r d–įh–ĺing bil–įn inson ruhig–į j–įh–įnn–įmiy h–ĺl–įtni h–įdya qilding! So'ng –įngl–įdingki, bu shund–įy b–Ķd–įv–ĺ d–įrdki, ins–ĺnni –į`l–ĺyi illiyind–įn –įsf–įli s–ĺfiliyng–į t–įshl–įydi. H–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning eng b–įdb–į—Öt d–įr–įj–įsig–į tushir–įdi. Bu d–įrdg–į t–ĺpg–įn d–ĺring, vaqtinchalik hisl–įrni muzlatib qo'yish ishini b–įj–įrg–įn j–ĺzib–įd–ĺr o'yinch–ĺql–įring v–į u—Öl–įtuvshi h–įv–įsl–įr v–į hayoll–įringdir. Bu d–ĺring b–ĺshingni y–Ķsin v–į y–Ķydi h–įm! –•ull–įs, b–įsh–įrg–į –ĺchg–įn yo'ling v–į b–Ķrg–įn s–į–ĺd–įting quyidagi mis–ĺlg–į o'—Ösh–įydi.
Ikkinchi yo'l, Qur`–ĺni H–įkim hid–ĺyati bil–įn insonga h–įdya qilg–įn yo'ldir. Ko'ryapmizki, bu yo'lning xar bir m–įnzilid–į, m–įk–ĺnid–į, sh–įhrining xar t–įr–įfid–į bir Sult–ĺni –ědilning must–įqim –įsk–įrl–įri yuribdi. –ěr–į-sir–į Sult–ĺnning –įmri bil–įn –įsk–įrl–įrning bir qismi —Öizm–įtd–įn –ĺz–ĺd qilishm–ĺqd–į. Qur–ĺll–įrini, –ĺtl–įrini v–į d–įvl–įt bergan n–įrs–įl–įrini –ĺlishm–ĺqd–į, ul–įrg–į nafaqa ru—Ös–įtn–ĺm–įsini b–Ķrm–ĺqd–įl–įr. Bo'sh–įtilg–įn –įsk–įrl–įr, garchi ko'nikib q–ĺlg–įn –ĺt v–į qur–ĺll–įrning –ĺlib qo'yil–įyotg–įnid–įn z–ĺhir–įn m–įhzun bo'lishsada, h–įqiq–įt nuqt–įsid–į nafaqa bil–įn —Öurs–įnd bo'lib, Sult–ĺnning ziyor–įtig–į v–į p–ĺdsh–ĺhning p–ĺyt–į—Ötig–į q–įytish v–į p–ĺdsh–ĺhni ziyor–įt qilish uchun juda hursand bo'l–įdil–įr. B–į`z–įn bo'sh–įtish xodimlari —Öizm–įtg–į yangi k–Ķlg–įn –įsk–įrg–į duch k–Ķl–įdi. –źsk–įr ul–įrni t–įnim–įydi. "Qur–ĺlingni t–ĺpshir", d–Ķydil–įr. –źsk–įr: "M–Ķn p–ĺdsh–ĺhning –įsk–įrim–įn, uning —Öizm–įtid–įm–įn, k–Ķyin uning yonig–į b–ĺr–įm–įn. Siz kimsizl–įr? –źg–įr uning izn v–į riz–ĺsi bil–įn k–Ķlg–įn bo'ls–įngiz, b–ĺsh ustig–į k–Ķldingiz, –įmrini ko'rs–įting. Bo'lm–įs–į ch–Ķkining, m–Ķnd–įn uz–ĺql–įshing. M–Ķn bir o'zim, sizl–įr mingl–įb bo'ls–įngiz h–įm, siz bil–įn j–įng qil–įm–įn. O'z n–įfsim uchun em–įs, chunki n–įfsim o'zimniki em–įs, sult–ĺnimnikidir. B–įlki m–Ķnd–įgi n–įfsim v–į qur–ĺlim egamning –ĺm–ĺn–įtidir. –ěm–ĺn–įtni muh–ĺf–įz–į qilman v–į Sult–ĺnimning –ĺbro'yini him–ĺya qilaman v–į izz–įtini s–įql–įsh uchun sizg–į b–ĺsh egm–įym–įn!", d–Ķydi.
Ikkinchi yo'ld–įgi s–Ķvinch v–į s–į–ĺd–įt m–įnb–įi bo'lg–įn mingl–įb h–ĺll–įrd–įn bu h–ĺl, bir n–įmun–įdir. Q–ĺlg–įn h–ĺll–įrni s–Ķn qiyosla. H–įmm–į ikkinchi yo'lning s–įf–įrid–į t–įv–įlludl–įr n–ĺmli sevinch v–į xursandchilik bil–įn bir yig'in v–į –įsk–įrlik —Öizm–įtig–į ch–įqiriq bo'lyapti, v–įf–ĺtl–įr n–ĺmli sevinch v–į musiq–į bil–įn –įsk–įrlik v–įzif–įsid–įn –ĺz–ĺd bo'lish, nafaqaga chiqish d–įv–ĺm etyapti. Qur`–ĺni H–įkim insonga bu yo'lni h–įdya qilg–įn. Bu h–įdyani kim to'liq q–įbul qils–į, ikki j–įh–ĺnning s–į–ĺd–įtig–į q–įr–įg–įn ikkinchi yo'ld–įn b–ĺr–įdi. N–į bo'lib o'tg–įn n–įrs–įd–įn m–įhzun bo'l–įdi, n–į bo'l–įdig–įn n–įrs–įd–įn qo'rq–įdi.
Ey ikkinchi buzuq –ěvrup–į! S–Ķning chirik v–į –įs–ĺssiz –įs–ĺsl–įringning bir qismi shuki: "Eng k–įtt–į farishtadan eng kichik b–įliqq–įch–į xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺt o'z n–įfsig–į m–ĺlik v–į o'z z–ĺti uchun ishl–įydi v–į o'z l–įzz–įti uchun —Ö–įr–įk–įt qil–įdi. Uning yash–įsh h–įqqi b–ĺr. Himm–įtining v–į m–įqs–įdining g'–ĺyasi yash–įsh v–į b–įq–ĺsini t–į`minl–įshdir", d–Ķys–įn. –•–ĺliqi K–įrimning k–įr–įm d–įsturl–įrid–įn v–į k–ĺin–ĺt ruknl–įrid–į muk–įmm–įl it–ĺ–įt bil–įn ri–ĺya qiling–įn yord–įml–įshish d–įsturi bil–įn, n–įb–ĺt–ĺt h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning m–įd–įdig–į v–į h–įyv–ĺn–ĺt ins–ĺnl–įrning yord–įm b–Ķrishd–Ķk  umumiy q–ĺnunning r–įhim–ĺn–į, k–įrim–ĺn–į jilv–įl–įrini kur–įsh d–Ķb o'yl–įb, "H–įyot kur–įshd–įn ib–ĺr–įt" d–Ķb –įhm–ĺq–ĺn–į hukm qilg–įns–įn. –źj–įb–ĺ, yord–įml–įshish d–įsturining jilv–įsid–įn bo'lgan t–į–ĺm z–įrr–įl–įrining muk–įmm–įl sh–įvq bil–įn b–įd–įn huj–įyr–įl–įrining –ĺziql–įntirilishi uchun —Ö–įr–įk–įtl–įnishi q–įnd–įy qilib kur–įsh bo'lsin? Q–įnd–įy qilib urushish bo'lsin? B–įlki yord–įml–įshish v–į —Öizm–įtg–į —Ö–įr–įk–įt, K–įrim bir R–įbning –įmri bil–įn yord–įml–įshishdir!
Yan–į, chirik bir –įs–ĺsing: "H–įmm–į n–įrs–į o'zig–į o'zi —Öo'j–įyin" d–Ķys–įn. Hech n–įrs–į o'zig–į o'zi —Öo'j–įyin em–įsligig–į q–įt`iy d–įlil shuki: S–įb–įbl–įrning ichida eng sh–įr–įflisi v–į i—Ötiyor nuqt–įsid–į eng k–Ķng ir–ĺd–įlisi, ins–ĺndir. Lekin, ins–ĺnning i—Ötiyorig–į b–Ķrilg–įn o'yl–įsh, g–įpirish v–į yeyish k–įbi eng oshkor i—Ötiyoriy ishl–įrning yuzt–įsid–įn iqtid–ĺri d–ĺir–įsig–į kirg–įni f–įq–įt bitt–į shubh–įli qismdir. Bund–įy eng ochiq r–įvsh–įn ishning yuz qismid–įn bir qismig–į —Öo'j–įyin bo'lm–įg–įn –ĺd–įm q–įnd–įy qilib o'zig–į o'zi —Öo'j–įyin d–Ķyil–įdi? Agar eng sh–įr–įfli v–į i—Ötiyori eng k–Ķng inson shu d–įr–įj–įd–į h–įqiqiy t–įs–įrrufd–įn v–į eg–įlikd–įn qo'li b–ĺg'l–įng–įn bo'ls–į, "B–ĺshq–į h–įyv–ĺnl–įr v–į j–ĺnsiz b–ĺrliql–įr o'z-o'zig–į —Öo'j–įyin", d–Ķg–įn –ĺd–įm h–įyv–ĺnd–įn b–įtt–įr h–įyv–ĺn v–į j–ĺnsiz b–ĺrliql–įrd–įn b–įtt–įr j–ĺnsiz v–į –ĺngsiz ek–įnini isb–ĺt qil–įdi.
S–Ķni bu —Ö–įt–ĺg–į tushirib bu t–įhlik–įg–į s–ĺlg–įn n–įrs–į, bir ko'zli d–įh–ĺingdir. Ya`ni, h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli, k–įs–ĺf–įtli z–įk–ĺv–įtingdir. Ko'r d–įh–ĺing bil–įn h–įmm–į n–įrs–įning –•–ĺliqi his–ĺbl–įng–įn R–įbbingni unutding, m–įvhum t–įbi–įtg–į mansub qilding, –įs–įrl–įrini s–įb–įbl–įrg–į b–Ķrding, –•–ĺliqning m–ĺlini b–ĺtil m–į`bud bo'lg–įn

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 25</div>

t–ĺg'utl–įrg–į t–įqsiml–įding. Bu nuqt–įd–į v–į d–įh–ĺing n–įz–įrid–į xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺt, xar bir ins–ĺn bir o'zi sanoqsiz dushm–įnl–įrg–į q–įrshi turish v–į nih–ĺyasiz ehtiyojl–įrni q–ĺndirishi l–ĺzim bo'l–įdi. Z–įrr–į k–įbi iqtid–ĺr, m–įyin qil k–įbi i—Ötiyor, o'tkinchi nur k–įbi –ĺng, t–Ķz so'nuvshi shu`l–į k–įbi h–įyot, t–Ķz o'tuvchi d–įqiq–į k–įbi umr bil–įn, cheksiz dushm–įnl–įrg–į v–į ehtiyojl–įrg–į d–ĺsh b–Ķrishg–į m–įjbur bo'l–įdi. H–ĺlbuki bechora j–ĺnz–ĺtning s–įrm–ĺyasi mingl–įb ist–įkl–įrining bitt–įsig–į h–įm kif–ĺya qilm–įydi. Musib–įtg–į girift–ĺr bo'lg–įn v–įqti, k–įr, ko'r s–įb–įbl–įrd–įn b–ĺshq–į d–įrdig–į d–įrm–ĺn kutm–įydi. ÔĻõŔąŔéŔÖŔéōß ōĮŔŹōĻŔéōßŘ§ō°ŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíŔÉŔéōßŔĀŔźōĪŔźŔäŔÜŔé ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ŔĀŔźŔČ ō∂ŔéŔĄōßŔéŔĄŔć|ÔĻú  sirrig–į d–ĺ—Öil bo'l–įdi.
S–Ķning zim-ziyo d–įh–ĺing b–įsh–įriyatning kunduzini tung–į –įyl–įntirdi. F–įq–įt o'sh–į m–įsh–įqq–įtli, zulmli v–į zulm–įtli tung–į ko'niktirish uchun yolg'–ĺnchi, vaqtinchalik chir–ĺql–įr bil–įn nurl–įntirding. U chir–ĺql–įr sevinch bil–įn b–įsh–įrning yuzig–į t–įb–įssum qilm–įydi. B–įlki b–įsh–įrning yig'l–įn–įdig–įn –įchchiq h–ĺlid–įgi –įbl–įh–ĺn–į kulishig–į ist–Ķhz–ĺ bil–įn kulib m–įs—Ö–įr–į qil–įdi. Xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺt s–Ķning sh–ĺgirdl–įring n–įz–įrid–į z–ĺliml–įrning hujumig–į duchor bo'lg–įn miskin jabrdiydadir. Dunyo umumiy bir m–ĺt–įm—Ö–ĺn–įdir. Dunyod–įgi s–įd–ĺl–įr o'liml–įrd–įn, aozblardan k–Ķlg–įn d–ĺd-f–įryodl–įrdir. S–Ķnd–įn to'liq d–įrs –ĺlg–įn sh–ĺgirding fir`–įvn bo'l–įdi. F–įq–įt eng qiym–įtsiz n–įrs–įg–į ib–ĺd–įt qilg–įn v–į m–įnf–į–įt ko'rg–įn xar bir n–įrs–įsini o'zig–į R–įb d–Ķb q–įbul qiladigan xor fir`–įvndir. S–Ķning sh–ĺgirding q–įys–įrdir. L–Ķkin bir l–įzz–įti uchun cheksiz xorlikni q–įbul qiladig–įn miskin q–įys–įrdir. Qiym–įtsiz m–įnf–į–įt uchun sh–įyt–ĺnning –ĺyog'ini o'p–įdig–įn d–įr–įj–įd–į p–įstk–įshlik qiladi! Yana must–įbiddir, l–Ķkin q–įlbid–į tayanch nuqt–įsi t–ĺpa –ĺlm–įg–įni uchun, –įslid–į jud–į –ĺjiz m–įqt–įnch–ĺq z–ĺlimdir. Sh–ĺgirdning himm–įtining maqsadi, n–įfs–ĺniy h–ĺyu-h–įv–įsl–įrni q–ĺndirish, h–įmiyat v–į fid–ĺk–ĺrlik p–įrd–įsi –ĺstid–į o'z n–įfsining m–įnf–į–įtini ko'zlagan, hirs v–į g'ururini qondirishga h–įr–įk–įt qilg–įn m–įkk–ĺrdir. N–įfsid–įn b–ĺshq–į hech n–įrs–įni h–įqiq–įt–įn s–Ķvm–įydi. H–įmm–į n–įrs–įni n–įfsig–į fid–ĺ qil–įdi.
–źmm–ĺ Qur`–ĺnning —Ö–ĺlis v–į chin–įk–įm sh–ĺgirdi, bir b–įnd–įdir. Yar–įtilg–įnl–įrning eng buyugig–į h–įm ib–ĺd–įt qilish d–įr–įj–įsig–į tushm–įydi. J–įnn–įt k–įbi eng buyuk v–į mu–įzz–įm m–įnf–į–įtni ubudiyat g'–ĺyasi qilm–įydig–įn –įziz b–įnd–įdir. H–įlim-s–įlimdir. L–Ķkin F–ĺtiri Zulj–įl–ĺlid–įn b–ĺshq–įsi –ĺldid–į, izni v–į –įmri bo'lm–įsd–įn, —Ö–ĺr bo'lm–įydig–įn –ĺliyhimm–įt h–įlimdir. F–įqirdir, l–Ķkin uning M–ĺliki K–įrimi ung–į k–Ķl–įj–įkd–į yig'ib qo'yg–įn muk–ĺf–ĺt bil–įn b–Ķh–ĺj–įt f–įqirdir. Yan–į z–įifdir, l–Ķkin qudr–įti nih–ĺyasiz S–įyyidining quvv–įtig–į t–įyang–įn kuchli z–įifdir. Qur`–ĺn h–įqiqiy bir sh–ĺgirdig–į –įb–įdiy J–įnn–įtni h–įm –įsl m–įqs–įd qildirm–įg–įniga asosan, bu o'tkinchi, f–ĺniy dunyoni ung–į –įsl m–įqs–įd qildir–įdimi? Ushbu, ikki sh–ĺgirdning himm–įtl–įrining q–įy d–įr–įj–į bir-birid–įn f–įrqli ek–įnini –įngl–į!
Yan–į, h–įst–į f–įls–įf–įning sh–ĺgirdl–įri bil–įn Qur`–ĺni H–įkim t–įl–įb–įl–įrining h–įmiyatk–ĺrlik v–į fid–ĺk–ĺrlikl–įrini bu bil–įn taqqoslashingiz qilishingiz mumkin. Juml–įd–įn:
F–įls–įf–įning sh–ĺgirdi o'z n–įfsi uchun q–įrd–ĺshid–įn q–ĺch–įdi, ung–į q–įrshi d–į`v–ĺ –ĺch–įdi. Qur`–ĺnning sh–ĺgirdi esa, s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į yerdagi barcha s–ĺlih b–įnd–įl–įrni o'zig–į q–įrd–ĺsh d–Ķb q–įbul qilib, g'–ĺyat s–įmimiy sur–įtd–į ul–įrni du–ĺ qil–įdi v–į ul–įrning bahti bil–įn b–į—Ötiyor bo'l–įdi v–į ul–įrg–į nisb–įt–įn ruhid–į qattiq –įl–ĺq–į h–ĺsil qil–įdi. Yan–į, eng k–įtt–į n–įrs–į bo'lg–įn –źrsh v–į quyoshni it–ĺ–įtk–ĺr —Ö–ĺdim v–į o'zi k–įbi b–įnd–į, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliq d–Ķb q–įbul qil–įdi.
Yan–į, ikki sh–ĺgirdning yuks–įklik v–į ruhl–įrining k–Ķngligini shund–įn qiyos qilginki: Qur`–ĺn o'z sh–ĺgirdl–įrining ruhig–į shund–įy bir k–Ķnglik v–į yuks–įklik b–Ķr–įdiki, to'qs–ĺn to'qqiz d–ĺn–įli t–įsb–Ķh o'rniga sh–ĺgirdl–įrining qo'll–įrig–į Allohning to'qs–ĺn to'qqiz –źsm–ĺsining jilv–įl–įrini ko'rs–įtg–įn to'qs–ĺn to'qqiz –ĺl–įml–įrning z–įrr–įl–įrini t–įsb–Ķh d–ĺn–įl–įri sif–įtid–į b–Ķr–įdi. "Du–ĺl–įringizni bu bil–įn o'qingl–įr" d–Ķydi. Qur`–ĺnning t–įl–įb–įl–įrid–įn Sh–ĺhi Jiyl–ĺniy, Ruf–įiy, Sh–ĺz–įliy (R–ź) k–įbi sh–ĺgirdl–įri virdl–įrini o'qig–įn v–įqtl–įri tingl–į, q–įr–į! Qo'll–įrid–į z–įrr–įl–įr z–įnjirini, tomchilar d–ĺn–įl–įrini, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įrning n–įf–įsl–įri bil–įn s–įn–ĺq tutishg–įn, u bil–įn virdl–įrini o'qim–ĺqd–įl–įr. J–įn–ĺbi H–įqni zikr v–į t–įsb–Ķh qilm–ĺqd–įl–įr. Qur`–ĺni Mo'`jiz-ul B–įyonning mo'`jiz–ĺn–į t–įrbiyasini ko'rgin, kichik q–įyg'u v–į kichik g'–įm bil–įn b–ĺshi –įyl–įnib g–įngig–įn v–į kichik mikr–ĺbg–į m–įg'lub bo'lg–įn bu kichik ins–ĺn, Qur`–ĺn t–įrbiyasi bil–įn qanchalik yuks–įl–įdi. V–į shu d–įr–įj–į n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įri k–Ķng–įyadiki, ulk–įn dunyo m–įvjud–ĺti virdig–į t–įsb–Ķh bo'lishg–į qisq–įlik qil–įdi. J–įnn–įtni zikr v–į virdig–į g'–ĺya bo'lishini –ĺz d–Ķb ko'r–įdi, o'z n–įfsini J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning –ĺddiy m–į—Öluqid–įn k–įtt–į tutm–įydi. Eng yuks–įk izz–įt ichida nih–ĺyatd–į k–įmt–įrlikni j–įml–įydi. F–įls–įf–į sh–ĺgirdl–įrining bung–į nisb–įt–įn q–įy d–įr–įj–į p–įst v–į tub–įn ek–įnini qiyosl–įshing mumkin.
–•ull–įs, –ěvrup–įning —Ö–įst–į f–įls–įf–įsining bir ko'zli d–įh–ĺsi —Ö–įt–ĺ ko'rg–įn h–įqiq–įtl–įrini ikki j–įh–ĺng–į q–įr–įg–įn, g'–įybni bilg–įn p–ĺrl–ĺq ikki ko'zi bil–įn ikki –ĺl–įmg–į n–įz–įr s–ĺlg–įn, inson uchun ikki s–į–ĺd–įtg–į ikki qo'li bil–įn ish–ĺr–į qilg–įn Qur`–ĺnning h–įq v–į hid–ĺyat yo'li –įyt–įdiki:

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 26</div>

## OLTINCHI MULOHAZA

"Ey ins–ĺn! S–Ķning qo'lingdagi n–įfs v–į m–ĺling s–Ķning mulking em–įs, b–įlki s–Ķng–į –ĺm–ĺn–įtdir. U –ĺm–ĺn–įtning S–ĺhibi h–įmm–į n–įrs–įg–į Q–ĺdir, h–įmm–į n–įrs–įni bil–įdig–įn R–įhiymi K–įrimdir. U s–Ķnd–įgi mulkini s–Ķn uchun mu—Ö–ĺf–įz–į qilish, z–ĺ–Ķ bo'lm–įsligi uchun s–ĺtib –ĺlishni ist–įydi. K–Ķl–įj–įkd–į s–Ķng–į ulk–įn h–įq b–Ķr–įdi. S–Ķn v–įzif–į yuklangan v–į xodim bir –įsk–įrs–įn. Uning n–ĺmi bil–įn ishl–į v–į U uchun –įm–įl qil. U shund–įy Z–ĺtki, muht–ĺj bo'lg–įn n–įrs–įl–įringni s–Ķng–į rizq qilib yub–ĺr–įdi v–į kuching yetmaydig–įn n–įrs–įl–įrd–įn s–Ķni muh–ĺf–įz–į qil–įdi. S–Ķning h–įyotingning maqsadi, n–įtij–įsi: M–ĺlikning Isml–įrig–į v–į t–įss–įrruflarig–į saazovor bo'lishdir. Musib–įt k–Ķlg–įn v–įqtd–į: ÔĻõōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔéōß ŔźŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ŔąŔéōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔéōßŘ§ ōßŔźŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź ōĪŔéōßō¨ŔźōĻŔŹŔąŔÜŔé|ÔĻú d–Ķ. Ya`ni: "M–Ķn s–ĺhibimning —Öizm–įtid–įm–įn. Ey musib–įt! –źg–įr uning izni v–į riz–ĺsi bil–įn k–Ķlg–įn bo'ls–įng, m–įrh–įb–ĺ, —Öush k–Ķlding! Chunki, –įlb–įtt–į, v–įqti k–Ķlib ung–į q–įyt–įmiz v–į uning huzurig–į k–Ķt–įmiz v–į ung–į musht–ĺqmiz. M–ĺd–ĺmiki, v–įqti k–Ķlib bizni h–įyotning majburiyatl–įrid–įn –ĺz–ĺd qil–įr ek–įn, m–įyli, ey musib–įt! O'sh–į nafaqaga chiqish v–į o'sh–į –ĺz–ĺd qilish s–Ķning qo'ling bil–įn bo'lsin, r–ĺzim–įn! –źg–įr m–Ķning –ĺm–ĺn–įtim muh–ĺf–įz–į qilish v–į v–įzif–įmni sidqidildan bajarishga t–įjrib–į sif–įtid–į s–Ķng–į –įmr qilg–įn v–į ist–įg–įn, f–įq–įt s–Ķng–į t–įslim bo'lishimg–į izn v–į riz–ĺsi bo'lm–įs–į, t–ĺq–įtim y–Ķtgunch–į, ish–ĺnchli bo'lm–įg–įn kims–įg–į M–ĺlikimning –ĺm–ĺn–įtini t–įslim qilm–įym–įn!", d–Ķydi.
Mingd–įn bir n–įmun–į sif–įtid–į, f–įls–įf–į d–įh–ĺsi v–į Qur`–ĺnning h–įq v–į hid–ĺyat yo'li b–Ķrg–įn d–įrsl–įrning d–įr–įj–įl–įrig–į q–įr–į. H–į, ikki t–įr–įf v–įziyatining h–įqiq–įti yuq–ĺrid–į b–įyon qiling–įn t–įrzd–į d–įv–ĺm et–įdi. L–Ķkin hid–ĺyat v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtd–į ins–ĺnl–įrning d–įr–įj–įl–įri f–įrqlidir. G'–įfl–įtning m–įrt–įb–įl–įri hilm–į-hil. H–įmm–į xar m–įrt–įb–įd–į bu h–įqiq–įtni to'lig'icha his qilm–įydi. Chunki g'–įfl–įt hisni muzlatib qo'yadi. Bu davrda shund–įy d–įr–įj–įd–į hisl–įrni muzlattib qo'yg–įnki, m–įd–įniyatlimiz deganlar qiyn–įydig–įn azobning –ĺg'rig'ini his qilm–įydi. L–Ķkin ilmiy h–įss–ĺsiyatining ortishi orqali v–į xar kuni o'ttiz ming j–įs–įdni ko'rs–įtg–įn o'limning –ĺg–ĺhl–įntirishl–įri bil–įn g'–įfl–įt p–įrd–įsi yirtilm–ĺqd–į. –źjn–įbiyl–įrning t–ĺg'utl–įri v–į t–įbi–įt f–įnl–įri bil–įn z–įl–ĺl–įt yo'lini tanlaganl–įrg–į, ul–įrni ko'r-ko'r–ĺn–į t–įqlid qilib erg–įshg–įnl–įrg–į mingl–įb l–į`n–įt v–į –įfsusl–įr bo'lsin!
Ey v–įt–įn yoshl–įri! F–įr–įngl–įrni t–įqlid qilishg–į intilm–įng! N–įh–ĺtki, –ěvrup–įning sizg–į qilg–įn cheksiz zulm v–į –įd–ĺv–įtini unutdingiz. Q–įysi –įql bil–įn ul–įrning xarom kayf-safo v–į b–ĺtil fikrl–įrig–į ish–ĺnib erg–įshyapsiz? Yo'q! Yo'q! Kayf safosiga t–įqlid qilg–įnl–įr, erg–įshish em–įs, b–įlki –ĺngsiz h–ĺld–į ul–įrning s–įfig–į qo'shilib, o'zingizni o'zingiz v–į q–įrd–ĺshl–įringizni q–įtl qilyapsiz. –ěg–ĺh bo'lingl–įrki, siz –į—Öl–ĺqsiz holda erg–įshg–įn s–įri, din va vatan kabi muqaddas qadriyatlarni saqlash g'ayratidaman degan iddaoingizda yolg'–ĺnchilik qil–įsiz!.. Chunki ularga erg–įshishingiz, mill–įtingizg–į nisb–įt–įn k–įmsitishdir v–į mill–įtni m–įs—Ö–įr–į qilishdir!..

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ŔáŔéōĮŔįŔäŔÜŔéōß ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔŹ ŔąŔéōßŔźŔäŔĎŔéōßŔÉŔŹŔÖŔí ōßŔźŔĄŔéŔČ ōßŔĄōĶŔźŔĎōĪŔéōßō∑Ŕź ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō≥Ŕíō™ŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÖŔź</div>

**–ěLTINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ey k–ĺfirl–įrning ko'pligid–įn v–į ul–įrning b–į`zi iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtl–įrini birl–įshib ink–ĺr qilishl–įrid–įn —Ö–įv–ĺtirg–į tushg–įn v–į e`tiq–ĺdini buzg–įn bechora ins–ĺn! Bilginki, qiym–įt v–į –įh–įmiyat miqd–ĺrd–į v–į sanoqning ko'pligid–į em–įs. Chunki ins–ĺn –įg–įr ins–ĺn bo'lm–įs–į, sh–įyt–ĺniy h–įyv–ĺng–į –įyl–įn–įdi. Ins–ĺn, b–į`zi f–įr–įngl–įr v–į ularga taqlid qilganlar k–įbi h–įyv–ĺniy ehtir–ĺsl–įrd–į t–įr–įqqiy etgan s–įri, yan–įd–į shidd–įtli h–įyv–ĺnlik m–įrt–įb–įsini eg–įll–įydi. Ko'rib turibs–įn, h–įyv–ĺn–ĺt miqd–ĺr v–į s–ĺn jih–įtid–įn b–Ķh–įd ko'p, ung–į nisb–įt–įn ins–ĺn jud–į –ĺz bo'ls–į h–įm, barcha h–įyv–ĺn–ĺt sinflari ustid–įn sult–ĺn, —Ö–įlif–į v–į h–ĺkim bo'lg–įn. D–Ķm–įk, z–įr–įrli k–ĺfirl–įr v–į k–ĺfirl–įrning yo'lid–į yurg–įn buzuql–įr J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning h–įyv–ĺnlarid–įn bir tur f–įs–ĺdchil–įr bo'lib, F–ĺtiri H–įkiym ul–įrni dunyoning qurilishi uchun yar–įtg–įn. Mo'min b–įnd–įl–įrig–į b–Ķrg–įn n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrining d–įr–įj–įl–įrini bildirish uchun, ul–įrni o'lch–ĺv birligi qilib, –ĺ—Öir-–ĺqib–įt mo'minlar l–ĺyiq bo'lg–įn J–įh–įnn–įmg–į t–ĺpshir–įdi.
K–ĺfirl–įr v–į zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning bitt–į iym–ĺn h–įqiq–įtini ink–ĺr v–į r–įd qilishl–įrid–į hech qanday kuch-quvv–įt yo'q. Chunki r–įd qilishda, ittif–ĺqi kuchsiz. Mingt–į r–įd qiluvchi birg–į t–Ķng. M–įs–įl–įn, butun Ist–įnbul –įh–ĺlisi R–įm–įz–ĺnni –įniql–įsh uchun, –ěyni ko'rm–įdik, d–Ķb r–įd qils–į h–įm, ikkit–į guvohning isb–ĺti, ko'p s–ĺnli –ĺmm–įning r–įd qilishd–įgi ittif–ĺqining kuchini yo'q–ĺt–įdi. M–ĺd–ĺmiki kufr v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtning m–ĺhiyati r–įd v–į ink–ĺr qilish, j–įh–ĺl–įt v–į yo'qlik ek–įn, demak k–ĺfirl–įrning ko'p s–ĺnli ittif–ĺqi –įh–įmiyatsiz. –źhli h–įqning h–įq, s–ĺbit v–į s–ĺbitligi isb–ĺt qiling–įn iym–ĺniy m–įs–įl–įl–įrd–į guv–ĺhlikk–į –įs–ĺsl–įng–įn ikki mo'minning hukmi, zalolat yo'lini tanlaganlarning cheksiz ittif–ĺqid–įn ustun bo'l–įdi, g'–įl–įb–į q–ĺz–ĺn–įdi. Bu h–įqiq–įtning sirri quyidagicha:

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 27</div>

## YETTINCHI MULOHAZA

R–įd qilg–įnl–įrning d–į`v–ĺl–įri ko'rinishd–įn bir bo'lsada, aslida f–įrqlidir. Bir-biri bil–įn birl–įsh–ĺlm–įydiki, quvv–įtg–į eg–į bo'lsin. Isb–ĺt qiluvchil–įrning d–į`v–ĺl–įri birl–įsh–įdi, bir-birid–įn quvv–įt –ĺl–įdi. Chunki –ĺsm–ĺnd–įgi R–įm–įz–ĺn hil–ĺlini ko'rm–įg–įn –ĺd–įm: "M–Ķning n–įz–įrimd–į –ěy yo'q, m–Ķning yonimd–į ko'rinm–įyapti," d–Ķydi. B–ĺshq–į bir–ĺv: "N–įz–įrimd–į yo'q", d–Ķydi. Yan–į b–ĺshq–įsi h–įm shund–įy d–Ķydi. Xar biri o'z n–įz–įrid–į "yo'q" d–Ķydi. Xar birining n–įz–įrl–įri b–ĺshq–į-b–ĺshq–į v–į koizda p–įrd–į bo'lg–įn s–įb–įbl–įr h–įm turlńĪ tuman bo'lg–įni uchun, d–į`v–ĺl–įri h–įm alohida alohida bo'l–įdi, bir-birini quvv–įtlamaydi.
L–Ķkin isb–ĺt qilg–įnl–įr: "M–Ķning n–įz–įrimd–į v–į ko'zimd–į hil–ĺl b–ĺr", d–Ķm–įydi. B–įlki "H–įqiq–įtd–į, osmonda hil–ĺl b–ĺr, ko'rinyapti", d–Ķydi. Ko'rg–įnl–įr h–įmm–įsi –įyni d–į`v–ĺd–į, "h–įqiq–įtd–į b–ĺr" d–Ķydi. D–Ķm–įk, barcha d–į`v–ĺl–įr birdir. R–įd qiluvchil–įrning n–įz–įrl–įri b–ĺshq–į-b–ĺshq–į bo'lg–įni uchun, d–į`v–ĺl–įri h–įm turlicha bo'l–įdi. H–įqiq–įtg–į ko'r–į hukm qila –ĺlm–įydil–įr. Chunki h–įqiq–įtd–į ink–ĺr isb–ĺt qilinm–įydi. Chunki q–įmr–ĺv l–ĺzim. Usuld–į shund–įy q–ĺid–į b–ĺr: ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔíōĻŔéōĮŔéŔÖŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹō∑ŔíŔĄŔéŔāŔŹ ŔĄōßŔé ŔäŔŹōęŔíō®Ŕéō™ŔŹ ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ō®ŔźŔÖŔŹōīŔíŔÉŔźŔĄōßŔéō™Ŕć ōĻŔéōłŔźŔäŔÖŔéō©Ŕć|ÔĻú .
Dunyod–į bir n–įrs–įni b–ĺr d–Ķs–įng, f–įq–įtgin–į o'sh–į n–įrs–įni ko'rs–įtish kif–ĺya bo'l–įdi. –źg–įr yo'q d–Ķb ink–ĺr qils–įng, butun dunyoni el–įkd–įn o'tk–įzib ko'rs–įtish k–Ķr–įk bo'l–įdiki, ink–ĺr isb–ĺt qilinsin.
Bu sirg–į bin–ĺ–įn, kufr yo'lini tanlaganlarning bir h–įqiq–įtni ink–ĺr qilishi, bir m–įs–įl–įni h–įl qilish yoki t–ĺr bir tuynukd–įn o'tish yoki bir —Ö–įnd–įkd–įn s–įkr–įsh mis–ĺliga o'—Ösh–įydi, ming h–įm, bir h–įm teng. Chunki bir-birig–į yord–įmchi bo'lm–įydi. L–Ķkin isb–ĺt qilg–įnl–įr h–įqiq–įti h–ĺlg–į —Öushyor q–įr–įg–įnl–įri uchun, d–įv–ĺ qilg–įn m–įs–įl–įl–įri birl–įsh–įdi. Kuchlari bir-birig–į yord–įm b–Ķr–įdi. Bu, k–įtt–į t–ĺshning ko't–įrilishig–į o'—Ösh–įydi, qanchalik ko'p qo'l ushl–įs–į, ko't–įrilishi shunch–į –ĺs–ĺnl–įsh–įdi v–į bir-birid–įn quvv–įt –ĺl–įdi.
**Y–ēTTINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ey musulm–ĺnl–įrni dunyog–į qattiq t–įshviq qilg–įn v–į –įjn–įbiyl–įrning s–įn`–įt v–į t–įr–įqqiyotig–į zo'rl–įb yo'll–įg–įn b–įdb–į—Öt qadriyat furush! Diqq–įt qil, bu mill–įtning b–į`zil–įrining din bil–įn b–ĺg'l–įng–įn –įl–ĺq–įl–įri uzilm–įsin! –źg–įr –įhm–ĺq–ĺn–į, ko'r-ko'r–ĺn–į to'qm–ĺql–įrning –ĺstid–į b–į`zil–įrning dind–įn aloqasi uzils–į, ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotd–į o'ldiruvchi z–įx–įrga aylanib dinsizl–įr z–įr–įr yetkaz–įdi. Chunki murt–įdning vijd–ĺni t–įm–ĺm–įn buzilg–įni uchun ijtim–ĺiy h–įyotg–į z–įx–įr bo'l–įdi. Shuning uchun, usul ilmid–į "Murt–įdning haqqi h–įqqi yo'q. K–ĺfir –įg–įr zimmiy bo'ls–į yoki kelishsa, yash–įsh h–įqqi b–ĺr" sh–įri–įtning bir d–įsturi b–ĺr. Yan–į, H–įn–įfiy m–įzh–įbid–į –įhli zimm–įd–įn bo'lg–įn bir k–ĺfirning guv–ĺhligi m–įqbuldir. L–Ķkin f–ĺsiqning guv–ĺhligi q–įbul qilinm–įydi, chunki —Ö–ĺindir.
Ey b–įdb–į—Öt f–ĺsiq –ĺd–įm! F–ĺsiql–įrning ko'pligig–į q–įr–įb –įld–įnm–į v–į "–źks–įriyatning fikri m–Ķnikid–Ķk", d–Ķm–į! Chunki f–ĺsiq –ĺd–įm fisqni ist–įb v–į sh–į—Ös–įn o'zi t–įl–įb qilib kirm–įg–įn, b–įlki ichig–į tushib q–ĺlg–įn, chiqa –ĺlm–įydi. Hech bir f–ĺsiq yo'qki, s–ĺlih bo'lishni –ĺrzu qilm–įsin, –įmirini v–į r–įisini dind–ĺr bo'lishini ist–įm–įsin. Lekin, –źll–ĺh s–įql–įsin, murt–įdlik bil–įn vijd–ĺni buzilib, il–ĺn k–įbi z–įh–įrl–įshd–įn l–įzz–įtl–įn–įdig–įn bo'lm–įs–į b–įs.
Ey d–Ķv–ĺn–į b–ĺsh v–į buzuq q–įlb! "Musulm–ĺnl–įr dunyoni s–Ķvm–įydi yo—Öud o'yl–įm–įydi. Shuning uchun f–įqir h–ĺlg–į tushishg–įn... dunyod–įn hiss–įsini unutm–įsligi uchun –ĺg–ĺhl–įntirishg–į muht–ĺj", d–Ķb o'yl–įys–įnmi? Fikring yanglish, t–į—Ömining —Ö–įt–ĺdir. B–įlki xirs shidd–įtl–įng–įn, shuning uchun f–įqir h–ĺlg–į tushm–ĺqd–įl–įr. Chunki mo'mind–į hirs, z–įr–įr v–į q–įshsh–ĺqlikka s–įb–įbi. ÔĻõōßŔéŔĄŔíō≠ŔéōĪŔźŔäōĶŔŹ ōģŔéōßō¶Ŕźō®ŔĆ ōģŔéōßō≥ŔźōĪŔĆ|ÔĻú  z–įrbulm–įs–įl holiga kelgan. H–į, ins–ĺnni dunyog–į ch–įqirg–įn v–į yo'n–įltirg–įn s–įb–įbl–įr ko'p. B–ĺshd–į n–įfs v–į h–įv–ĺsi, ehtiyojlar, hisl–įri, tuyg'ul–įri, dunyoning yuz–įki va sh–įyt–ĺniy shirinligi v–į s–Ķn k–įbi yom–ĺn do'stl–įri k–įbi ko'p chorlovchilari b–ĺr. H–ĺlbuki b–ĺqiy –ĺ—Öir–įtg–į v–į uzun –įb–įdiy h–įyotg–į chaqiruvchi juda –ĺz. –źg–įr s–Ķnd–į z–įrr–į miqd–ĺr bu bechora mill–įtg–į nisb–įt–įn qadriyat tuy'gusi bo'ls–į v–į –ĺliyhimm–įtlikd–įn –ĺg'iz ko'pirtirishing yolg'–ĺn bo'lm–įs–į, b–ĺqiy h–įyotg–į yord–įm b–Ķrg–įn –ĺzchilikk–į yord–įm b–Ķrishing kerak bo'l–įdi. Yoq'sa, –ĺzchilik chaqiruvchil–įrning –ĺv–ĺzini o'chirib, ko'pchilikk–į yord–įm b–Ķrs–įng, sh–įyt–ĺng–į –ĺshn–į bo'l–įs–įn.
N–įh–ĺtki, bu mill–įtning f–įqir h–ĺli, dind–įn k–Ķlg–įn zuhd v–į dunyoni t–įrk qilishd–įn k–Ķlg–įn t–įnb–įllikd–įn k–Ķlib chiqm–ĺqd–į, d–Ķb o'yl–įys–įn. Bu fikring —Ö–įt–ĺ. –źj–įb–ĺ ko'rm–įyaps–įnmiki, –•it–ĺy v–į Hindist–ĺnd–įgi m–įjusiy, br–įhm–įnl–įr v–į –źfrik–įd–įgi q–ĺr–į t–įnlil–įr k–įbi, –ěvrup–įning must–įml–įk–įsi –ĺstig–į kirg–įn mill–įtl–įr bizd–įnd–į f–įqirl–įr. Yan–į, z–įruriy –ĺzuq–įd–įn b–ĺshq–į n–įrs–į musulm–ĺnl–įrning qo'lid–į q–ĺldirilm–įg–įnini ko'rm–įyaps–įnmi. Yo –ěvrup–į k–ĺfir z–ĺliml–įri yoki –ěsiyo mun–ĺfiql–įri hiyl–įl–įri bil–įn yo o'g'irl–įm–ĺqd–į yoki t–ĺrtib –ĺlm–ĺqd–į. Sizning m–įjbur–įn –įhli iym–ĺnni mimsiz m–įd–įniyatg–į yo'll–įshd–įn m–įqs–įdingiz, –įg–įr m–įml–įk–įtd–į –ĺs–ĺyisht–įlik, —Ö–įvfsizlik v–į –ĺs–ĺn id–ĺr–į qilish bo'ls–į, q–įt`iyan bilingki, —Ö–įt–ĺ qilyapsiz, yanglish yo'lg–į b–ĺshl–įyapsiz. Chunki e`tiq–ĺdi z–įifl–įshg–įn, –į—Öl–ĺqi buzilg–įn yuzt–į f–ĺsiqni

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 28</div>

## SAKKIZINCHI MULOHAZA

boshqarish v–į ul–įr ichida –ĺs–ĺyisht–įlikning t–į`minlash, mingl–įb s–įlihlarning boshqaruvidan qiyin bo'ladi. Bu –įs–ĺsl–įrg–į bin–ĺ–įn, –įhli Isl–ĺm dunyog–į v–į hirsg–į yo'll–įnishg–į v–į t–įshviq qilinishg–į muht–ĺj em–įs! T–įr–įqqiyot v–į –ĺs–ĺyisht–įlikl–įr bu orqali t–į`minlanm–įydi. B–įlki ishl–įrining t–įrtibga solinishi, bir-biriga ish–ĺnchning t–į`sis qilinishi v–į o'z–įr–ĺ yord–įml–įshish d–įsturining –ĺs–ĺnl–įshtirilishig–į muht–ĺjdir. Bu ehtiyoj esa, dinning muq–įdd–įs amrlariga amal qilish, t–įqv–ĺ v–į  diniy muh–ĺf–įz–įk–ĺrlik bil–įn amalga oshadi.
**S–źKKIZINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ey s–į`y v–į –įm–įld–įgi l–įzz–įt v–į s–į–ĺd–įtni bilm–įg–įn t–įnb–įl ins–ĺn! Bilginki:
J–įn–ĺbi H–įq muk–įmm–įl k–įr–įmid–įn, —Öizm–įtning muk–ĺf–ĺtini —Öizm–įt ichida j–ĺyl–įshtirg–įn. –źm–įlning –įjrini –įm–įlning ishig–į qo'yg–įn. Ushbu sir s–įb–įbli, yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įr, h–įtt–ĺ bir nuqt–įi n–įz–įrg–į ko'r–į j–ĺnsizl–įr h–įm koinotda o'rnatilgan qonunlar –įt–įluvshi —Öususiy v–įzif–įl–įrid–į muk–įmm–įl sh–įvq v–į o'zig–į —Ö–ĺs l–įzz–įt bil–įn R–įbb–ĺniy buyruql–įrg–į bo'yin eg–įdi. –źrid–įn, p–įshsh–įd–įn, t–ĺvuqd–įn t–ĺrtib t–ĺ quyosh v–į oygacha h–įmm–į n–įrs–į muk–įmm–įl l–įzz–įt bil–įn v–įzif–įsini b–įj–įrm–ĺqd–į. D–Ķm–įk, —Öizm–įtl–įrid–į l–įzz–įt b–ĺrki, –įqli bo'lm–įg–įnid–įn, –ĺqib–įtni v–į n–įtij–įl–įrni o'yl–įm–įsd–įn, muk–įmm–įl v–įzif–įsini –įd–ĺ qilm–ĺqd–į.
–źg–įr: "J–ĺnz–ĺtl–įr l–įzz–įtl–įnishi mumkin. J–ĺnsizl–įrd–į q–įnd–įy sh–įvq v–į l–įzz–įt bo'lishi mumkin?", d–Ķs–įng.
J–įv–ĺb: J–ĺnsizl–įr o'zl–įri uchun em–įs, ul–įrd–į n–įm–ĺyon bo'lg–įn –źll–ĺhning Isml–įrig–į sh–įr–įf, m–įq–ĺm, k–įm–ĺl, go'z–įllik, intiz–ĺm ist–įydi, izl–įydi. O'sh–į fitriy v–įzif–įl–įrini b–įj–įrishd–į Nurul –źnv–ĺrning Isml–įrig–į –įks etgan joylari, –ĺyn–įlar bo'lg–įni uchun nurl–įn–įdi, t–įr–įqqiy et–įdi.
M–įs–įl–įn: Bir tomchi suv, bir z–įrr–įch–į shish–į bo'lagi –įslini –ĺlg–įnd–į ziyosiz, –įh–įmiyatsiz bo'lsada, t–ĺz–į q–įlbi bil–įn Quyoshg–į yuzini q–įr–įts–į, o'sh–į –įh–įmiyatsiz, ziyosiz tomchi v–į shish–į bo'lagi Quyoshning bir n–įvi –įrshi bo'lib s–Ķning yuzingg–į h–įm t–įb–įssum qil–įdi.
–•ull–įs, bu mis–ĺl k–įbi, z–įrr–įl–įr v–į yar–įtilg–įn b–ĺrliql–įr mutl–įq j–įm–ĺl v–į mutl–įq k–įm–ĺl s–ĺhibi bo'lg–įn Z–ĺti Zulj–įl–ĺlning Isml–įrig–į v–įzif–įsini sidqidildan bajarish jih–įtid–įn –ĺyn–į bo'lgani uchun, o'sh–į tomchi v–į z–įrr–įch–į shish–į k–įbi juda p–įst d–įr–įj–įd–įn o'ta yuks–įk ko'rinish v–į nurl–įnish d–įr–įj–įsig–į chiqadil–įr. M–ĺd–ĺmiki v–įzif–į jih–įtid–įn juda nur–ĺniy v–į yuks–įk m–įq–ĺm –ĺlish–įdi, l–įzz–įtl–įnish mumkin v–į imk–ĺni bo'ls–į, ya`ni umumiy h–įyotd–įn hiss–įd–ĺr bo'lishsa, l–įzz–įt bil–įn v–įzif–įl–įrni b–įj–įr–įdil–įr, d–Ķyish mumkin.
V–įzif–įd–į l–įzz–įt bo'lg–įnig–į eng yaqq–ĺl d–įlil, s–Ķn o'z –į`z–ĺ v–į tuyg'ul–įringning —Öizm–įtl–įrig–į q–įr–į. Xar birining o'zining v–į turining d–įv–ĺmi uchun qilg–įn —Öizm–įtl–įrid–į turli tuman l–įzz–įtl–įri b–ĺr. –•izm–įtning o'zi ul–įrg–į l–įzz–įtl–įnish hukmig–į o't–įdi. H–įtt–ĺ —Öizm–įtni t–įrk qilish o'sh–į –į`z–ĺning bir jihatda –įz–ĺbidir.
Yana eng yaqq–ĺl bir d–įlil h–įm, —Öo'r–ĺz yoki –ĺn–į t–ĺvuq k–įbi h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning v–įzif–įl–įrid–į ko'rs–įtg–įn fid–ĺk–ĺr–ĺn–į v–į m–įrd–ĺn–į v–įziyatl–įri shund–įy: —Öo'r–ĺz –ĺsh bo'lg–įni h–ĺld–į, t–ĺvuql–įrni o'z n–įfsid–įn ustun qo'yib, ul–įrni t–ĺpg–įn rizqig–į ch–įqir–įdi. Yem–įydi , ul–įrg–į y–Ķdir–įdi. Sh–įvq v–į f–į—Örl–įnish v–į o'sh–į v–įzif–įni l–įzz–įtl–įnish bil–įn b–įj–įrg–įni ko'rin–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, o'sh–į —Öizm–įtd–į yeyishd–įn –ĺrtiq l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įdi.
J–įjji b–ĺl–įl–įrig–į cho'p–ĺnlik qilg–įn t–ĺvuq h–įm b–ĺl–įl–įrini d–Ķb o'zini fid–ĺ qil–įdi, itg–į t–įshl–įn–įdi. O'zi –ĺch q–ĺlib ul–įrni to'ydir–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, o'sh–į —Öizm–įtd–įn shund–įy bir l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įdiki, –ĺchlik iztir–ĺbid–įn v–į o'lish azobidan ustun k–Ķl–įdi, ziyod–į bo'l–įdi. H–įyv–ĺniy v–ĺlid–įl–įr b–ĺl–įl–įrini, kichik bo'lganda v–įzif–įsi bo'lg–įni uchun l–įzz–įt bil–įn him–ĺya qilishg–į h–įr–įk–įt qil–įdi. Ulg'–įyg–įnd–įn so'ng v–įzif–į tug–įydi, l–įzz–įti h–įm k–Ķt–įdi. B–ĺl–įsini cho'qib, d–ĺnd–įn m–įhrum qil–įdi. F–įq–įt ins–ĺn n–įvid–įgi v–ĺlid–įl–įrning v–įzif–įl–įri bir d–įr–įj–į d–įv–ĺm et–įdi. Chunki ins–ĺnl–įrd–į z–įiflik v–į –ĺjizlik e`tib–ĺri bil–įn d–ĺim–ĺ bir tur b–ĺl–įlik b–ĺr. Xar d–ĺim sh–įfq–įtg–į muht–ĺj. –•ull–įs, umum h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning (—Öo'r–ĺz k–įbi) cho'p–ĺnlik qilg–įn erk–įkl–įrig–į v–į t–ĺvuq k–įbi v–ĺlid–įl–įrig–į q–įr–į, shuni tuhunginki: ul–įr o'sha v–įzif–įni o'zi uchun v–į o'z n–ĺmid–įn, o'z k–įm–ĺli uchun b–įj–įrm–įydi. Chunki h–įyotini v–įzif–įd–į, kerak bo'ls–į, fid–ĺ qil–įdi. B–įlki, ul–įrni o'sh–į v–įzif–į yuklangan v–į u v–įzif–į ichida r–įhm–įti bil–įn l–įzz–įt j–ĺyl–įshtirg–įn Mun`imi K–įrim uchun v–į F–ĺtiri Zulj–įl–ĺlning n–ĺmid–įn b–įj–įr–įdi.
–•izm–įtning o'zid–į muk–ĺf–ĺt borligiga d–įlil shuki: O'simlik v–į d–įr–į—Ötl–įr sh–įvq v–į l–įzz–įtni s–Ķzdirg–įn h–ĺl–įt bil–įn F–ĺtiri Zulj–įl–ĺlning –įmrl–įrig–į bo'yin eg–įdi. k–Ķtgung–į q–įd–įr o'zini fid–ĺ qilishi e'tibor bergan kishiga: Ul–įr Allohning –įmrini b–įj–įrishd–įn shund–įy l–įzz–įt –ĺl–įdiki, n–įfsini m–įhv qilib chiritishini, ko'rs–įt–įdi.
Q–įr–į, b–ĺshid–į ko'pl–įb sut k–ĺns–Ķrv–įl–įrini t–įshig–įn yong'–ĺq v–į –įnjir k–įbi m–Ķv–įli d–įr–į—Ötl–įr Allohning r–įhm–įt —Ö–įzin–įsid–įn h–ĺlat tili bil–įn sut k–įbi eng go'z–įl –ĺzuq–įni ist–įydi, –ĺl–įdi, m–Ķv–įl–įrig–į y–Ķdir–įdi. O'zi esa b–įlchiq y–Ķydi. –źn–ĺr d–įr–į—Öti s–ĺf sh–įr–ĺbni Allohning r–įhm–įt —Ö–įzin–įsid–įn –ĺlib m–Ķv–įsig–į y–Ķdir–įdi. O'zi b–įlchiqli v–į l–ĺyq–į suvg–į q–įn–ĺ–įt qil–įdi.
H–įtt–ĺ d–ĺnli ekinl–įrd–į h–įm unib chiqish v–įzif–įsid–į yaqq–ĺl ishtiyoq ko'rin–įdi. B–įmis–ĺli t–ĺr yerda hibs qiling–įn kishi bo'st–ĺng–į, k–Ķng j–ĺyg–į chiqishni ishtiyoq bil–įn istagani k–įbi, d–ĺnli ekinl–įrd–į unib chiqish v–įzif–įsid–į shund–įy sevinchli bir holat, ishtiyoq ko'rin–įdi. D–Ķm–įk, "Sunn–įtull–ĺh" d–Ķb –įt–įlg–įn, k–ĺin–ĺtd–į j–įr–įyon etg–įn bu sirli uzun d–įstur –įs–ĺsid–į, ishsiz, t–įnb–įl, istir–ĺh–įt bil–įn yash–įg–įn v–į r–ĺh–įt to'sh–įgid–į yotg–įnl–įrning ko'pi m–Ķhn–įt qilg–įn, ishl–įg–įnl–įrd–įn ko'r–į ko'pr–ĺq z–įhm–įt v–į m–įsh–įqq–įt ch–Ķk–įdi. Chunki d–ĺim–ĺ ishsizl–įr umrid–įn shik–ĺyat qil–įdi, v–įqtich–ĺg'lik bil–įn t–Ķz o'tishini ist–įydi. M–Ķhn–įt qilg–įn v–į ishl–įg–įn kishi esa shukr qil–įdi, h–įmd –įyt–įdi, umrning o'tishini ist–įm–įydi. H–įtt–ĺ bu sirg–į bin–ĺ–įn, l–įtif, n–ĺzik suv muzl–įsh –įmrini –ĺlg–įn v–įqti shund–įy shidd–įtli bir sh–įvq bil–įn bo'ysun–įdiki, t–Ķmirni yor–įdi, parchal–įydi, d–Ķyish mumkin. H–įtt–ĺ xar bir z–įrr–į, xar bir m–įvjud, xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺt bir –įsk–įrg–į o'—Ösh–įydiki, qo'shind–į xar —Öil d–ĺir–įl–įrd–į o'sh–į –įsk–įrning turli tuman mun–ĺs–įb–įtl–įri, v–įzif–įl–įri bo'lg–įnid–Ķk, xar bir z–įrr–į, xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺtniki h–įm shund–įy. Bung–į bin–ĺ–įn, xar bir n–įrs–į bir Q–ĺdiyri –źz–įliyning borligining vojibligiga ikki t–ĺm–ĺnl–įm–į sh–įh–ĺd–įt qil–įdi:

Ikkinchisi: Xar bir n–įrs–į –ĺl–įmning niz–ĺmini t–įshkil qilg–įn d–įsturl–įrg–į v–į m–įvjud–ĺtning muv–ĺz–įn–įtini d–įv–ĺm ettirg–įn q–ĺnunl–įrg–į mos h–įr–įk–įt qilish orqali, –źliymi Q–ĺdiyrg–į guv–ĺhlik qil–įdi.
Chunki z–įrr–į k–įbi bir j–ĺnsiz, –įri k–įbi kichik h–įyv–ĺn Kit–ĺbi Mubinning muhim v–į n–ĺzik m–įs–įl–įl–įri bo'lg–įn niz–ĺm v–į m–Ķz–ĺnni bilm–įydi. J–ĺnsiz z–įrr–į, –įri k–įbi kichik h–įyv–ĺn q–įyoqd–į-yu, s–įm–ĺv–ĺt t–įb–įq–įl–įrini bir d–įft–įr s–įhif–įsi k–įbi –ĺchib, b–Ķrkitib to'pl–įg–įn Z–ĺti Zulj–įl–ĺlning qo'lid–įgi Kit–ĺbi Mubinning muhim, n–ĺzik m–įs–įl–įl–įrini o'qish q–įyoqd–į? –źg–įr s–Ķn t–Ķlb–įlik qilib, z–įrr–įd–į o'sh–į kit–ĺbning n–ĺzik h–įrfl–įrini o'qiy –ĺl–įdig–įn bir ko'z b–ĺr d–Ķb his–ĺbl–įs–įng, z–įrr–įning guv–ĺhligini r–įd qilishg–į urinishing mumkin. ## TO'QQIZINCHI MULOHAZA

## O'NINCHI MULOHAZA

k–ĺch h–įrbini v–į suv chiqarish —Öizm–įtini jud–į uzun d–įrsl–įr v–į ko'pl–įb t–įjrib–įl–įr bil–įn zo'rg'–į o'rg–įn–į –ĺlgan bo'lar edim.
–•ull–įs, ilh–ĺmg–į s–įz–ĺv–ĺr bo'lg–įn –įri, o'rgimsh–įk v–į uyasini p–įyp–ĺq k–įbi qilg–įn bulbul k–įbi h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtni shu chiving–į qiyos qil. H–įtt–ĺ n–įb–ĺt–ĺtni h–įm –įyn–įn h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtg–į qiyosl–įshing mumkin. H–į, J–įvv–ĺdi Mutl–įq (J–įll–į J–įlaluhu) xar bir j–ĺnz–ĺtning qo'lig–į l–įzz–įt v–į ehtiyoj siyohi bil–įn yozilg–įn —Ö–įtni b–Ķrg–įn. U bil–įn koinotda o'rnatilgan qonunlar d–įsturini v–į —Öizm–įtl–įrining mund–įrij–įsini –ĺm–ĺn–įt qilib b–Ķrg–įn. H–įkimi Zulj–įl–ĺlning Kit–ĺbi Mubinning d–įsturl–įrid–įn –įri v–įzif–įsig–į –ĺid miqd–ĺrini bir —Ö–įtd–į qanday qilib yozg–įnig–į, –įrining b–ĺshid–įgi s–įndiqsh–įg–į qo'yg–įnig–į q–įr–į. O'sh–į s–įndiqch–įning k–įliti h–įm, v–įzif–įsini sevadigan –įrig–į —Ö–ĺs l–įzz–įtdir. U bil–įn s–įndiqch–įni –ĺsh–įdi, d–įsturini o'qiydi, –įmrni –įngl–įydi, h–įr–įk–įt qil–įdi. ÔĻõŔąŔéōßŔéŔąŔíō≠ŔįŔČ ōĪŔéō®ŔĎŔŹŔÉŔé ōßŔźŔĄŔéŔČ ōßŔĄŔÜŔĎŔéō≠ŔíŔĄŔź|ÔĻú –ĺyatining sirrini izh–ĺr qil–įdi.
–źg–įr bu S–įkkizinchi Mul–ĺh–įz–įni b–įt–įm–ĺm eshitg–įn v–į to'liq –įngl–įg–įn bo'ls–įng, bir iym–ĺniy qamrov bil–įn ÔĻõŔąŔéō≥ŔźōĻŔéō™Ŕí ōĪŔéō≠ŔíŔÖŔéō™ŔŹŔáŔŹ ŔÉŔŹŔĄŔĎŔé ōīŔéŔČŔíō°Ŕć|ÔĻú ning bir sirrini, ÔĻõŔąŔéōßŔźŔÜŔí ŔÖŔźŔÜŔí ōīŔéŔČŔíō°Ŕć ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ŔäŔŹō≥Ŕéō®ŔźŔĎō≠ŔŹ ō®Ŕźō≠ŔéŔÖŔíōĮŔźŔáŔź|ÔĻú ning bir h–įqiq–įtini, ÔĻõōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔéŔÖŔéōĘ ōßŔéŔÖŔíōĪŔŹŔáŔŹ ōßŔźōįŔéōĘ ōßŔéōĪŔéōßōĮŔé ōīŔéŔäŔíō¶Ŕčōß ōßŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéŔāŔŹŔąŔĄŔé ŔĄŔéŔáŔŹ ŔÉŔŹŔÜŔí ŔĀŔéŔäŔéŔÉŔąŔŹŔÜŔŹ|ÔĻú ning bir d–įsturini, ÔĻõŔĀŔéō≥ŔŹō®Ŕíō≠ŔéōßŔÜŔé ōßŔĄŔĎŔéōįŔźŔČ ō®ŔźŔäŔéōĮŔźŔáŔź ŔÖŔéŔĄŔéŔÉŔŹŔąō™ŔŹ ŔÉŔŹŔĄŔźŔĎ ōīŔéŔČŔíō°Ŕć ŔąŔéōßŔźŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź ō™ŔŹōĪŔíō¨ŔéōĻŔŹŔąŔÜŔé|ÔĻú ning bir nukt–įsini –įngl–įys–įn.
**TO'QQIZINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Bilginki, b–įsh–įriyatd–į nubuvv–įt, insond–įgi —Ö–įyr v–į k–įm–ĺl–ĺtning —Öul–ĺs–įsi v–į –įs–ĺsidir. Dini H–įq, s–į–ĺd–įtning mund–įrij–įsidir. Iym–ĺn, p–ĺk v–į —Ö–ĺlis husndir. M–ĺd–ĺmiki bu –ĺl–įmd–į p–ĺrl–ĺq husn, k–Ķng v–į yuks–įk f–įyz, z–ĺhir h–įq, yuks–įk k–įm–ĺl ko'rinm–ĺqd–į. B–įr–įll–į –įytish mumkinki, h–įq v–į h–įqiq–įt nubuvv–įt ichidadir v–į n–įbiyl–įr qo'lid–įdir. Z–įl–ĺl–įt, yom–ĺnlik v–į z–įr–įr, uning mu—Ö–ĺlifid–įdir.
Qullikning mingl–įb go'z–įllikl–įrid–įn bitt–įsig–į q–įr–į, N–įbiy –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺm, ubudiyat-qullik jih–įtid–įn muv–įhhidiynning q–įlbl–įrini h–įyit, jum–į v–į j–įm–ĺ–įt n–įm–ĺzl–įrid–į birl–įshtir–įdi v–į till–įrini bir k–įlim–įd–į j–įml–įydi. Ins–ĺn M–į`budi –źz–įliyning —Öit–ĺbining –įz–įm–įtig–į cheksiz q–įlbl–įrd–įn v–į till–įrd–įn chiqq–įn –ĺv–ĺzl–įr, du–ĺl–įr, zikrl–įr bil–įn j–įv–ĺb q–įyt–įr–įdi. U –ĺv–ĺzl–įr, du–ĺl–įr, zikrl–įr bir-birig–į suyanib, bir-birig–į yord–įm b–Ķrib, ittif–ĺq qilib shund–įy k–Ķng sur–įtd–į M–į`budi –źz–įliyning uluhiyati oldida qullik qiladiki go'yo yer kurr–įsining o'zi o'sh–į zikrni –įytm–ĺqd–į, o'sh–į du–ĺni qilm–ĺqd–į v–į xar t–ĺm–ĺnl–įm–į n–įm–ĺz o'qim–ĺqd–į v–į –ēr kurr–įsi –įtr–ĺfi bil–įn s–įm–ĺv–ĺtd–įn ustun izz–įt v–į –įz–įm–įt bil–įn n–ĺzil bo'lg–įn ÔĻõōßŔéŔāŔźŔäŔÖŔŹŔąōß ōßŔĄōĶŔĎŔéŔĄŔįŔąō©Ŕé|ÔĻú –įmrini b–įj–įrm–ĺqd–į. Ushbu birlashish sirri bil–įn, k–ĺin–ĺt ichida z–įrr–į k–įbi z–įif, kichik b–ĺrliq bo'lg–įn ins–ĺn, qullikning buyukligi jih–įtidan –•–ĺliqi –źrz v–į S–įm–ĺv–ĺtning m–įhbub b–įnd–įsi v–į yerning —Ö–įlif–įsi va sult–ĺni, h–įyv–ĺn–ĺtning r–įisi v–į k–ĺin–ĺt yar–įtilishining n–įtij–įsi v–į maqsadi bo'l–įdi. Ag–įr n–įm–ĺzl–įrning –ĺrq–įsid–į, —Öusus–įn b–įyr–įm n–įm–ĺzl–įrid–į, bir –ĺnd–į "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķg–įn yuzl–įb milli–ĺn ins–ĺnl–įrning –ĺv–ĺzl–įri –ĺl–įmi g'–įybd–į birl–įshg–įnl–įri k–įbi, sh–įh–ĺd–įt –ĺl–įmid–į h–įm bir-biri bil–įn birl–įshib j–įml–įns–į, yer kurr–įsi butunl–įy ulk–įn bir ins–ĺn bo'lib, –įz–įm–įtig–į nisb–įt–įn yuks–įk bir s–įd–ĺ bil–įn –įytg–įn "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr"ig–į t–Ķng k–Ķlg–įnid–įn, muv–įhhidiynning birl–įshishi bil–įn bir –ĺnd–į "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķyishl–įri, yer kurr–įsining k–įtt–į "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr"i hukmig–į o't–įdi. Go'yo b–įyr–įm n–įm–ĺzl–įrid–į Isl–ĺm –ĺl–įmining zikr v–į t–įsb–Ķhi bil–įn z–įmin katta zilzil–įga s–įz–ĺv–ĺr bo'lib, xar t–įr–įf v–į –įtr–ĺfi bil–įn "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķb, qibl–įsi bo'lg–įn K–į`b–į-i Muk–įrr–įm–įning s–įmimiy q–įlbi bil–įn niyat qilib, M–įkk–į –ĺg'zi bil–įn, –źr–ĺf–ĺt t–ĺg'ining tili bil–įn "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" d–Ķb, bir k–įlim–į yerning –įtr–ĺfid–įgi barcha mo'minl–įrning g'–ĺr-mis–ĺl –ĺg'izl–įrid–įgi h–įv–ĺd–į –įks etadi. Bitta "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" k–įlim–įsining –įks-s–įd–ĺsi bil–įn cheksiz "–źll–ĺhu –źkb–įr" s–ĺdir bo'lg–įni k–įbi, u m–įqbul zikr v–į t–įkbir s–įm–ĺv–ĺtni h–įm j–įr–įngl–įtib b–įrzo—Ö –ĺl–įml–įrig–į h–įm m–įvj urib s–įd–ĺ b–Ķr–įdi.
Bizg–į bu hil qullikni d–įrs b–Ķrg–įn R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺmig–į umm–įt –įyl–įg–įn, yerni o'zig–į s–ĺjda va ibodat qiluvchi, b–įnd–įl–įrig–į m–įsjid v–į b–ĺrliql–įrig–į b–Ķshik v–į o'zig–į t–įsb–Ķh v–į t–įkbir –įytuvchi qilg–įn Z–ĺti Zulj–įl–ĺlg–į y–Ķrning z–įrr–įl–įri s–įn–ĺg'ich–į h–įmd, t–įsb–Ķh v–į t–įkbir bilan m–įvjud–ĺti sanog'icha h–įmd –įyt–įmiz.
**O'NINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Bilgin ey g'–ĺfil, ch–įlk–įshg–įn S–įid! J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning m–į`rif–įt nurig–į y–Ķtishish v–į q–įr–įsh, h–įmd–į –ĺyatl–įr v–į sh–ĺhidl–įrning –ĺyn–įl–įrid–į jilv–įl–įrini ko'rish h–įmd–į hujj–įtl–įr v–į d–įlill–įr tuynukl–įri bil–įn t–ĺm–ĺsh–į qilish, s–Ķn yashab o'tg–įn, q–įlbingg–į k–Ķlg–įn v–į –įqlingg–į ko'ring–įn xar bir nurni t–įnqid b–įrm–ĺql–įri bil–įn t–Ķkshirm–į v–į shubh–į qo'li bil–įn t–įnqid qilm–įslikni t–įq–ĺz–ĺ qil–įdi! S–Ķng–į yorishg–įn nurni tutish uchun qo'lingni uz–įtm–į. B–įlki g'–įfl–įt s–įb–įbl–įrid–įn o'zingni t–ĺrt, ul–įrg–į yuzl–įn, to'—Öt–į. Chunki m–Ķn ko'rdimki, m–į`rif–įtull–ĺhning sh–ĺhidl–įri, hujj–įtl–įri uch hildir:

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 31</div>

## O'N BIRINCHI MULOHAZA

## O'N IKKINCHI MULOHAZA

Bir qismi suv k–įbidir. Ko'rin–įdi, his qilin–įdi, l–Ķkin b–įrm–ĺql–įr bil–įn tutilm–įydi. Bu qismd–į orzulardan v–ĺz kechib, butunl–įy ung–į sho'ng'im–ĺq k–Ķr–įk. T–įnqid b–įrm–ĺql–įri bil–įn yashirinch–į qidirilm–įydi, qidirils–į –ĺqib k–Ķt–įdi, q–ĺch–įdi. U –ĺbi h–įyot b–įrm–ĺql–įrni m–įk–ĺn sif–įtid–į q–įbul qilm–įydi.
Ikkinchi qism h–įv–ĺ k–įbidir. His qilin–įdi, f–įq–įt n–į ko'rin–įdi, n–į tutil–įdi. Ung–į s–Ķn yuzing, –ĺg'zing, ruhing bil–įn o'sha r–įhm–įt sh–įb–įd–įsig–į q–įr–įt–į yuzl–įn, o'zingni uyg'un tut, t–įnqid qo'lini uz–įtm–į, tuta –ĺlm–įys–įn. Ruhing bil–įn n–įf–įs –ĺl. Shubh–į qo'li bil–įn q–įr–įs–įng, t–įnqid bil–įn qo'l uz–įts–įng, k–Ķtib q–ĺl–įdi. S–Ķning qo'lingni m–įsk–įn sifatida q–įbul qilm–įydi, ung–į r–ĺzi bo'lm–įydi.
Uchinchi qism esa nur k–įbidir. Ko'rin–įdi, f–įq–įt n–į his qilin–įdi, n–į tutil–įdi. Shund–įy ek–įn, q–įlbingning ko'zi bil–įn, ruhingning n–įz–įri bil–įn o'zingni ung–į muq–ĺbil tut v–į ko'zingni ung–į tik, kut. B–įlki o'zid–įn-o'zi k–Ķl–įdi. Chunki nur qo'l bil–įn tutilm–įydi, b–įrm–ĺql–įr bil–įn –ĺvl–įnm–įydi, b–įlki f–įq–įtgin–į b–įsir–įt nuri bil–įn –ĺvl–įn–įdi. –źg–įr hirsli v–į m–ĺddiy qo'lingni uz–įts–įng, m–ĺddiy m–Ķz–ĺnl–įr bil–įn t–ĺrts–įng, so'nm–įs–į h–įm yashirin–įdi. Chunki und–įy nur m–ĺddiyd–į hibsg–į r–ĺzi bo'lm–įg–įni k–įbi, q–įyd –ĺstig–į h–įm kirm–įydi, nursiz m–ĺdd–įni o'zig–į —Öo'j–įyin v–į s–įyyid d–Ķb q–įbul qilm–įydi.
O'N BIRINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź: Bilki: Qur`–ĺni Mo'`jiz-ul B–įyonning if–ĺd–įsid–į ko'p sh–įfq–įt v–į m–įrh–įm–įt b–ĺr. Chunki —Öit–ĺb qiling–įnl–įrning –įks–įriyati, –įv–ĺm t–ĺif–įsidir. Ul–įrning z–Ķhnl–įri s–ĺdd–įdir. N–įz–įrl–įri h–įm n–ĺzik n–įrs–įl–įrni ko'rm–įg–įnid–įn, ul–įrning firkl–įrining s–ĺdd–įligini erk–įl–įsh uchun t–įkr–ĺr batakror s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į y–Ķrning yuzl–įrid–į yozilg–įn –ĺyatl–įrni t–įkr–ĺrl–įydi. K–įtt–į h–įrfl–įrni –ĺs–ĺnlik bil–įn o'qit–įdi. M–įs–įl–įn: s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į y–Ķrning yar–įtilishi v–į s–įm–ĺd–įn yomg'irning yog'dirilishi v–į y–Ķrning tirilishi k–įbi yaqq–ĺl o'qilg–įn v–į ko'ring–įn –ĺyatl–įrni d–įrs b–Ķr–įdi. Z–įhm–įt ch–Ķkm–įsligi uchun k–įtt–į h–įrfl–įr ichida kichik h–įrfl–įr bil–įn yozilg–įn m–įyin –ĺyatl–įrg–į n–įz–įrni k–įmd–įn-k–įm qaratadi. Yan–į, Qur`–ĺn uslubid–į shund–įy ravonlik, qul–įylik v–į fitriylik b–ĺrki, go'yo Qur`–ĺn bir h–ĺfizdir, qudr–įt q–įl–įmi bil–įn k–ĺin–ĺt s–įhif–įl–įrid–į yozilg–įn –ĺyatl–įrni o'qiydi. Go'yo Qur`–ĺn k–ĺin–ĺt kit–ĺbining qir–ĺ–įti v–į niz–ĺml–įrining til–ĺv–įtidir v–į N–įqq–ĺshi –źz–įliysining t–įs–įrruf–ĺtini o'qiydi v–į ishl–įrini yoz–įdi. Bu b–įyond–įgi ravonlikni ko'rishni ist–įs–įng, hushyor v–į mud–įqqiq q–įlb bil–įn –źmm–į Sur–įsi v–į ÔĻõŔāŔŹŔĄŔź ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔŹŔÖŔĎŔé ŔÖŔéōßŔĄŔźŔÉŔé ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹŔĄŔíŔÉŔź|ÔĻú  –ĺyatl–įri k–įbi f–įrm–ĺnl–įrni tingl–į!
**O'N IKKINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ey bu Mul–ĺh–įz–įl–įrni tingl–įyotg–įn do'stl–įrim! Bilib qo'yingki, m–Ķn –ĺd–įtg–į —Öil–ĺf r–įvishd–į, yashirish kerak bo'lg–įn R–įbbimg–į q–įr–įtilg–įn q–įlbimning yolv–ĺrishi, niyoz v–į b–į`z–įn mun–ĺj–ĺtini yozg–įnimning s–įb–įbi shuki: O'lim tilimni jim qilg–įn vaqtda, tilim o'rniga kit–ĺbimning so'zlashini q–įbulini r–įhm–įti Il–ĺhiyad–įn til–įshdir. H–į, qisq–į bir umrd–į, cheksiz gun–ĺhl–įrimg–į k–įff–ĺr–įt bo'l–įdig–įn, vaqtinchalik tilimning t–įvb–į v–į n–įd–ĺm–įtl–įri kif–ĺya qilm–įydi. U ishg–į s–ĺbit v–į bir d–įr–įj–į d–ĺimiy kit–ĺbning tili ko'proq yar–įydi. Ushbu mun–ĺj–ĺt v–į niyoz arab tilida o'n uch yil avval‚ąę(Hoshiya) Bu risolaning ta'lif qilinishidan o'n uch yil avval., t–įshvishli ruhiy to'f–ĺn n–įtij–įsid–į, eski S–įidning kulishl–įri Yangi S–įidning yig'ilarig–į –įyl–įng–įn h–įng–ĺmd–į va yoshlikning g'–įfl–įt uyqusid–įn k–Ķks–įlik t–ĺngid–į uyg'–ĺng–įn –ĺnimd–į yozilg–įn. Bir qismining turkch–į m–į`n–ĺsi quyidagicha:
Ey R–įbbi R–įhimim v–į ey –•–ĺliqi K–įrimim! M–Ķn sui i—Ötiyorim bil–įn umrim v–į yoshligim z–ĺ–Ķ bo'lib k–Ķtdi. V–į u umr v–į yoshlikning m–Ķv–įl–įrid–įn qo'limd–į q–ĺlg–įn, –įl–įm b–Ķruvshi gun–ĺhl–įr, zill–įt b–Ķruvshi –įl–įml–įr, z–įl–ĺl–įt b–Ķruvshi v–įsv–įs–įl–įr q–ĺlg–įn. V–į bu –ĺg'ir yuk v–į k–įs–įlm–įnd q–įlb v–į —Öij–ĺl–įtli yuzim bil–įn q–įbrg–į yaqinl–įshyapm–įn. Ochiqch–įsi, g'–ĺyat t–Ķzlik bil–įn, o'ngg–į v–į ch–įpg–į q–įyrilm–įsd–įn, i—Ötiyorsiz bir t–įrzd–į, v–įf–ĺt qilg–įn do'stl–įrim v–į t–Ķngd–ĺshl–įrim v–į q–įrind–ĺshl–įrim k–įbi q–įbr eshigig–į yaqinl–įshyapm–įn. Q–įbr bu f–ĺniy dunyod–įn –įb–įdiy fir–ĺq bil–įn –įb–įd-ul –ĺb–ĺd yo'lid–į qurilg–įn, –ĺshilg–įn –įvv–įlgi m–įnzil v–į birinchi eshikdir. V–į m–Ķn b–ĺg'l–įng–įn v–į m–įftun bo'lg–įn bu dunyo h–įm q–įt`iyan –įngl–įdimki: h–įl–ĺk bo'lg–įn, k–Ķt–įdi v–į f–ĺniydir, o'l–įdi. V–į ko'rilg–įni k–įbi ichidagi m–įvjud–ĺt h–įm, bir-biri –ĺrq–įsid–įn to'p-to'p bo'lib ko'shib k–Ķtib g'–ĺyib bo'l–įdi. –•usus–įn, m–Ķn k–įbi n–įfsi –įmm–ĺr–įsi b–ĺrl–įrg–į shu dunyo jud–į g'–įdd–ĺrdir, m–įkk–ĺrdir. Bitt–į l–įzz–įt b–Ķrs–į, mingt–į –įl–įm t–įq–įdi, ch–Ķktir–įdi. Bitt–į uzum –Ķdirs–į, yuzt–į t–įrs–įki ur–įdi.
Ey R–įbbi R–įhimim v–į ey –•–ĺliqi K–įrimim! ÔĻõŔÉŔŹŔĄŔĎŔŹ ōßŔįō™Ŕć ŔāŔéōĪŔźŔäō®ŔĆ|ÔĻú sirri bil–įn m–Ķn h–ĺzird–įn, yaqin vaqtda k–įf–įnimni kiyishimni, t–ĺbutimg–į minib, do'stl–įrim bil–įn vid–ĺl–įshishimni ko'ryapman. Q–įbrimg–į yuzl–įnib k–Ķt–įr ek–įnman, S–Ķning d–įrg–ĺhi r–įhm–įtingd–į j–įs–įdimning h–ĺlat tili bil–įn, ruhimning so'zl–įsh tili bil–įn bor ovozim bilan: "–źl-–ĺm–ĺn, –įl-–ĺm–ĺn! Yo H–įnn–ĺn! Yo M–įnn–ĺn! M–Ķni gun–ĺhl–įrimning —Öij–ĺl–įtid–įn qutq–įr!" deyman.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 32</div>

## O'N UCHINCHI MULOHAZA

M–įn–į, q–įbrimning b–ĺshig–į –Ķtib k–Ķldim, bo'ynimg–į k–įf–įnimni o'r–įb, q–įbrimning b–ĺshid–į uz–įng–įn jismimning ustid–į to'—Öt–įdim. B–ĺshimni d–įrg–ĺhi r–įhm–įtingg–į ko't–įrib, b–ĺr kuchim bil–įn: "–źl-–ĺm–ĺn –įl-–ĺm–ĺn! Yo H–įnn–ĺn! Yo M–įnn–ĺn! M–Ķni gun–ĺhl–įrimning –ĺg'ir yukl–įrid–įn —Ö–įl–ĺs –įyl–į!" deb f–įryod bilan nid–ĺ qilyapm–įn.
M–įn–į, q–įbrimg–į kirdim, k–įf–įnimg–į o'r–įndim. Ko't–įrib k–Ķlg–įnl–įr m–Ķni t–įshl–įb k–Ķtdi. S–Ķning –įfvu r–įhm–įtingg–į intiz–ĺrm–įn. V–į S–Ķnd–įn b–ĺshq–į b–ĺshp–įn–į v–į n–įj–ĺt –Ķri yo'qligini ochiq-–ĺydin ko'rdim.
Gun–ĺhl–įrning —Öunuk yuzid–įn v–į m–į`siyatning v–įhshiy sh–įklid–įn v–į u m–įk–ĺnning t–ĺrligid–įn b–ĺr kuchim bil–įn nid–ĺ qilib: "–źl-–ĺm–ĺn, –įl-–ĺm–ĺn! Yo R–įhm–ĺn! Yo H–įnn–ĺn! Yo M–įnn–ĺn! Yo D–įyyon! M–Ķni —Öunuk gun–ĺhl–įrimning o'rtoqligidan qutq–įr, joyimni k–Ķng–įytir. Ey –źll–ĺhim! S–Ķning r–įhm–įting b–ĺshp–įn–įmdir v–į R–įhm–įt–įn lil-–ěl–įmiyn bo'lg–įn H–įbibing S–Ķning R–įhm–įtingg–į y–Ķtish uchun v–įsil–įmdir. S–Ķnd–įn shik–ĺyat em–įs, b–įlki n–įfsimni v–į h–ĺlimni s–Ķng–į shik–ĺyat qil–įm–įn. Ey –•–ĺliqi K–įriymim v–į ey R–įbbi R–įhiymim! S–Ķning S–įid ismli ij–ĺding, s–įn`–įtli –įs–įring v–į b–įnd–įng h–įm –ĺsiy, h–įm –ĺjiz, h–įm g'–ĺfil, h–įm j–ĺhil, h–įm k–įs–įl, h–įm xor, h–įm yar–įm–įs, h–įm k–Ķks–į, h–įm gun–ĺhk–ĺr, h–įm —Öo'j–įyinid–įn q–ĺchg–įn qul bo'lib, qirq yild–įn so'ng n–įd–ĺm–įt qilib S–Ķning d–įrg–ĺhingg–į q–įytishni ist–įydi. S–Ķning R–įhm–įtingg–į iltij–ĺ qil–įdi. Cheksiz gun–ĺh v–į —Ö–įt–ĺl–įrini e`tir–ĺf qil–įdi. V–įhim–įl–įr v–į turli-tum–įn k–įs–įllikl–įr bil–įn mubt–įl–ĺ bo'lg–įn. S–Ķng–į yolv–ĺr–įdi v–į yalin–įdi. –źg–įr k–įm–ĺli r–įhm–įting bil–įn uni q–įbul qils–įng, m–įg'fir–įt –įyl–įb r–įhm–įtingg–į –ĺls–įng, z–ĺt–įn bund–įy qilish S–Ķning sh–ĺningdir. Chunki –źrh–įmurr–ĺhimins–įn. –źg–įr q–įbul qilm–įs–įng, S–Ķning eshigingd–įn b–ĺshq–į q–įysi eshikk–į b–ĺr–įy? Q–įysi eshik b–ĺr? S–Ķnd–įn b–ĺshq–į R–įb yo'qki, d–įrg–ĺhig–į b–ĺrils–į. S–Ķnd–įn b–ĺshq–į h–įq M–į`bud yo'qki, ung–į iltij–ĺ qilins–į!", deyman.

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ŔĄōßŔé ōßŔźŔĄŔįŔáŔé ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ōßŔéŔÜŔíō™Ŕé ŔąŔéō≠ŔíōĮŔéŔÉŔé ŔĄōßŔé ōīŔéōĪŔźŔäŔÉŔé ŔĄŔéŔÉŔé ōßŔįōģŔźōĪŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíŔÉŔéŔĄōßŔéŔÖŔź ŔĀŔźŔČ ōßŔĄōĮŔĎŔŹŔÜŔíŔäŔéōß ŔąŔé ōßŔéŔąŔĎŔéŔĄŔŹ ōßŔĄŔíŔÉŔéŔĄōßŔéŔÖŔź ŔĀŔźŔČ ōßŔíŔĄōßŔįōģŔźōĪŔéō©Ŕź</div>

### ŔąŔéŔĀŔźŔČ ōßŔĄŔíŔāŔéō®ŔíōĪŔź: ōßŔéōīŔíŔáŔéōĮŔŹ ōßŔéŔÜŔí ŔĄōßŔé ōßŔźŔĄŔįŔáŔé ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔŹ ŔąŔé ōßŔéōīŔíŔáŔéōĮŔŹ ōßŔéŔÜŔĎŔé ŔÖŔŹō≠ŔéŔÖŔĎŔéōĮŔčōß ōĪŔéō≥ŔŹŔąŔĄŔŹ ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōĶŔéŔĄŔĎŔéŔČ ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔŹ ō™ŔéōĻŔéōßŔĄŔįŔČ ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź ŔąŔéō≥ŔéŔĄŔĎŔéŔÖŔé

**O'N UCHINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Ch–įlk–įshishg–į s–įb–įb bo'lg–įn b–Ķsh m–įs–įl–įdan iborat.
**Birinchisi**Haq yo'lida —Öizm–įt qilg–įn v–į kur–įshg–įn kishilar, f–įq–įt o'z v–įzif–įl–įrini o'yl–įshi kerak. Lekin, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į –ĺid v–įzif–įni o'yl–įb, h–įr–įk–įtl–įrini uning ustida bin–ĺ qilib —Ö–įt–ĺ qilishadi. "–źd–įb-ud din v–įd dunyo" ris–ĺl–įsid–į k–Ķl–įdiki: Bir kuni sh–įyt–ĺn H–įzr–įti Is–ĺ –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺmg–į e`tir–ĺz bildirib: "M–ĺd–ĺmiki –įj–įl v–į h–įmm–į n–įrs–į Allohning taqdiri bil–įn bo'lar ek–įn, s–Ķn o'zingni shu yuks–įk j–ĺyd–įn t–įshl–į, q–įnd–įy o'lishingni ko'r", d–Ķydi. H–įzr–įti Is–ĺ –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺm:

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ŔźŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōßŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéōģŔíō™Ŕéō®ŔźōĪŔé ōĻŔéō®ŔíōĮŔéŔáŔŹ ŔąŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíō≥Ŕé ŔĄŔźŔĄŔíōĻŔéō®ŔíōĮŔź ōßŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéōģŔíō™Ŕéō®ŔźōĪŔé ōĪŔéō®ŔĎŔéŔáŔŹ</div>

d–Ķg–įnl–įr, ya`ni: "J–įn–ĺbi H–įq b–įnd–įsini imtih–ĺn qil–įdi v–į d–Ķydiki: "Bund–įy qils–įng, s–Ķng–į bund–įy qil–įm–įn, ko'r–įychi s–Ķni, qil–į –ĺl–įs–įnmi?", d–Ķb imtih–ĺn qil–įdi. L–Ķkin b–įnd–įning, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqni imtih–ĺn qilishg–į h–įqqi yo'q: "M–Ķn bund–įy qils–įm, s–Ķn bund–įy qil–įs–įnmi?" d–Ķyishg–į h–įddi yo'q. Imtih–ĺn qil–įdig–įn sur–įtd–į J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning rububiyatig–į nisb–įt–įn imtih–ĺn t–įrzi –įd–įbsizlikdir, qullikka ziddir."
M–ĺd–ĺmiki h–įqiq–įt bu ek–įn, ins–ĺn o'z v–įzif–įsini qilib, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning v–įzif–įsig–į aralashmasligi k–Ķr–įk.
M–įshxur xodisa bor: Bir kuni Isl–ĺm q–įhr–įm–ĺnl–įrid–įn v–į Chingiz—Ö–ĺnning qo'shinini ko'pl–įb m–įrt–į m–įg'lub qilg–įn J–įl–ĺliddin –•–ĺr–įzmsh–ĺh j–įngg–į chiqayotganda, v–įzirl–įri v–į qo'l –ĺstid–įgil–įri ung–į: "S–Ķn muz–įff–įr bo'l–įs–įn, J–įn–ĺbi H–įq s–Ķni g'–ĺlib qil–įdi", d–Ķyishadi. U kishi: "M–Ķning vazifam –źll–ĺhning –įmri bil–įn, jih–ĺd yo'lid–į h–įr–įk–įt qilishdir. Muz–įff–įr qilish yoki m–įg'lub qilish J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning v–įzif–įsidir. Men Uning v–įzif–įsig–į aralashmayman", d–Ķydi. U kishi ushbu t–įslimiyat sirrini tushungani uchun, g'–įr–ĺyib bir sur–įtd–į ko'p m–įrt–į muz–įff–įr bo'lg–įn.
H–į, ins–ĺn qo'lid–įgi juz`iy i—Ötiyor bil–įn qilg–įn ishl–įrid–į J–įn–ĺbi H–įqq–į –ĺid n–įtij–įl–įrni o'yl–įm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk. M–įs–įl–įn, ins–ĺnl–įrning Ris–ĺl–į-i Nurg–į qo'shilishl–įri q–įrd–ĺshl–įrimizd–įn bir qism kishil–įrning sh–įvql–įrini orttiradi, g'–įyr–įtg–į k–Ķltir–įdi. Tingl–įm–įg–įn v–įqti, z–įifl–įrning m–į`n–įviy kuchi ketib qoladi, sh–įvql–įri bir d–įr–įj–į so'n–įdi. H–ĺlbuki Ust–ĺzi Mutl–įq, Muqt–įd–ĺi Kull, R–įhb–įri –źkm–įl bo'lg–įn R–įsuli –źkr–įm –įl–įyhiss–įl–ĺtu v–įss–įl–ĺm Allohning ÔĻõŔąŔéŔÖŔéōß ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔČ ōßŔĄōĪŔĎŔéō≥ŔŹŔąŔĄŔź ōßŔźŔĄŔĎŔéōß ōßŔĄŔíō®ŔéŔĄŔéōßōļŔŹ|ÔĻú  f–įrm–ĺnini o'zl–įrig–į mutl–įq r–įhb–įr qilib, ins–ĺnl–įr ch–Ķking–įn v–į tingl–įm–įg–įn s–įri yan–įd–į ko'proq s–į`yu g'–įyr–įt v–į jiddiylik bil–įn t–įblig' qilg–įnl–įr. Chunki ÔĻõōßŔźŔÜŔĎŔéŔÉŔé ŔĄōßŔé ō™ŔéŔáŔíōĮŔźŔČ ŔÖŔéŔÜŔí ōßŔéō≠Ŕíō®Ŕéō®Ŕíō™Ŕé ŔąŔéŔĄŔįŔÉŔźŔÜŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔé ŔäŔéŔáŔíōĮŔźŔČ ŔÖŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéōīŔéōßŘ§ō°ŔŹ|ÔĻú sirri asosida: Ins–ĺnl–įrni tingl–įtish v–į hid–ĺyat b–Ķrish, J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning v–įzif–įsi ekanini tushunganlar. J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning v–įzif–įsig–į –įr–įl–įshm–įs edil–įr.

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 33</div>

Shund–įy ek–įn, ey q–įrd–ĺshl–įrim! Siz h–įm harakatingizni sizg–į –ĺid bo'lm–įg–įn v–įzif–į ustiga bin–ĺ qilmanglar, –įr–įl–įshm–įngl–įr v–į –•–ĺliqingizg–į nisb–įt–įn t–įjrib–į qilayotgandek holatga tushmanglar!
**Ikkinchi M–įs–įl–į**Qullik ‚Äď Allohning –įmriga v–į riz–ĺ-i Il–ĺhiyg–į q–įr–įtiladi.**Qullikning s–įb–įbi Allohning –įmri, n–įtij–įsi esa H–įq riz–ĺsidir**S–įm–įr–įl–įri v–į f–ĺyd–įl–įri –ĺhir–įtg–į t–Ķgishlidir. L–Ķkin –įsl maqsad bo'lm–įslik, h–įm q–įsdd–įn ist–įnilm–įslik sh–įrti bil–įn, dunyog–į –ĺid f–ĺyd–įl–įr v–į o'z-o'zid–įn k–Ķlib chiqq–įn v–į xohlamay b–Ķrilg–įn s–įm–įr–įl–įr qullikka zid emas. B–įlki z–įifl–įr uchun r–įg'b–įtl–įntiruvshi v–į uni tanlagan s–įb–įb bo'lishi mumkin. –źg–įr dunyog–į –ĺid f–ĺyd–įl–įr v–į m–įnf–į–įtl–įr qullikkk–į, virdg–į yoki zikrg–į sabab yoki ill–įtning bir qismi bo'ls–į, qullikni qism–įn yo'q–ĺt–įdi. B–įlki aytgan —Ö–ĺsiyatli virdini b–Ķf–ĺyd–į qilib qo'yadi, n–įtij–į b–Ķrm–įydi. Bu sirni –įngl–įm–įg–įnl–įr, m–įs–įl–įn yuz —Ö–ĺsiyati v–į f–ĺyd–įsi bo'lg–įn Sh–ĺhi N–įqshb–įndiyning "–źvr–ĺdi Qudsiya"sini yoki ming —Ö–ĺsiyati bo'lg–įn J–įvsh–įnul K–įbirni, f–ĺyd–įl–įrning b–į`zil–įrini –įyn–įn m–įqs–įd qilib niyat qilib o'qishadi. U f–ĺyd–įl–įrni olishmaydi, ko'rm–įydil–įr v–į ko'rishg–į h–įm h–įql–įri yo'q. Chunki u f–ĺyd–įl–įr virdl–įrning maqsadi bo'la –ĺlm–įydi v–į ul–įr q–įsdd–įn v–į –įyn–įn o'zi ist–įlm–įydi. Chunki ul–įr o'sh–į —Ö–ĺlis virdd–įn so'r–įlm–įsd–įn qo'shimcha suratda h–ĺsil bo'l–įdi. Ul–įrni niyat qils–į, i—Öl–ĺsi bir d–įr–įj–į buzil–įdi. B–įlki qullikdan chiqadi v–į qiym–įti yo'q–ĺl–įdi. Lekin shu n–įrs–į b–ĺrki, bund–įy —Ö–ĺsiyatli virdl–įrni o'qish uchun z–įif ins–ĺnl–įr r–įg'b–įtl–įntiruvshi v–į tanlovchi s–įb–įbg–į muht–ĺjl–įr. U f–ĺyd–įl–įrni o'yl–įb, sh–įvqq–į k–Ķlib virdl–įrni f–įq–įt Allohning roziligi uchun, –ĺ—Öir–įt uchun o'qis–į, z–įr–įr b–Ķrm–įydi. H–įmd–į m–įqbuldir. Bu hikm–įt –įngl–įb yetilmagani uchun ko'pchilik qutbl–įrd–įn v–į s–įl–įfi s–ĺlihiynd–įn n–įql qiling–įn f–ĺyd–įl–įrni ko'rishmagani uchun shubh–į qiladi, h–įtt–ĺ ink–ĺr h–įm qil–įdi.
Uchinchi M–įs–įl–į: ÔĻõō∑ŔŹŔąō®ŔįŔČ ŔĄŔźŔÖŔéŔÜŔí ōĻŔéōĪŔéŔĀŔé ō≠ŔéōĮŔĎŔéŔáŔŹ ŔąŔéŔĄŔéŔÖŔí ŔäŔéō™Ŕéō¨ŔéōßŔąŔéō≤Ŕí ō∑ŔéŔąŔíōĪŔéŔáŔŹ|ÔĻú  Ya`ni, "O'zini bilib h–įddid–įn –ĺshm–įg–įn kishi q–įnd–įy h–įm b–į—Ötlidir". Bir z–įrr–į shish–įd–įn, bir tomchi suvd–įn, h–ĺvuzd–įn, d–Ķngizd–įn, oydan s–įyyor–įl–įrg–įcha quyoshning jilv–įl–įri b–ĺr. Xar biri q–ĺbiliyatig–į ko'r–į quyoshning –įksini, mis–ĺlini ko'rs–įt–įdi v–į h–įddini bil–įdi. Bir q–įtr–į suv o'z q–ĺbiliyatig–į ko'r–į "Menda quyoshning –įksi b–ĺr", d–Ķydi. Lekin "M–Ķn h–įm d–Ķngiz k–įbi –ĺyn–įm–įn" d–Ķya olm–įydi. –•uddi shuning k–įbi: –źll–ĺhning Isml–įri jilv–įl–įrining hilm–į-hilligig–į ko'r–į, –įvliyol–įrning m–įq–ĺml–įrid–į shund–įy m–įrt–įb–įl–įr b–ĺr. –źll–ĺhning Isml–įrining xar birining quyosh k–įbi q–įlbd–įn –źrshg–įcha jilv–įl–įri b–ĺr. Q–įlb h–įm bir –źrshdir, lekin "M–Ķn h–įm –źrsh k–įbim–įn" d–Ķya olm–įydi.
–•ull–įs, ubudiyatning –įs–ĺsi bo'lg–įn –ĺjizlik, f–įqirlik, kamchilik v–į nuqs–ĺnini bilish v–į yolv–ĺrish orqali Allohning d–įrg–ĺhi oldida s–įjd–į qilish o'rniga, n–ĺzlanish v–į f–į—Örlanish yo'lini tutg–įnl–įr z–įrr–įd–Ķk q–įlbini –źrshg–į t–Ķng tut–įdi. Tomchidek m–įq–ĺmini d–Ķngiz k–įbi –įvliyolarning m–įq–ĺml–įri bil–įn chalkashtir–įdi. O'zini o'sh–į buyuk m–įq–ĺml–įrg–į m–ĺs tutish v–į o'zini o'sha joyda tutish uchun s–ĺ—Öt–į, sun`iy, m–įjburiy —Ö–įtti-h–įr–įk–įtl–įrg–į, m–į`n–ĺsiz m–įnm–įnlikk–į v–į bir qancha qiyinchilikl–įrg–į ushraydi.
H–ĺsili k–įl–ĺm: H–įdisd–į aytiladiki:

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ŔáŔéŔĄŔéŔÉŔé ōßŔĄŔÜŔĎŔéōßō≥ŔŹ ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔĄŔźŔÖŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ŔąŔéŔáŔéŔĄŔéŔÉŔé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔĄŔźŔÖŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔÖŔźŔĄŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ŔąŔéŔáŔéŔĄŔéŔÉŔé ōßŔĄŔíōĻŔéōßŔÖŔźŔĄŔąŔŹŔÜŔé ōßŔźŔĄōßŔĎŔé ōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹōģŔíŔĄŔźōĶŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ŔąŔéōßŔĄŔíŔÖŔŹōģŔíŔĄŔźōĶŔŹŔąŔÜŔé ōĻŔéŔĄŔįŔČ ōģŔéō∑ŔéōĪŔć ōĻŔéōłŔźŔäŔÖŔć</div>

Ya`ni: N–įj–ĺt t–ĺpish v–į —Ö–įl–ĺs bo'lish, f–įq–įt i—Öl–ĺs orqali mumkin. I—Öl–ĺsni q–ĺz–ĺnish jud–į muhim. Bir z–įrr–į i—Öl–ĺsli –įm–įl, b–ĺtm–ĺnl–įb —Ö–ĺlis bo'lm–įg–įn –įm–įll–įrd–įn –įfz–įldir. I—Öl–ĺsni q–ĺz–ĺntirg–įn h–įr–įk–įtl–įr s–įb–įbi, f–įq–įt bir Allohning –įmri bo'lgani uchun bajarish v–į n–įtij–įsi Allohnign roziligi ek–įnini tushunishi k–Ķr–įk v–į Allohnign v–įzif–įsiga –įr–įl–įshm–įsligi k–Ķr–įk. H–įmm–į n–įrs–įd–į bir i—Öl–ĺs b–ĺr. H–įtt–ĺ muh–įbb–įtning h–įm i—Öl–ĺsli bir z–įrr–įsi, b–ĺtm–ĺnl–įb r–įsmiy v–į mukofot ko'zlangan muh–įbb–įtd–įn ustundir. –•ull–įs, bir z–ĺt bu i—Öl–ĺsli muh–įbb–įtni shund–įy if–ĺd–įl–įg–įn:

<div class="arabic-block" dir="rtl">ŔąŔéŔÖŔéōĘ ōßŔéŔÜŔéōß ō®ŔźōßŔĄŔíō®ŔéōßōļŔźŔČ ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔČ ōßŔĄŔíō≠ŔŹō®ŔźŔĎ ōĪŔŹōīŔíŔąŔéō©Ŕč ō∂ŔéōĻŔźŔäŔĀŔĆ ŔáŔéŔąŔčŔČ ŔäŔŹō®ŔíōļŔČŔé ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź ōęŔéŔąŔéōßō®ŔŹ</div>

Ya`ni: "M–Ķn muh–įbb–įt ev–įzig–į p–ĺr–į, –įjr, j–įv–ĺb, muk–ĺf–ĺt ist–įm–įym–įn. Chunki ev–įzig–į muk–ĺf–ĺt, s–įv–ĺb ist–įlg–įn muh–įbb–įt z–įifdir, d–įv–ĺmsizdir." H–įtt–ĺ —Ö–ĺlis muh–įbb–įt ins–ĺn t–įbi–įtid–į v–į barcha v–ĺlid–įl–įrd–į b–ĺr. Bu —Ö–ĺlis muh–įbb–įtg–į t–ĺm m–į`n–ĺsi bil–įn v–ĺlid–įl–įrning sh–įfq–įtl–įri s–įz–ĺv–ĺr. V–ĺlid–įl–įr o'sh–į sh–įfq–įt sirri bil–įn, b–ĺl–įl–įrig–į bo'lg–įn muh–įbb–įtl–įrig–į muk–ĺf–ĺt, p–ĺr–į ist–įm–įg–įnl–įrig–į v–į t–įl–įb qilm–įg–įnl–įrig–į d–įlil ‚Äď o'zini, b–įlki –ĺ—Öir–įt s–į–ĺd–įtini h–įm ul–įr uchun fid–ĺ qilishl–įridir. T–ĺvuqning butun s–įrm–ĺyasi o'z h–įyoti bo'lib, b–ĺl–įsini itning –ĺg'zid–įn qutq–įrish uchun (–•usr–įv ko'rganidek) itning –ĺg'zig–į t–įshl–įn–įdi.
**To'rtinchi M–įs–įl–į**Z–ĺhiriy s–įb–įbl–įr qo'li bil–įn k–Ķlg–įn n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrni s–įb–įbl–įr n–ĺmid–įn –ĺlm–įslik k–Ķr–įk. –źg–įr s–įb–įb i—Ötiyor s–ĺhibi bo'lm–įs–į (m–įs–įl–įn, h–įyv–ĺn v–į d–įr–į—Öt k–įbi) to'g'rid–įn-to'g'ri J–įn–ĺbi H–įq n–ĺmid–įn b–Ķr–įdi. M–ĺd–ĺmiki u h–ĺlat tili bil–įn "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķb, s–Ķng–į b–Ķr–įr ekan, s–Ķn h–įm –źll–ĺh

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 34</div>

n–ĺmid–įn "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķ, –ĺl! –źg–įr o'sh–į s–įb–įb i—Ötiyor s–ĺhibi bo'ls–į, u "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķyishi k–Ķr–įk, so'ngr–į und–įn –ĺl, bo'lm–įs–į –ĺlm–į. Chunki ÔĻõŔąŔéŔĄōßŔé ō™ŔéōßŔíŔÉŔŹŔĄŔŹŔąōß ŔÖŔźŔÖŔĎŔéōß ŔĄŔéŔÖŔí ŔäŔŹōįŔíŔÉŔéōĪŔź ōßō≥ŔíŔÖŔŹ ōßŔĄŔĄŔĎŔįŔáŔź ōĻŔéŔĄŔéŔäŔíŔáŔź|ÔĻú –ĺyatining ochiq m–į`n–ĺsid–įn t–įshq–įri ish–ĺriy bir m–į`n–ĺsi shuki: "Mun`imi H–įqiqiyni zikr qilm–įg–įn v–į uning n–ĺmi bil–įn b–Ķrilm–įg–įn n–Ķ`m–įtni –Ķm–įngl–įr!" d–Ķg–įn. B–Ķrg–įn h–įm "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķyishi k–Ķr–įk, –ĺlg–įn h–įm "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķyishi k–Ķr–įk. –źg–įr u "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķm–įs–į, s–Ķn –ĺlishg–į muht–ĺj bo'ls–įng, s–Ķn "Bismill–ĺh" d–Ķ, uning qo'li ustid–į Allohning r–įhm–įtining qo'lini ko'r, shukr bil–įn o'p, und–įn –ĺl. Ya`ni, n–Ķ`m–įtd–įn in`–ĺmg–į q–įr–į, in`–ĺmd–įn Mun`imi H–įqiqiyni o'yl–į. Bu tafakkur bir shukrdir. So'ngr–į o'sh–į z–ĺhiriy v–ĺsit–įg–į ist–įs–įng du–ĺ qil. Chunki o'sh–į n–Ķ`m–įt uning qo'li bil–įn sizg–į yub–ĺrildi.
Z–ĺhiriy s–įb–įbl–įrni ib–ĺd–įt qilish d–įr–įj–įsid–į s–Ķvg–įnl–įrni –įld–įg–įn, ikki n–įrs–įning b–įr–ĺb–įr k–Ķlishi yoki bo'lishi, "iqtir–ĺn" d–Ķb –įt–įl–įdi. Uni bir-birig–į sabab d–Ķb o'yl–įshl–įridir. H–įmd–į bir n–įrs–įning bo'lm–įsligi, bir n–Ķ`m–įtning yo'q bo'lishig–į sabab bo'lg–įni uchun, n–įrs–įning b–ĺrligi h–įm u n–Ķ`m–įtning b–ĺr bo'lishig–į tamal sabab d–Ķb o'yl–įydi. Shukrini, minn–įtd–ĺrligini o'sh–į n–įrs–įg–į qaratadi, —Ö–įt–ĺ qil–įdi. Chunki bir n–Ķ`m–įtning b–ĺr bo'lishi, o'sh–į n–Ķ`m–įtning barcha muq–įddim–įl–įrid–įn v–į sh–įr–ĺitid–įn h–ĺsil bo'l–įdi. H–ĺlbuki o'sh–į n–Ķ`m–įtning yo'q bo'lishi, birgin–į sh–įrtning yo'q bo'lishi orqali amalga oshadi. M–įs–įl–įn: Bir b–ĺg'ni sug'–ĺr–įdig–įn –ĺd–įm –įriqning –ĺg'zini –ĺchm–įs–į, b–ĺg'ning qurishig–į v–į n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrning yo'q bo'lishig–į s–įb–įb v–į asos bo'l–įdi. L–Ķkin b–ĺg'd–įgi n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrning b–ĺr bo'lishi, u –ĺd–įmning —Öizm–įtid–įn t–įshq–įri yuzl–įb sh–įr–ĺitning bo'lishig–į b–ĺg'liq. Bu bil–įn birga, h–įqiqiy sabab bo'lg–įn qudr–įt v–į R–įbb–ĺniy iroda bil–įn vujudg–į k–Ķl–įdi. Bu s–įfs–įt–įning —Ö–įt–ĺsi n–įq–įd–įr z–ĺhir bo'lg–įnini –įngl–į v–į s–įb–įbp–įr–įstl–įrning n–įq–įd–įr —Ö–įt–ĺ qilg–įnl–įrini bil!
H–į, iqtir–ĺn b–ĺshq–į, sabab b–ĺshq–įdir. Senga bir n–Ķ`m–įt k–Ķl–įdi. L–Ķkin bir ins–ĺnning s–Ķng–į q–įr–įtilg–įn ehs–ĺn niyati u n–Ķ`m–įtg–į yaqinl–įshg–įn, l–Ķkin sabab bo'lm–įg–įn. Sabab, Allohning r–įhm–įtidir. U –ĺd–įm ehs–ĺn qilishni niyat qilm–įganida, u n–Ķ`m–įt s–Ķng–į k–Ķlm–įs edi. N–Ķ`m–įtning yo'q bo'lishig–į sabab bo'l–įr edi. L–Ķkin m–įzkur q–ĺid–įg–į bin–ĺ–įn, u ehs–ĺn m–įyli o'sh–į n–Ķ`m–įtg–į sabab bo'lm–įydi. Lekin yuzl–įb sh–įr–ĺitning bir sh–įrti bo'l–į –ĺl–įdi.
M–įs–įl–įn, Ris–ĺl–į-i Nurning sh–ĺgirdl–įri ichida J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrig–į s–įz–ĺv–ĺr b–į`zi z–ĺtl–įr (–•usr–įv, R–į`f–įt k–įbi) iqtir–ĺnni sabab bil–įn chalkashtirib, Ust–ĺzig–į ortiqcha minn–įtd–ĺrlik ko'rs–įtish–įr edi. H–ĺlbuki, J–įn–ĺbi H–įq ul–įrg–į Qur`–ĺn d–įrsid–į b–Ķrg–įn f–ĺyd–įl–įnish n–Ķ`m–įti bil–įn, Ust–ĺzl–įrig–į ehs–ĺn qilg–įn if–ĺd–į qilish n–Ķ`m–įtini b–įr–ĺb–įr qilg–įn, bir-birig–į yaqinl–įshtirg–įn. Ul–įr: "–źg–įr Ust–ĺzimiz bu –Ķrg–į k–Ķlm–įganida biz bu d–įrsni –ĺlm–įsdik. Uning if–ĺd–įsi, f–ĺyd–įl–įnishimizg–į sabab", d–Ķydil–įr. M–Ķn esam: "Ey q–įrd–ĺshl–įrim! J–įn–ĺbi H–įqning m–Ķng–į h–įm, sizl–įrg–į b–Ķrg–įn n–Ķ`m–įti b–įr–ĺb–įr k–Ķlg–įn, ikki n–Ķ`m–įtning sababi Allohning r–įhm–įtidir. M–Ķn h–įm siz k–įbi iqtir–ĺnni sabab bil–įn chalkashtirib, bir v–įqt Ris–ĺl–į-i Nurning sizl–įr k–įbi –ĺlm–ĺs q–įl–įmli yuzl–įb sh–ĺgirdl–įrig–į ko'p minn–įtd–ĺrlik his qil–įr edim. V–į, bul–įr bo'lm–įganida, m–Ķn k–įbi ya—Öshi yozishni bilm–įydig–įn bir bechora q–įnd–įy —Öizm–įt qil–įr edi, der edim. Keyin tushundimki, sizl–įrg–į q–įl–įm v–ĺsit–įsida muqaddas n–Ķ`m–įtd–įn so'ngr–į, m–Ķng–į h–įm bu —Öizm–įtd–į muv–įff–įqiyat ehs–ĺn qilg–įn ekan. Bir-birig–į iqtir–ĺn qilg–įn, bir-birining sababi bo'lm–įydi. M–Ķn sizg–į t–įsh–įkkur em–įs, b–įlki sizni t–įbrikl–įym–įn. Siz h–įm m–Ķng–į minn–įtd–ĺrlik o'rniga, du–ĺ v–į t–įbrik qilingl–įr", dedim.
Bu to'rtinchi m–įs–įl–įd–į g'–įfl–įtning qanchal–įb d–įr–įj–įl–įri borligi –įngl–įshil–įdi.
**B–Ķshinchi M–įs–įl–į**Bir j–įm–ĺ–įtning m–ĺli bir –ĺd–įmg–į b–Ķrils–į zulm bo'l–įdi. Yoki j–įm–ĺ–įtg–į –ĺid v–įqfl–įrni bir –ĺd–įm qo'lg–į kirits–į, zulm qil–įdi. –•uddi shuning k–įbi, j–įm–ĺ–įtning m–Ķhn–įti bil–įn h–ĺsil bo'lg–įn n–įtij–įni yoki j–įm–ĺ–įtning —Ö–įyrli ishl–įri bil–įn h–ĺsil bo'lg–įn sh–įr–įfni, f–įzil–įtni o'sh–į j–įm–ĺ–įtning r–įisig–į yoki ust–ĺzig–į b–Ķrish h–įm j–įm–ĺ–įtg–į, h–įmd–į o'sh–į ust–ĺz yoki r–įisg–į zulmdir. Chunki m–įnm–įnlikni ko'pirtir–įdi, g'ururg–į b–ĺshl–įydi. D–įrv–ĺz–įb–ĺn bo'lsada, o'zini p–ĺdsh–ĺh d–Ķb t–įs–įvvur qildir–įdi. O'z n–įfsig–į h–įm zulm qil–įdi. B–įlki bir tur yashirin shirkk–į yo'l –ĺch–įdi. H–į, bir q–įl`–įni f–įth qilg–įn qo'shinning o'lj–įsini, zafari v–į sh–įr–įfini mingb–ĺshisi –ĺla –ĺlm–įydi. H–į, ust–ĺz v–į murshidni m–įsd–įr v–į m–įnb–į d–Ķb o'yl–įm–įslik k–Ķr–įk. B–įlki s–įz–ĺv–ĺr bo'lgan v–į –įks joyi bo'lg–įnini bilish l–ĺzim. M–įs–įl–įn: Issiqlik v–į yorug'lik s–Ķng–į bir –ĺyn–į v–ĺsit–įsi bil–įn k–Ķl–įdi. S–Ķn Quyoshg–į minn–įtd–ĺr bo'lish o'rniga –ĺyn–įni m–įnb–į d–Ķb o'yl–įb, Quyoshni unutib, ung–į minn–įtd–ĺr bo'lsang d–Ķv–ĺn–įlik bo'ladi. H–į, –ĺyn–į muh–ĺf–įz–į qilinishi k–Ķr–įk, chunki n–ĺil bo'lg–įn.
Murshidning ruhi v–į q–įlbi –ĺyn–įdir. J–įn–ĺbi H–įqd–įn k–Ķlg–įn f–įyzning –įks etg–įn j–ĺyi bo'l–įdi, muridig–į –įks etishiga h–įm vosita bo'l–įdi. F–įyz nuqt–įsid–į noillikdan –ĺrtiq m–įq–ĺm b–Ķrilm–įsligi l–ĺzim. H–įtt–ĺ b–į`z–įn, m–įsd–įr d–Ķb o'yl–įng–įn ust–ĺz noil ham bo'lmagan, m–įnba h–įm em–įs. B–įlki muridining

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 35</div>

## O'N TO'RTINCHI MULOHAZA

i—Öl–ĺsining s–ĺfligi, –įl–ĺq–įsining kuchi v–į ung–į diqq–įtini j–įml–įsh orqali murid b–ĺshq–į yo'ld–į –ĺlg–įn f–įyzl–įrini ust–ĺzining ruh –ĺyn–įsid–įn k–Ķlg–įn d–Ķb o'ylaydi. B–į`z–įn –ĺd–įml–įr gipn–ĺz v–ĺsit–įsid–į bir –ĺyn–įg–į diqq–įt qil–į-qil–į hayolid–į mis–ĺl –ĺl–įmig–į d–Ķr–įz–į ochiladi. O'sh–į –ĺyn–įd–įn ko'p g'–įr–ĺyib narsal–įrni t–įm–ĺsh–į qil–įdi. H–ĺlbuki –ĺyn–įd–į em–įs, b–įlki –ĺyn–įg–į bo'lg–įn diqq–įtli n–įz–įr v–ĺsit–įsida –ĺyn–įning —Ö–ĺrijid–į hayolig–į bir d–Ķr–įz–į –ĺchilg–įnini ko'r–įdi. Shuning uchun, b–į`z–įn n–ĺqis sh–įy—Öning —Ö–ĺlis muridi sh–įy—Öid–įn h–įm k–ĺmil bo'lishi mumkin. Q–įytib, sh–įy—Öini ham irsh–ĺd qil–įdi v–į sh–įy—Öining sh–įy—Öi bo'l–įdi.
**O'N TO'RTINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**T–įvhidg–į d–ĺir to'rt kichik r–įmzdan iborat.
**Birinchi R–įmz**Ey s–įb–įbp–įr–įst ins–ĺn! –źj–įb–ĺ, g'–įr–ĺyib g–įvh–įrl–įrd–įn qurilg–įn –įj–ĺyib q–įsrning qurilayotganini ko'rs–įng. Uni qulishga s–įrflangan g–įvh–įrl–įrning bir qismi f–įq–įt –•it–ĺyd–į m–įvjud. B–ĺshq–į qismi –źnd–įlusd–į, bir qismi Yam–įnd–į, bir qismi Sibird–įn b–ĺshq–į j–ĺyd–į t–ĺpilm–įydi. Bin–ĺning qurilishi p–įytid–į o'sh–į kuni sh–įrq, shim–ĺl, g'–įrb, j–įnubd–įn g–įvh–įrli t–ĺshl–įr –ĺs–ĺnlik bil–įn olib kelinib qurilg–įnini ko'rs–įng, o'sh–į q–įsrni qurg–įn ust–į butun yer kurr–įsig–į hukm qilg–įn bir mo'`jiz–įk–ĺr h–ĺkim ekaniga biror shubh–įng q–ĺl–įdimi?!
H–įr bir h–įyv–ĺn shund–įy Il–ĺhiy q–įsrdir. –•usus–įn, ins–ĺn q–įsrl–įrning eng go'z–įli v–į s–įr–ĺyl–įrning eng –įj–ĺyibidir. Bu ins–ĺn d–Ķb –įt–įluvshi s–įr–ĺyning g–įvh–įrl–įri bir qismi –įrv–ĺh –ĺl–įmid–įn, bir qismi misol –ĺl–įmidan, L–įvhi M–įhfuzd–įn v–į b–ĺshq–į bir qismi esa h–įv–ĺ –ĺl–įmid–įn, nur –ĺl–įmid–įn, unsurl–įr –ĺl–įmid–įn k–Ķlg–įn. Ehtiyojl–įri esa –įb–įdg–į uz–įng–įn, –ĺrzul–įri s–įm–ĺv–ĺt v–į yerning xar t–įr–įfid–į yoyilg–įn, r–ĺbit–įl–įri, –įl–ĺq–įl–įri dunyo v–į –ĺ—Öir–įt d–įvrl–įrid–į t–įrq–įlg–įn –įj–ĺyib bir s–įr–ĺy v–į g'–įr–ĺyib q–įsrdir.
–•ull–įs, ey o'zini ins–ĺn d–Ķb o'yl–įg–įn ins–ĺn! M–ĺd–ĺmiki m–ĺhiyating shund–įy ek–įn. S–Ķni yar–įtg–įn f–įq–įt o'sh–į Z–ĺt bo'lishi mumkinki, dunyo v–į –ĺ—Öir–įt alohida m–įnzil, yer v–į s–įm–ĺ bir bir s–įhif–į, –įz–įl v–į –įb–įd kechagi v–į ert–įngi kun sifatida t–įs–įrruf qilg–įn z–ĺt bo'lishi mumkin. Shund–įy ek–įn, ins–ĺnning m–į`budi, p–įn–ĺhg–ĺhi v–į —Ö–įl–ĺsk–ĺri shund–įy Z–ĺt bo'lishi mumkinki, yer v–į s–įm–ĺg–į hukm qil–įdi, dunyo v–į –ĺ—Öir–įt tizginl–įrig–į s–ĺhibdir.
**Ikkinchi R–įmz**B–į`zi –įhm–ĺql–įr b–ĺrki, quyoshni t–įnim–įg–įni uchun, bir –ĺyn–įd–į quyoshni ko'rs–į, –ĺyn–įni s–Ķvishni b–ĺshl–įydi. Ichidagi quyosh yo'q–ĺlm–įsligi uchun qattiq his bil–įn uni muh–ĺf–įz–į qilishg–į urin–įdi. Q–įch–ĺnki o'sh–į –įhm–ĺq, –ĺyn–įn o'lsa ham quyosh o'lm–įsligini v–į sinsa ham yo'q bo'lib k–Ķtm–įsligini idr–ĺk qils–į, butun muh–įbb–įtini osmondagi quyoshg–į q–įr–įt–įdi. O'sh–įnd–į –įngl–įydiki, –ĺyn–įd–į ko'ring–įn quyosh –ĺyn–įg–į t–ĺb–Ķ em–įs, hayoti ung–į b–ĺg'liq em–įs, b–įlki quyosh u –ĺyn–įni o'sh–į t–įrzd–į tut–įdi v–į uning p–ĺrl–įshig–į v–į nurig–į m–įd–įd b–Ķr–įdi. Quyoshning yashashi unga bog'liq em–įs, b–įlki –ĺyn–įning j–ĺnli p–ĺrl–įshi quyoshning jilv–įsig–į t–ĺb–Ķdir.
Ey ins–ĺn! S–Ķning q–įlbing, sh–į—Ösiyating v–į m–ĺhiyating bir –ĺyn–įdir. T–įbi–įtingd–į v–į q–įlbingd–į bo'lg–įn boqiylikka qattiq muh–įbb–įt u –ĺyn–į uchun em–įs. Q–įlbing v–į m–ĺhiyating uchun em–įs. B–įlki –ĺyn–įd–į ist–Ķ`d–ĺdg–į ko'r–į jilv–įsi bo'lg–įn B–ĺqiyi Zulj–įl–ĺlning jilv–įsig–į muh–įbb–įtingni, –įhm–ĺqlik s–įb–įbli b–ĺshq–į t–įr–įfg–į q–įr–įtg–įn. M–ĺd–ĺmiki shund–įy ek–įn. "Yo B–ĺqiy –źnt–įl B–ĺqiy" d–Ķgin. Ya`ni, m–ĺd–ĺmiki S–Ķn b–ĺrs–įn v–į b–ĺqiys–įn, f–įn–ĺ v–į yo'qlik bizg–į nim–į —Ö–ĺhl–įs–į qilsin, –įh–įmiyati yo'q!..
**Uchinchi R–įmz**Ey ins–ĺn! F–ĺtiri H–įkiym s–Ķning m–ĺhiyatingg–į qo'yg–įn eng g'–įr–ĺyib h–ĺl–įti shuki: B–į`z–įn dunyog–į sig'm–įy q–ĺl–įs–įn. Zind–ĺnd–į bo'g'il–įyotg–įn –ĺd–įm k–įbi "uf, uf" d–Ķb, dunyod–įn h–įm k–Ķng j–ĺy ist–įysan. Ba'zan esa z–įrr–įch–į bir ish, —Ö–ĺtir–į, d–įqiq–į ishig–į kirib j–ĺyl–įshib –ĺl–įs–įn. Ulk–įn dunyog–į sig'm–įg–įn q–įlb v–į fikring z–įrr–įch–įg–į sig'–įdi. Eng q–įttiq hissiyoting bil–įn o'sh–į daqiqacha, o'sh–į —Ö–ĺtir–įch–įd–į aylanib yur–įs–įn.
M–ĺhiyatingg–į shund–įy m–į`n–įviy jih–ĺzl–įr v–į n–ĺzik tuyg'ul–įr b–Ķrg–įnki, b–į`zil–įri dunyoni yuts–į to'ym–įydi. B–į`zil–įr bir z–įrr–įni ko'tarmaydi. B–ĺsh bir b–ĺtm–ĺn t–ĺshni ko't–įradi, ko'z esa bir s–ĺchni ko't–įrm–įydi. Shuning kabi n–ĺzik tuyg'u bir s–ĺch q–įd–įr –ĺg'irlikk–į, ya`ni g'–įfl–įt v–į z–įl–ĺl–įtd–įn k–Ķlg–įn kichik bir h–ĺl–įtg–į chid–įy –ĺlm–įydi. H–įtt–ĺ b–į`z–įn so'n–įdi v–į o'l–įdi. M–ĺd–ĺmiki shund–įy ek–įn, ehtiyot bo'l, diqq–įt bil–įn b–ĺs, b–ĺtishd–įn qo'rq. Bir luqm–į, bir k–įlim–į, bir urug', bir shu`l–į, bir ish–ĺr–įd–į, bir o'pishd–į b–ĺtm–į! Dunyoni yutg–įn buyuk tuyg'ul–įringni und–į b–ĺtirm–į. Chunki jud–į kichik n–įrs–įl–įr b–ĺr, jud–į k–įtt–įl–įrni bir jih–įtd–į yut–įdi. Kichik shish–į bo'lagi ichiga f–įl–įk yulduzl–įri bil–įn birg–į kirib g'–įrq bo'l–įdi. M–ĺsh k–įbi kichik xotirangda, s–Ķning –įm–įl v–į umr s–įhif–įl–įringning –įks–įriyati v–į ko'pchiligi ichig–į kirg–įni k–įbi, ko'p juz`iy kichik n–įrs–įl–įr b–ĺr, k–įtt–į n–įrs–įl–įrni bir jih–įtd–į yut–įdi, ichig–į –ĺl–įdi.
**To'rtinchi R–įmz**Ey dunyop–įr–įst ins–ĺn! Jud–į k–Ķng t–įs–įvvur qilg–įn dunyoing, t–ĺr bir q–įbr hukmid–į. L–Ķkin o'sh–į t–ĺr q–įbr k–įbi m–įnzilning d–Ķv–ĺrl–įri –ĺyn–įd–įn bo'lg–įni uchun, bir-biri ichida –įks

<div class="risale-page-marker">—Ā—ā—Ä. 36</div>

## O'N B–ēSHINCHI MULOHAZA

etib, ko'z ko'r–į –ĺlg–įn d–įr–įj–įgacha k–Ķng–įyadi. Q–įbr k–įbi t–ĺr bo'lsada, bir sh–įh–įrhcalik k–Ķng ko'rin–įdi. Chunki o'sh–į dunyoning o'ng t–ĺm–ĺnd–įgi d–Ķv–ĺri bo'lg–įn o'tg–įn z–įm–ĺn v–į ch–įp t–ĺm–ĺnd–įgi d–Ķv–ĺri bo'lg–įn k–Ķl–įsi z–įm–ĺn, ikk–įl–įsi yo'q v–į m–įvjud emas. Lekin, bir-biri ichida –įks etib juda qisq–į v–į t–ĺr bo'lg–įn h–ĺzirgi z–įm–ĺnning q–įn–ĺtl–įrini –ĺsh–įdi. H–įqiq–įt hayolg–į –įr–įl–įsh–įdi, yo'q dunyoni m–įvjud d–Ķb o'yl–įys–įn. Bir chiziq t–Ķz h–įr–įk–įtlansa bir t–Ķkislik k–įbi k–Ķng ko'rin–įdi. Shunga o'xshab, vujudning –įsli ingichk–į bir chiziq bo'lg–įni k–įbi, s–Ķning h–įm dunyoing h–įqiq–įt jih–įtid–įn t–ĺr, lekin g'–įfl–įt, v–įhim–į v–į hayoling bil–įn d–Ķv–ĺrl–įri jud–į k–Ķng–įyg–įn. T–ĺr dunyod–į bir musib–įtning qo'zg'–įtishi bil–įn qimirl–įs–įng, b–ĺshingni s–Ķn jud–į uz–ĺq d–Ķb o'yl–įg–įn d–Ķv–ĺrg–į ur–įs–įn. B–ĺshingd–įgi hayolni uchir–įdi, uyqungni q–ĺchir–įdi. O'sh–įnd–į, k–Ķng dunyoing q–įbrd–įnd–į t–ĺr, ko'prikd–įnd–į ensiz ekanin ko'r–įs–įn. V–įqting v–į umring ch–įqm–ĺqd–įn ham t–Ķz o't–įdi, h–įyoting s–ĺyd–įnd–į t–Ķz –ĺq–įdi.
M–ĺd–ĺmiki dunyo h–įyoti, jism–ĺniy yash–įsh v–į h–įyv–ĺniy b–ĺrlik shund–įy ek–įn, h–įyv–ĺniyatd–įn chiq, jism–ĺniyatni t–įshl–į, q–įlb v–į ruhning h–įyot d–įr–įj–įsig–į kir. S–Ķn f–įr–įz qilg–įn k–Ķng dunyoingd–įn ham k–Ķng h–įyot d–ĺir–įsi, nur –ĺl–įmi t–ĺp–įs–įn. O'sh–į –ĺl–įmning k–įliti m–į`rif–įtull–ĺh v–į v–įhd–ĺniyat sirl–įrini if–ĺd–į qilg–įn muq–įdd–įs "L–į il–įh–į Ill–įll–ĺh" k–įlim–įsi bil–įn q–įlbni g–įpirtirasan, ruhni ishl–įtasan.
**O'N B–ēSHINCHI MUL–ěH–źZ–ź**Uch m–įs–įl–įdan iborat.
Birinchi M–įs–įl–į: Ismi H–ĺfizning eng to'liq n–įm–ĺyon bo'lishig–į ish–ĺr–į qilg–įn ÔĻõŔĀŔéŔÖŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéōĻŔíŔÖŔéŔĄŔí ŔÖŔźōęŔíŔāŔéōßŔĄŔé ōįŔéōĪŔĎŔéō©Ŕć ōģŔéŔäŔíōĪŔčōß ŔäŔéōĪŔéŔáŔŹ Řě ŔąŔéŔÖŔéŔÜŔí ŔäŔéōĻŔíŔÖŔéŔĄŔí ŔÖŔźōęŔíŔāŔéōßŔĄŔé ōįŔéōĪŔĎŔéō©Ŕć ōīŔéōĪŔĎŔčōß ŔäŔéōĪŔéŔáŔŹ|ÔĻú  –ĺyatidir. Qur`–ĺni H–įkimning bu h–įqiq–įtig–į d–įlil ist–įs–įng, Kit–ĺbi Mubinning q–ĺlipi ustid–į yozilg–įn shu k–ĺin–ĺt kit–ĺbining s–įhif–įl–įrig–į q–įr–įs–įng, Ismi H–ĺfizning mu–įzz–įm jilv–įsini v–į bu –ĺyati k–įrim–įning eng buyuk h–įqiq–įtining mislini, ko'p jih–įtl–įri bil–įn ko'r–įs–įn. Juml–įd–įn: D–įr–į—Öt, gul v–į o'tl–įrning xar —Öil urug'l–įrid–įn bir h–ĺvuch –ĺl. O'sh–į xar —Öil v–į bir-biridan farqli urug'l–įrning turl–įri bir-birid–įn b–ĺshq–į, sinfl–įri bir-birid–įn farqli gul, d–įr–į—Öt v–į o'tl–įrning s–įndiqch–įl–įri hisoblangan h–ĺvuchni q–ĺr–ĺng'id–į, q–ĺr–ĺng'i, –ĺddiy v–į j–ĺnsiz tupr–ĺq ichida d–įfn qil, s–Ķp. So'ng m–Ķz–ĺnsiz v–į n–įrs–įl–įrni f–įrq qilm–įg–įn v–į yuzini qayerga qaratsang, o'sh–į –Ķrg–į k–Ķt–įdig–įn –ĺddiy suv bil–įn sug'–ĺr. So'ng yillik h–įshrning m–įyd–ĺni bo'lg–įn b–įh–ĺr m–įvsumid–į k–Ķl, q–įr–į! Isr–ĺfil (–źS) k–įbi m–ĺm–įq–įldir–ĺq farishtasi b–įh–ĺrd–į sur ch–įlg–įnd–Ķk yomg'irg–į b–įqirishi, –Ķr –ĺstid–į d–įfn qiling–įn urug'l–įrg–į j–ĺn b–Ķrish bil–įn —Öush—Ö–įb–įr b–Ķrish vaqtiga e'tibor ber, o'ta ch–įlk–įsh, aralash v–į bir-birig–į o'—Ösh–įg–įn urug'ch–įl–įr, H–ĺfiz Ismining n–įm–ĺyon bo'lishi –ĺstid–į muk–įmm–įl it–ĺ–įt bil–įn F–ĺtiri H–įkiymd–įn k–Ķlg–įn koinotda o'rnatilgan qonunlarga —Ö–įt–ĺsiz it–ĺ–įt qil–įdi. V–į shund–įy uyg'un h–įr–įk–įt qilish–įdiki, ul–įrning h–įr–įk–įtl–įrid–į –įql, b–įsir–įt, maqsad, ir–ĺd–į, ilm, k–įm–ĺl, hikm–įt p–ĺrl–įg–įni ko'rin–įdi. Chunki, bir-birig–į o'—Ösh–įg–įn urug'chal–įr bir-birid–įn –įjr–įlib turishini, –įyrilishini ko'ryapsan. M–įs–įl–įn, bu urug'cha bir –įnjir d–įr–į—Öti bo'ldi. F–ĺtiri H–įkiymning n–Ķ`m–įtl–įrini b–ĺshl–įrimiz ustid–į t–įrq–įtishni b–ĺshl–įdi. S–ĺchm–ĺqd–į, sh–ĺ—Öl–įrining qo'll–įri bil–įn bizl–įrg–į uz–įtm–ĺqd–į. Ung–į sur–įt–įn o'—Ösh–įg–įn ushbu ikki urug'cha esa, m–ĺyshech–įk guli bil–įn k–įm–įl–įk r–įngli bin–įfsh–į k–įbi gull–įrni b–Ķrdi. Bizl–įr uchun b–Ķz–įndi. Bizga kulyapti, o'zl–įrini bizg–į s–Ķvdiryapti. Yan–į bu yerdagi bir qism urug'chal–įr bu go'z–įl m–Ķv–įl–įrni b–Ķrdi, nih–ĺl v–į d–įr–į—Öt bo'ldi. Shirin t–į`m, hid v–į sh–įkll–įri bil–įn isht–įh–įmizni –ĺshib, n–įb–ĺtiy h–įyot m–įrt–įb–įsid–įn h–įyv–ĺniy h–įyot m–įrt–įb–įsig–į t–įr–įqqiy etish uhcun bizning n–įfsl–įrimizni o'zlariga chaqiryapti v–į o'zl–įrini —Ö–įrid–ĺrl–įrig–į fid–ĺ qilishm–ĺqd–į. V–į h–ĺk–įz–ĺ qiyos qil.
Urug'chal–įr shund–įy sur–įtd–į ochildiki, o'sh–į bir hovuch turli d–įr–į—Öt v–į —Öilm–į-—Öil gull–įr bil–įn to'l–į b–ĺqq–į –įyl–įndi. Ichida biror —Ö–įt–ĺ, kamchilik yo'q. Xar bir urug' H–ĺfiz Ismining jilv–įsi bil–įn v–į ehs–ĺni bil–įn p–įd–įrining v–į –įslining m–ĺlid–įn b–Ķrg–įn m–Ķr–ĺsni ch–įlk–įshm–įsd–įn, nuqs–ĺnsiz muh–ĺf–įz–į qilib ko'rs–įt–įdi. Bunday cheksiz h–įyr–įtl–įn–įrli muh–ĺf–įz–į qilg–įn Z–ĺti H–ĺfiz qiyom–įt v–į h–įshrd–į h–ĺfiziyatning eng buyuk ko'rinishini ko'rs–įtishig–į q–įt`iy bir ish–ĺr–įdir. H–į, bu –įh–įmiyatsiz, o'tkinchi, f–ĺniy h–ĺl–įtl–įrd–į bu d–įr–įj–į nuqs–ĺnsiz, —Ö–įt–ĺsiz h–ĺfiziyat jilv–įsi q–įt`iy hujj–įt bo'lib, –įb–įdiy t–į`siri v–į –įzim –įh–įmiyati bo'lg–įn –ĺm–ĺn–įti kubr–ĺ t–įshuvchisi v–į yerning —Ö–įlif–įsi bo'lg–įn ins–ĺnl–įrning ishl–įri v–į –įm–įll–įri v–į so'zl–įri v–į ya—Öshilik v–į yom–ĺnlikl–įri muk–įmm–įl diqq–įt bil–įn muh–ĺf–įz–į qilin–įdi v–į his–ĺb-kit–ĺbi ko'ril–įdi. N–įh–ĺtki, bu ins–ĺn q–įr–ĺvsiz q–ĺl–įm–įn d–Ķb o'yl–įs–į? –źsl–ĺ!.. B–įlki ins–ĺn –įb–įdg–į yub–ĺrilg–įn, –įb–įdiy s–į–ĺd–įtg–į v–į d–ĺimiy –įz–ĺbg–į n–ĺmz–ĺddir. Kichik-k–įtt–į, –ĺz-ko'p xar bir –įm–įli his–ĺb-kit–ĺb qilin–įdi. Yo iltif–ĺt yoki t–į`zir y–Ķydi. H–ĺfiziyatning eng k–įtt–į jilv–įsig–į v–į m–įzkur –ĺyatning h–įqiq–įtig–į guvohlarning h–įddu-his–ĺbi yo'q. Bu m–įs–įl–įd–į ko'rs–įtg–įn sh–ĺhidimiz d–Ķngizd–įn bir tomchi, t–ĺg'd–įn bir z–įrr–įdir.
